"use client";

/**
 * PlannerClient — UWorld-style main study planner page.
 *
 * Three tabs:
 * 1. امروز (Today) — sectioned task list: overdue / today / upcoming / completed
 * 2. هفته (Week)   — Saturday–Friday weekly calendar view
 * 3. برنامه‌ها (Plans) — plan list and management
 *
 * Hosts the overdue modal, reschedule dialog, and planner progress summary.
 */

import { useState, useCallback, useEffect, Component, type ReactNode } from "react";
import { motion } from "framer-motion";
import {
  CalendarCheck,
  CalendarDays,
  LayoutList,
  TrendingUp,
  Flame,
  Target,
  BookOpen,
  Clock,
  AlertTriangle,
  RefreshCw,
  Brain,
} from "lucide-react";
import { PageHeader } from "@/components/ui/page-header";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { TodayTaskList } from "@/components/planner/TodayTaskList";
import { WeeklyView } from "@/components/planner/WeeklyView";
import { OverdueModal } from "@/components/planner/OverdueModal";
import { RescheduleDialog } from "@/components/planner/RescheduleDialog";
import { PlanList } from "./PlanList";
import { RecommendationPanel } from "@/components/planner/RecommendationPanel";
import { n, useVisibilityRefresh } from "@/components/planner/task-helpers";
import { getPlannerSummaryAction } from "@/lib/actions/planner-actions";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Tab types                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

type Tab = "today" | "week" | "recommendations" | "plans";

const TABS: { id: Tab; label: string; icon: React.ElementType }[] = [
  { id: "today", label: "امروز", icon: CalendarCheck },
  { id: "week", label: "هفته", icon: CalendarDays },
  { id: "recommendations", label: "پیشنهادها", icon: Brain },
  { id: "plans", label: "برنامه‌ها", icon: LayoutList },
];

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Error Boundary                                                     */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

class PlannerErrorBoundary extends Component<
  { children: ReactNode },
  { hasError: boolean }
> {
  state = { hasError: false };

  static getDerivedStateFromError() {
    return { hasError: true };
  }

  componentDidCatch(error: Error) {
    console.error("[Planner]", error);
  }

  render() {
    if (this.state.hasError) {
      return (
        <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto py-12">
          <Surface variant="subtle" padding="lg">
            <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-4 py-8">
              <AlertTriangle size={32} style={{ color: colorLight.danger }} />
              <div className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                خطایی در نمایش برنامه مطالعه رخ داد
              </div>
              <button
                onClick={() => {
                  this.setState({ hasError: false });
                  window.location.reload();
                }}
                className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-semibold px-4 py-2 rounded-lg transition-colors"
                style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft, color: colorLight.accent }}
              >
                <RefreshCw size={13} />
                بارگذاری مجدد
              </button>
            </div>
          </Surface>
        </div>
      );
    }
    return this.props.children;
  }
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Planner Progress Banner                                            */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

interface PlannerSummary {
  plan: { title: string; progressPercent: number; completedTasks: number; totalTasks: number } | null;
  today: { totalTasks: number; completedTasks: number; progressPercent: number; estimatedMinutes: number } | null;
  streak: { current: number; longest: number };
  overdueTasks: number;
  upcomingTaskCount: number;
}

function PlannerProgressBanner({ summary }: { summary: PlannerSummary | null }) {
  if (!summary?.plan) return null;

  const planPct = summary.plan.progressPercent;
  const todayPct = summary.today?.progressPercent ?? 0;
  const todayDone = summary.today?.completedTasks ?? 0;
  const todayTotal = summary.today?.totalTasks ?? 0;

  return (
    <Surface variant="default" padding="sm" className="mb-4">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
        {/* Plan progress */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-1">
          <TrendingUp size={13} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
          <span className="font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
            {summary.plan.title}
          </span>
          <div className="flex-1 h-1.5 rounded-full overflow-hidden" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}>
            <div
              className="h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
              style={{
                width: `${planPct}%`,
                backgroundColor: planPct >= 100 ? colorLight.success : colorLight.accent,
              }}
            />
          </div>
          <span className="font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}>
            {n(planPct)}%
          </span>
        </div>

        {/* Divider */}
        <div className="w-px h-4" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />

        {/* Today stats */}
        <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
          <CalendarCheck size={12} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
          {n(todayDone)}/{n(todayTotal)}
        </span>

        {/* Streak */}
        {summary.streak.current > 0 && (
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
            <Flame size={12} style={{ color: colorLight.warning }} />
            {n(summary.streak.current)}
          </span>
        )}

        {/* Overdue */}
        {summary.overdueTasks > 0 && (
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1 font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}>
            <AlertTriangle size={12} />
            {n(summary.overdueTasks)}
          </span>
        )}
      </div>
    </Surface>
  );
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Main PlannerClient Component                                       */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export default function PlannerClient() {
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<Tab>("today");
  const [overdueOpen, setOverdueOpen] = useState(false);
  const [rescheduleTaskId, setRescheduleTaskId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [refreshKey, setRefreshKey] = useState(0);
  const [summary, setSummary] = useState<PlannerSummary | null>(null);

  const fetchSummary = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const res = await getPlannerSummaryAction();
      if (res.ok) setSummary(res.data);
    } catch {
      // silent
    }
  }, []);

  const triggerRefresh = useCallback(() => {
    setRefreshKey((k) => k + 1);
    fetchSummary();
  }, [fetchSummary]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchSummary();
  }, [fetchSummary]);

  useVisibilityRefresh(fetchSummary, true);

  function handleShowOverdue() {
    setOverdueOpen(true);
  }

  function handleReschedule(taskId: string) {
    setRescheduleTaskId(taskId);
  }

  return (
    <PlannerErrorBoundary>
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto pb-12">
      <PageHeader
        title="برنامه مطالعه"
        description="برنامه‌ریزی و پیگیری مطالعات روزانه"
        icon={<CalendarCheck size={22} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />}
        breadcrumb={[
          { label: "داشبورد", href: "/" },
          { label: "برنامه مطالعه" },
        ]}
      />

      {/* ---- Progress Banner ---- */}
      <PlannerProgressBanner summary={summary} />

      {/* ---- Tab Bar ---- */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mb-6">
        {TABS.map((tab) => {
          const isActive = activeTab === tab.id;
          const TabIcon = tab.icon;
          return (
            <button
              key={tab.id}
              onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab.id)}
              className={`
                relative flex items-center gap-1.5 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium
                rounded-xl transition-all
              `}
              style={{
                backgroundColor: isActive ? colorLight.accent : "transparent",
                color: isActive ? "#fff" : colorLight.textMuted,
              }}
            >
              <TabIcon size={15} />
              {tab.label}
              {isActive && (
                <motion.div
                  layoutId="planner-tab-indicator"
                  className="absolute inset-0 rounded-xl -z-[1]"
                  style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accent }}
                  transition={{ type: "spring", duration: 0.4, bounce: 0.15 }}
                />
              )}
            </button>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {/* ---- Tab Content ---- */}
      <motion.div
        key={`${activeTab}-${refreshKey}`}
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.25 }}
      >
        {activeTab === "today" && (
          <TodayTaskList
            onShowOverdue={handleShowOverdue}
            onReschedule={handleReschedule}
          />
        )}
        {activeTab === "week" && (
          <WeeklyView
            onReschedule={handleReschedule}
            onShowOverdue={handleShowOverdue}
          />
        )}
        {activeTab === "recommendations" && (
          <RecommendationPanel onTaskCreated={triggerRefresh} />
        )}
        {activeTab === "plans" && <PlanList />}
      </motion.div>

      {/* ---- Overdue Modal ---- */}
      <OverdueModal
        open={overdueOpen}
        onClose={() => setOverdueOpen(false)}
        onResolved={triggerRefresh}
      />

      {/* ---- Reschedule Dialog ---- */}
      <RescheduleDialog
        open={rescheduleTaskId !== null}
        taskId={rescheduleTaskId}
        onClose={() => setRescheduleTaskId(null)}
        onDone={triggerRefresh}
      />
    </div>
    </PlannerErrorBoundary>
  );
}

};

/**

 * bucket-based PlannerPage composition.
 */

"use client";

/**
 * PlanList — manage study plans (list, activate, pause, archive, delete).
 *
 * Also provides a "Create New Plan" CTA that (for now) shows a simple
 * form to generate a weekly plan.
 */

import { useEffect, useState, useTransition, useCallback } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import {
  Plus,
  Play,
  Pause,
  CheckCircle2,
  Archive,
  Trash2,
  Loader2,
  LayoutList,
  RefreshCw,
  AlertTriangle,
} from "lucide-react";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { n, formatPersianDate, useVisibilityRefresh } from "@/components/planner/task-helpers";
import {
  listPlansAction,
  activatePlanAction,
  pausePlanAction,
  completePlanAction,
  archivePlanAction,
  removePlanAction,
} from "@/lib/actions/planner-actions";

interface Plan {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  status: string;
  startDate: string;
  endDate: string | null;
  totalTasks: number;
  completedTasks: number;
  progressPercent: number;
}

const STATUS_LABEL: Record<string, string> = {
  draft: "پیش‌نویس",
  active: "فعال",
  paused: "متوقف",
  completed: "تکمیل شده",
  archived: "آرشیو",
};

const STATUS_COLOR: Record<string, { text: string; bg: string }> = {
  draft: { text: "#6B7280", bg: "#F3F4F6" },
  active: { text: "#0EA5A4", bg: "#CCFBF1" },
  paused: { text: "#D97706", bg: "#FEF3C7" },
  completed: { text: "#16A34A", bg: "#DCFCE7" },
  archived: { text: "#9CA3AF", bg: "#F3F4F6" },
};

export function PlanList() {
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState<Plan[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [isPending, startTransition] = useTransition();

  const fetchPlans = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const res = await listPlansAction();
      if (res.ok) {
        setPlans(res.data);
        setError(null);
      } else {
        setError(res.error?.message ?? "خطا در دریافت برنامه‌ها");
      }
    } catch {
      setError("خطا در دریافت برنامه‌ها");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchPlans();
  }, [fetchPlans]);

  // Auto-refresh on tab focus
  useVisibilityRefresh(fetchPlans, !loading);

  function handleAction(
    action: (id: string) => Promise<{ ok: boolean; error?: { code?: string; message: string } }>,
    planId: string,
    successMsg: string,
  ) {
    startTransition(async () => {
      const res = await action(planId);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success(successMsg);
        fetchPlans();
      } else {
        const errMsg = res.error?.message ?? "خطا در انجام عملیات";
        if (res.error?.code === "NOT_FOUND") {
          toast.error("این برنامه دیگر وجود ندارد");
          fetchPlans();
        } else {
          toast.error(errMsg);
        }
      }
    });
  }

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-3 animate-pulse">
        {[1, 2].map((i) => (
          <Surface key={i} variant="default" padding="md">
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
              <div className="flex-1 space-y-2">
                <div className="h-4 w-2/3 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
                <div className="h-3 w-1/3 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
                <div className="h-1.5 rounded-full" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
              </div>
            </div>
          </Surface>
        ))}
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (error) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3 py-6">
          <AlertTriangle size={28} style={{ color: colorLight.danger }} />
          <div className="text-sm text-center" style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}>
            {error}
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={() => { setLoading(true); setError(null); fetchPlans(); }}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs font-semibold px-4 py-2
              rounded-lg transition-colors"
            style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft, color: colorLight.accent }}
          >
            <RefreshCw size={13} />
            تلاش مجدد
          </button>
        </div>
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {/* ---- Empty State ---- */}
      {plans.length === 0 && (
        <Surface variant="subtle" padding="lg">
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center text-center gap-3 py-6">
            <LayoutList size={32} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
            <div>
              <div className="text-sm font-semibold mb-1" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                هنوز برنامه‌ای ایجاد نشده
              </div>
              <div className="text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                یک برنامه مطالعه جدید بسازید تا تسک‌ها و روزهای مطالعه به صورت خودکار ایجاد شوند.
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Surface>
      )}

      {/* ---- Plan Cards ---- */}
      <AnimatePresence mode="popLayout">
        {plans.map((plan) => {
          const sc = STATUS_COLOR[plan.status] ?? STATUS_COLOR.draft;

          return (
            <motion.div
              key={plan.id}
              layout
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -8 }}
            >
              <Surface variant="default" padding="md">
                <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                  {/* Left — Info */}
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                      <span className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                        {plan.title}
                      </span>
                      <span
                        className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-medium"
                        style={{ backgroundColor: sc.bg, color: sc.text }}
                      >
                        {STATUS_LABEL[plan.status] ?? plan.status}
                      </span>
                    </div>

                    <div className="text-[11px] mb-2" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                      {formatPersianDate(plan.startDate)}
                      {plan.endDate && ` — ${formatPersianDate(plan.endDate)}`}
                    </div>

                    {/* Progress */}
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px]" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                      <span>{n(plan.completedTasks)} از {n(plan.totalTasks)} تسک</span>
                      <span style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}>{n(plan.progressPercent)}%</span>
                    </div>

                    <div className="h-1.5 rounded-full overflow-hidden mt-1.5" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}>
                      <div
                        className="h-full rounded-full transition-all"
                        style={{
                          width: `${plan.progressPercent}%`,
                          backgroundColor: colorLight.accent,
                        }}
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Right — Actions */}
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1 ms-3">
                    {(plan.status === "draft" || plan.status === "paused") && (
                      <button
                        onClick={() =>
                          handleAction(activatePlanAction, plan.id, "برنامه فعال شد")
                        }
                        disabled={isPending}
                        className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-teal-50 transition-colors"
                        title="فعال‌سازی"
                      >
                        <Play size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
                      </button>
                    )}
                    {plan.status === "active" && (
                      <>
                        <button
                          onClick={() =>
                            handleAction(pausePlanAction, plan.id, "برنامه متوقف شد")
                          }
                          disabled={isPending}
                          className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-yellow-50 transition-colors"
                          title="توقف"
                        >
                          <Pause size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.warning }} />
                        </button>
                        <button
                          onClick={() =>
                            handleAction(completePlanAction, plan.id, "برنامه تکمیل شد")
                          }
                          disabled={isPending}
                          className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-green-50 transition-colors"
                          title="تکمیل"
                        >
                          <CheckCircle2 size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.success }} />
                        </button>
                      </>
                    )}
                    {(plan.status === "completed" || plan.status === "paused") && (
                      <button
                        onClick={() =>
                          handleAction(archivePlanAction, plan.id, "برنامه آرشیو شد")
                        }
                        disabled={isPending}
                        className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors"
                        title="آرشیو"
                      >
                        <Archive size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
                      </button>
                    )}
                    {(plan.status === "draft" || plan.status === "archived") && (
                      <button
                        onClick={() =>
                          handleAction(removePlanAction, plan.id, "برنامه حذف شد")
                        }
                        disabled={isPending}
                        className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-red-50 transition-colors"
                        title="حذف"
                      >
                        <Trash2 size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.danger }} />
                      </button>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </Surface>
            </motion.div>
          );
        })}
      </AnimatePresence>

      {/* Info note */}
      {plans.length > 0 && (
        <Surface variant="subtle" padding="sm">
          <div className="text-center text-[11px]" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
            فقط یک برنامه می‌تواند همزمان فعال باشد. برنامه‌های قدیمی را آرشیو یا حذف کنید.
          </div>
        </Surface>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\planner\PlannerPage.tsx

"use client";

/**
 * PlannerPage — Bucket-based planner composition.
 *
 * Renders PlannerSummary + Calendar + five PlannerBucket sections,
 * each containing PlannerTaskCards.
 */

import { useState, useCallback, useTransition, useEffect } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { PlannerSummary, type PlannerSummaryProps } from "./PlannerSummary";
import {
  PlannerRecommendationCard,
  type PlannerRecommendationCardProps,
} from "./PlannerRecommendationCard";
import { PlannerBucket } from "./PlannerBucket";
import { PlannerTaskCard } from "./PlannerTaskCard";
import { RescheduleDialog } from "./RescheduleDialog";
import {
  SECTION_LABEL,
  SECTION_ORDER,
  type PlannerSection,
} from "./task-helpers";
import {
  completeTaskAction,
  moveToTodayAction,
  rescheduleTaskAction,
} from "@/lib/actions/planner-actions";
import type { TaskBucket } from "@/lib/planner/types";

// ----- اضافه شده: ایمپورت‌های تقویم و مودال -----
import { PlannerCalendar } from "./calendar/PlannerCalendar";
import { CalendarDayModal } from "./calendar/CalendarDayModal";
import { PlannerDndContext } from "./dnd/PlannerDndContext";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/* Virtual task ID detection                                         */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function isVirtualTask(taskId: string): boolean {
  return taskId.startsWith("fsrs-virtual-") || taskId.startsWith("weak-virtual-");
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/* Task shape (minimal, matching PlannerTaskCard)                     */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface BucketTask {
  id: string;
  taskType: string;
  status: string;
  title: string;
  description?: string | null;
  estimatedMinutes: number;
  priority: number;
  sourceType?: string | null;
  scheduledFor?: string | null;
  linkUrl?: string | null;
  linkLabel?: string | null;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/* Props                                                             */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface PlannerPageProps {
  summary: PlannerSummaryProps;
  buckets: Record<TaskBucket, BucketTask[]>;
  recommendation: PlannerRecommendationCardProps["recommendation"];
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/* Helpers                                                           */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/** Remove a task from every bucket (optimistic removal). */
function removeBucketTask(
  prev: Record<TaskBucket, BucketTask[]>,
  taskId: string,
): Record<TaskBucket, BucketTask[]> {
  const next = { ...prev };
  for (const key of Object.keys(next) as TaskBucket[]) {
    next[key] = next[key].filter((t) => t.id !== taskId);
  }
  return next;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/* Component                                                         */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function PlannerPage({
  summary,
  buckets: initialBuckets,
  recommendation,
}: PlannerPageProps) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [isPending, startTransition] = useTransition();
  const [buckets, setBuckets] = useState(initialBuckets);

  // Sync local optimistic state when server data refreshes
  useEffect(() => {
    setBuckets(initialBuckets);
  }, [initialBuckets]);

  const [rescheduleTaskId, setRescheduleTaskId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // ----- اضافه شده: مدیریت State تقویم و مودال -----
  const [selectedDate, setSelectedDate] = useState<Date | null>(null);
  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false);

  const handleDayClick = useCallback((date: Date) => {
    setSelectedDate(date);
    setIsModalOpen(true);
  }, []);

  // تمام تسک‌ها رو فلت می‌کنیم تا به تقویم بدیم
  const allTasks = Object.values(buckets).flat();

  // فیلتر کردن تسک‌های همون روزی که کاربر روش کلیک کرده (برای نمایش در مودال)
  const selectedDateTasks = selectedDate
    ? allTasks.filter((t) => {
        if (!t.scheduledFor) return false;
        // گرفتن بخش YYYY-MM-DD
        const taskDate = new Date(t.scheduledFor).toISOString().split("T")[0];
        const clickedDate = selectedDate.toISOString().split("T")[0];
        return taskDate === clickedDate;
      })
    : [];

  /* ---- Complete ---- */
  const handleComplete = useCallback(
    (taskId: string) => {
      if (isVirtualTask(taskId)) {
        setBuckets((prev) => removeBucketTask(prev, taskId));
        toast.success("تسک مجازی از لیست حذف شد");
        return;
      }

      // Optimistic: move task to completed bucket
      setBuckets((prev) => {
        const task = Object.values(prev)
          .flat()
          .find((t) => t.id === taskId);
        const next = removeBucketTask(prev, taskId);
        if (task) {
          next.completed = [
            { ...task, status: "completed" },
            ...next.completed,
          ];
        }
        return next;
      });

      startTransition(async () => {
        const res = await completeTaskAction(taskId);
        if (res.ok) {
          toast.success("تسک تکمیل شد");
        } else {
          toast.error(res.error.message);
        }
        router.refresh();
      });
    },
    [router],
  );

  /* ---- Move to today ---- */
  const handleMoveToToday = useCallback(
    (taskId: string) => {
      if (isVirtualTask(taskId)) {
        toast.info("تسک مجازی قابل انتقال نیست");
        return;
      }

      setBuckets((prev) => {
        const next = removeBucketTask(prev, taskId);
        const task = Object.values(prev)
          .flat()
          .find((t) => t.id === taskId);
        if (task) {
          next.today = [...next.today, { ...task, status: "pending" }];
        }
        return next;
      });

      startTransition(async () => {
        const res = await moveToTodayAction(taskId);
        if (res.ok) {
          toast.success("به امروز منتقل شد");
        } else {
          toast.error(res.error.message);
        }
        router.refresh();
      });
    },
    [router],
  );

  /* ---- DnD Reschedule ---- */
  const handleDndReschedule = useCallback(
    (taskId: string, targetDate: string) => {
      if (isVirtualTask(taskId)) {
        toast.info("تسک مجازی قابل زمان‌بندی مجدد نیست");
        return;
      }

      // Optimistic: remove task from current bucket
      setBuckets((prev) => removeBucketTask(prev, taskId));

      startTransition(async () => {
        const res = await rescheduleTaskAction(taskId, targetDate);
        if (res.ok) {
          toast.success("تسک به تاریخ جدید منتقل شد");
        } else {
          toast.error(res.error.message);
        }
        router.refresh();
      });
    },
    [router],
  );

  /* ---- Reschedule ---- */
  const handleRescheduleDone = useCallback(() => {
    setRescheduleTaskId(null);
    router.refresh();
  }, [router]);

  return (
    <PlannerDndContext onTaskReschedule={handleDndReschedule}>
    <div
      className="flex flex-col gap-6" // فاصله رو کمی بیشتر کردم تا تقویم جا باز کنه
      style={{ opacity: isPending ? 0.7 : 1, transition: "opacity 200ms" }}
    >
      {/* Recommendation card */}
      <PlannerRecommendationCard recommendation={recommendation} />

      {/* Summary strip */}
      <PlannerSummary {...summary} />

      {/* ----- اضافه شده: کامپوننت تقویم ----- */}
      <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
        <h2 className="text-xl font-bold px-1">تقویم مطالعه</h2>
        <PlannerCalendar
          tasks={allTasks}
          dailyStats={{}}
          onDayClick={handleDayClick}
        />
      </div>

      {/* Buckets */}
      <div className="flex flex-col gap-0 mt-4">
        {SECTION_ORDER.map((section) => {
          const bucket = section as TaskBucket;
          const tasks = buckets[bucket] ?? [];

          // اگر سطلی خالی بود، می‌تونی اینجا تصمیم بگیری که کلا رندر نشه یا خالی بمونه
          return (
            <PlannerBucket
              key={section}
              section={section}
              title={SECTION_LABEL[section]}
              count={tasks.length}
            >
              <AnimatePresence initial={false}>
              {tasks.map((task) => (
                <PlannerTaskCard
                  key={task.id}
                  task={task}
                  bucket={bucket}
                  onComplete={handleComplete}
                  onReschedule={setRescheduleTaskId}
                  onMoveToToday={handleMoveToToday}
                />
              ))}
              </AnimatePresence>
            </PlannerBucket>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {/* Reschedule dialog */}
      <RescheduleDialog
        open={rescheduleTaskId !== null}
        taskId={rescheduleTaskId}
        onClose={() => setRescheduleTaskId(null)}
        onDone={handleRescheduleDone}
      />

      {/* ----- اضافه شده: مودال جزئیات روزانه ----- */}
      {selectedDate && (
        <CalendarDayModal
          open={isModalOpen}
          onOpenChange={setIsModalOpen}
          date={selectedDate}
          tasks={selectedDateTasks}
        />
      )}
    </div>
    </PlannerDndContext>
  );
}

"use client";

/**
 * PlannerSummary — Compact stats strip at the top of the planner page.
 *
 * Shows: today's planned/completed minutes, due flashcards, active weak areas,
 * and exam countdown (if exam date exists).
 */

import {
  CreditCard,
  AlertTriangle,
  CalendarDays,
} from "lucide-react";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { n, formatMinutes } from "./task-helpers";
import { ProgressRing } from "./ui/ProgressRing";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Props                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface PlannerSummaryProps {
  todayPlannedMinutes: number;
  todayCompletedMinutes: number;
  dueFlashcardsCount: number;
  activeWeakAreasCount: number;
  examDate: string | null; // ISO date YYYY-MM-DD
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Helpers                                                            */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function daysUntil(isoDate: string): number {
  const now = new Date();
  now.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  const target = new Date(isoDate + "T00:00:00");
  return Math.max(0, Math.ceil((target.getTime() - now.getTime()) / 86_400_000));
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Stat Cell                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function StatCell({
  icon: Icon,
  label,
  value,
  accent,
}: {
  icon: React.ElementType;
  label: string;
  value: string;
  accent?: string;
}) {
  const color = accent ?? colorLight.textMuted;
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
      <Icon size={14} style={{ color, flexShrink: 0 }} />
      <div className="min-w-0">
        <div
          className="text-[11px] leading-tight truncate"
          style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
        >
          {label}
        </div>
        <div
          className="text-sm font-bold tabular-nums leading-tight"
          style={{ color }}
        >
          {value}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Component                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function PlannerSummary({
  todayPlannedMinutes,
  todayCompletedMinutes,
  dueFlashcardsCount,
  activeWeakAreasCount,
  examDate,
}: PlannerSummaryProps) {
  const minutesPct =
    todayPlannedMinutes > 0
      ? Math.round((todayCompletedMinutes / todayPlannedMinutes) * 100)
      : 0;

  return (
    <Surface variant="default" padding="sm" className="mb-4">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-6 flex-wrap">
        {/* Time progress */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-1 min-w-[180px]">
          <ProgressRing
            value={minutesPct}
            size={40}
            label={`${n(Math.min(minutesPct, 100))}٪`}
          />
          <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-[11px] mb-0.5">
              <span style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>زمان امروز</span>
              <span
                className="font-bold tabular-nums"
                style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}
              >
                {formatMinutes(todayCompletedMinutes)} / {formatMinutes(todayPlannedMinutes)}
              </span>
            </div>
            <div
              className="h-1.5 rounded-full overflow-hidden"
              style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}
            >
              <div
                className="h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
                style={{
                  width: `${Math.min(100, minutesPct)}%`,
                  backgroundColor:
                    minutesPct >= 100 ? colorLight.success : colorLight.accent,
                }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Divider */}
        <div
          className="w-px h-8 hidden sm:block"
          style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}
        />

        {/* Due flashcards */}
        <StatCell
          icon={CreditCard}
          label="فلش‌کارت‌های سررسید"
          value={n(dueFlashcardsCount)}
          accent={dueFlashcardsCount > 0 ? colorLight.warning : undefined}
        />

        {/* Weak areas */}
        <StatCell
          icon={AlertTriangle}
          label="نقاط ضعف فعال"
          value={n(activeWeakAreasCount)}
          accent={activeWeakAreasCount > 0 ? colorLight.danger : undefined}
        />

        {/* Exam countdown */}
        {examDate && (
          <StatCell
            icon={CalendarDays}
            label="تا آزمون"
            value={`${n(daysUntil(examDate))} روز`}
            accent={
              daysUntil(examDate) <= 7 ? colorLight.danger : colorLight.accent
            }
          />
        )}
      </div>
    </Surface>
  );
}

"use client";

/**
 * TodayTaskList — UWorld-style sectioned task view for the Today tab.
 *
 * Sections:
 * 1. Progress Summary header (overall stats)
 * 2. Overdue tasks (red alert, with move-to-today / snooze actions)
 * 3. Today's tasks (active work area)
 * 4. Upcoming (this week) — preview of what's next
 * 5. Completed (collapsible) — done / skipped tasks
 *
 * Fetches all data via getTodayPlanAction and getUpcomingTasksAction.
 */

import { useEffect, useState, useCallback } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import {
  CalendarCheck,
  Loader2,
  AlertTriangle,
  PartyPopper,
  Clock,
  RefreshCw,
  ChevronDown,
  ChevronUp,
  Target,
  BookOpen,
  CreditCard,
  GraduationCap,
  TrendingUp,
  Flame,
  CheckCircle2,
} from "lucide-react";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { TaskCard } from "./TaskCard";
import {
  n,
  formatMinutes,
  formatPersianDate,
  useVisibilityRefresh,
  SECTION_LABEL,
} from "./task-helpers";
import { getTodayPlanAction, getUpcomingTasksAction } from "@/lib/actions/planner-actions";
import type { TodayPlanResult } from "@/lib/db/queries/planner";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

interface UpcomingTask {
  id: string;
  taskType: string;
  status: string;
  title: string;
  description?: string | null;
  estimatedMinutes: number;
  actualMinutes: number;
  progressPercent: number;
  targetCount?: number | null;
  completedCount: number;
  priority: number;
  scheduledDate?: string | null;
  linkedChapter?: { id: string; title: string; chapterNo: number } | null;
  linkedChunk?: { id: string; title: string | null; chunkIndex: number } | null;
  linkedExamSession?: { id: string; title: string | null; status: string } | null;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Section Header                                                     */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function SectionHeader({
  label,
  count,
  color,
  icon: IconEl,
  collapsible,
  collapsed,
  onToggle,
}: {
  label: string;
  count: number;
  color: string;
  icon: React.ElementType;
  collapsible?: boolean;
  collapsed?: boolean;
  onToggle?: () => void;
}) {
  const content = (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between py-2">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        <div
          className="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center"
          style={{ backgroundColor: `${color}18` }}
        >
          <IconEl size={13} style={{ color }} />
        </div>
        <span className="text-xs font-bold tracking-wide" style={{ color }}>
          {label}
        </span>
        <span
          className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full font-semibold tabular-nums"
          style={{ backgroundColor: `${color}18`, color }}
        >
          {n(count)}
        </span>
      </div>
      {collapsible && (
        collapsed
          ? <ChevronDown size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
          : <ChevronUp size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
      )}
    </div>
  );

  if (collapsible && onToggle) {
    return (
      <button onClick={onToggle} className="w-full text-right hover:bg-gray-50/50 rounded-lg px-1 transition-colors">
        {content}
      </button>
    );
  }

  return <div className="px-1">{content}</div>;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Progress Summary                                                   */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function ProgressSummary({
  todayDate,
  dayLabel,
  totalTasks,
  completedTasks,
  skippedTasks,
  estimatedMinutes,
  remainingMinutes,
  overdueTasks,
  progressPct,
  tasksByType,
}: {
  todayDate: string;
  dayLabel?: string;
  totalTasks: number;
  completedTasks: number;
  skippedTasks: number;
  estimatedMinutes: number;
  remainingMinutes: number;
  overdueTasks: number;
  progressPct: number;
  tasksByType: Record<string, number>;
}) {
  return (
    <Surface variant="default" padding="md">
      {/* Top row: date + percentage */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
        <div>
          <div className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
            {formatPersianDate(todayDate)}
          </div>
          {dayLabel && (
            <div className="text-xs mt-0.5" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
              {dayLabel}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        <div className="text-left">
          <div
            className="text-2xl font-bold tabular-nums"
            style={{ color: progressPct >= 100 ? colorLight.success : colorLight.accent }}
          >
            {n(progressPct)}%
          </div>
          <div className="text-[11px]" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
            {n(completedTasks)} از {n(totalTasks)} تسک
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Progress bar */}
      <div className="h-2.5 rounded-full overflow-hidden" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}>
        <motion.div
          initial={{ width: 0 }}
          animate={{ width: `${progressPct}%` }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.6, delay: 0.2 }}
          className="h-full rounded-full"
          style={{ backgroundColor: progressPct >= 100 ? colorLight.success : colorLight.accent }}
        />
      </div>

      {/* Stats row */}
      <div className="flex items-center flex-wrap gap-x-4 gap-y-1 mt-3 text-[11px]" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
        {remainingMinutes > 0 && (
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
            <Clock size={11} />
            {formatMinutes(remainingMinutes)} باقی‌مانده
          </span>
        )}
        {overdueTasks > 0 && (
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1" style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}>
            <AlertTriangle size={11} />
            {n(overdueTasks)} عقب‌افتاده
          </span>
        )}
        {skippedTasks > 0 && (
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
            {n(skippedTasks)} رد شده
          </span>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Task type breakdown chips */}
      {Object.keys(tasksByType).length > 1 && (
        <div className="flex items-center flex-wrap gap-1.5 mt-3">
          {Object.entries(tasksByType).map(([type, count]) => {
            const ICONS: Record<string, React.ElementType> = {
              question_block: Target,
              flashcard_review: CreditCard,
              chapter_read: BookOpen,
              exam_block: GraduationCap,
            };
            const TypeIcon = ICONS[type];
            const LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
              question_block: "تست",
              flashcard_review: "فلش‌کارت",
              chapter_read: "مطالعه",
              chunk_review: "مرور",
              exam_block: "آزمون",
              notebook_review: "نوت‌بوک",
              custom_task: "دلخواه",
            };
            return (
              <span
                key={type}
                className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full"
                style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border, color: colorLight.textSoft }}
              >
                {TypeIcon && <TypeIcon size={10} />}
                {LABELS[type] ?? type}: {n(count)}
              </span>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      )}
    </Surface>
  );
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Props                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

interface TodayTaskListProps {
  onShowOverdue?: () => void;
  onReschedule?: (taskId: string) => void;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Main Component                                                     */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function TodayTaskList({ onShowOverdue, onReschedule }: TodayTaskListProps) {
  const [data, setData] = useState<TodayPlanResult | null>(null);
  const [upcomingTasks, setUpcomingTasks] = useState<UpcomingTask[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [showCompleted, setShowCompleted] = useState(false);
  const [showUpcoming, setShowUpcoming] = useState(true);

  const fetchAll = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const [todayRes, upcomingRes] = await Promise.all([
        getTodayPlanAction(),
        getUpcomingTasksAction(10),
      ]);

      if (todayRes.ok) {
        setData(todayRes.data);
        setError(null);
      } else {
        setData(null);
        setError(todayRes.error.code === "NO_ACTIVE_PLAN" ? null : todayRes.error.message);
      }

      if (upcomingRes.ok) {
        setUpcomingTasks(upcomingRes.data as UpcomingTask[]);
      }
    } catch {
      setError("خطا در دریافت اطلاعات");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchAll();
  }, [fetchAll]);

  useVisibilityRefresh(fetchAll, !loading);

  // ---- Loading ----

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-3 animate-pulse">
        <Surface variant="default" padding="md">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <div className="h-4 w-24 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
              <div className="h-3 w-16 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
            </div>
            <div className="h-8 w-14 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
          </div>
          <div className="h-2.5 rounded-full" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
        </Surface>
        {[1, 2, 3].map((i) => (
          <Surface key={i} variant="default" padding="md">
            <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
              <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
              <div className="flex-1 space-y-2">
                <div className="h-4 w-3/4 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
                <div className="h-3 w-1/2 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
              </div>
            </div>
          </Surface>
        ))}
      </div>
    );
  }

  // ---- Error ----

  if (error) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3 py-6">
          <AlertTriangle size={28} style={{ color: colorLight.danger }} />
          <div className="text-center">
            <div className="text-sm font-semibold mb-1" style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}>
              {error}
            </div>
            <div className="text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
              اتصال شما را بررسی کنید و دوباره تلاش کنید
            </div>
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={() => { setLoading(true); fetchAll(); }}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs font-semibold px-4 py-2
              rounded-lg transition-colors"
            style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft, color: colorLight.accent }}
          >
            <RefreshCw size={13} />
            تلاش مجدد
          </button>
        </div>
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  // ---- No active plan ----

  if (!data) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="subtle" padding="lg">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3 py-6">
          <CalendarCheck size={32} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
          <div>
            <div className="text-sm font-semibold mb-1" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
              برنامه فعالی وجود ندارد
            </div>
            <div className="text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
              از تب «برنامه‌ها» یک برنامه مطالعه جدید بسازید.
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  // ---- Data classification ----

  const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);

  // Filter out rescheduled tasks (they have been moved to another day)
  const todayTasks = data.tasks.filter((t) => t.status !== "rescheduled");

  // Overdue tasks from past days (separate section in the UI)
  const overdueTasks = data.overdueTasks ?? [];
  const overdueIds = new Set(overdueTasks.map((t) => t.id));

  // Today's active = not done, not overdue (overdue shown in its own section)
  const activeTasks = todayTasks.filter(
    (t) =>
      t.status !== "completed" &&
      t.status !== "skipped" &&
      t.status !== "overdue" &&
      !overdueIds.has(t.id),
  );
  const completedTasks = todayTasks.filter(
    (t) => t.status === "completed" || t.status === "skipped",
  );

  const totalTasks = todayTasks.length;
  const completedCount = todayTasks.filter((t) => t.status === "completed").length;
  const skippedCount = todayTasks.filter((t) => t.status === "skipped").length;
  const progressPct = totalTasks > 0 ? Math.round((completedCount / totalTasks) * 100) : 0;
  const estimatedMinutes = todayTasks.reduce((s, t) => s + t.estimatedMinutes, 0);
  const remainingMinutes = todayTasks
    .filter((t) => t.status === "pending" || t.status === "in_progress" || t.status === "overdue")
    .reduce((s, t) => s + t.estimatedMinutes, 0);

  const allDone = totalTasks > 0 && completedCount + skippedCount >= totalTasks;

  // Task type breakdown
  const tasksByType: Record<string, number> = {};
  todayTasks.forEach((t) => {
    tasksByType[t.taskType] = (tasksByType[t.taskType] ?? 0) + 1;
  });

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {/* ── PROGRESS SUMMARY ── */}
      <ProgressSummary
        todayDate={today}
        dayLabel={data.day?.label ?? undefined}
        totalTasks={totalTasks}
        completedTasks={completedCount}
        skippedTasks={skippedCount}
        estimatedMinutes={estimatedMinutes}
        remainingMinutes={remainingMinutes}
        overdueTasks={overdueTasks.length}
        progressPct={progressPct}
        tasksByType={tasksByType}
      />

      {/* ── OVERDUE SECTION ── */}
      {overdueTasks.length > 0 && (
        <div>
          <SectionHeader
            label={SECTION_LABEL.overdue}
            count={overdueTasks.length}
            color={colorLight.danger}
            icon={AlertTriangle}
          />
          <div className="space-y-2 mt-1">
            {/* Quick batch action */}
            <Surface variant="default" padding="sm" interactive>
              <button
                onClick={onShowOverdue}
                className="w-full flex items-center justify-between text-xs"
              >
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2" style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}>
                  <AlertTriangle size={13} />
                  <span className="font-semibold">
                    {n(overdueTasks.length)} تسک عقب‌افتاده
                  </span>
                </div>
                <span className="text-[11px] font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}>
                  مدیریت یکجا
                </span>
              </button>
            </Surface>
            <AnimatePresence mode="popLayout">
              {overdueTasks.map((task) => (
                <TaskCard
                  key={task.id}
                  task={task}
                  onMutate={fetchAll}
                  onReschedule={onReschedule}
                  showMoveToToday
                  showSnooze
                  section="overdue"
                />
              ))}
            </AnimatePresence>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* ── ALL DONE CELEBRATION ── */}
      {allDone && (
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
          transition={{ delay: 0.3 }}
        >
          <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md">
            <div className="flex flex-col items-center text-center gap-2 py-4">
              <PartyPopper size={28} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
              <div className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}>
                تبریک! تسک‌های امروز تکمیل شد.
              </div>
            </div>
          </Surface>
        </motion.div>
      )}

      {/* ── REST DAY ── */}
      {data.day?.isRestDay === 1 && totalTasks === 0 && (
        <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md">
          <div className="text-center py-4">
            <div className="text-sm font-semibold mb-1" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
              ☕ امروز روز استراحت است
            </div>
            <div className="text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
              استراحت کنید و انرژی جمع کنید.
            </div>
          </div>
        </Surface>
      )}

      {/* ── TODAY'S ACTIVE TASKS ── */}
      {activeTasks.length > 0 && (
        <div>
          <SectionHeader
            label={SECTION_LABEL.today}
            count={activeTasks.length}
            color={colorLight.accent}
            icon={CalendarCheck}
          />
          <div className="space-y-2 mt-1">
            <AnimatePresence mode="popLayout">
              {activeTasks.map((task) => (
                <TaskCard
                  key={task.id}
                  task={task}
                  onMutate={fetchAll}
                  onReschedule={onReschedule}
                  showSnooze
                  section="today"
                />
              ))}
            </AnimatePresence>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* ── No Day Record ── */}
      {!data.day && totalTasks === 0 && !allDone && (
        <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md">
          <div className="text-center text-sm" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
            برای امروز تسکی تعریف نشده است.
          </div>
        </Surface>
      )}

      {/* ── UPCOMING (THIS WEEK) ── */}
      {upcomingTasks.length > 0 && (
        <div>
          <SectionHeader
            label={SECTION_LABEL.upcoming}
            count={upcomingTasks.length}
            color="#6366F1"
            icon={TrendingUp}
            collapsible
            collapsed={!showUpcoming}
            onToggle={() => setShowUpcoming((v) => !v)}
          />
          <AnimatePresence>
            {showUpcoming && (
              <motion.div
                initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                animate={{ height: "auto", opacity: 1 }}
                exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                className="overflow-hidden"
              >
                <div className="space-y-2 mt-1">
                  {upcomingTasks.map((task) => (
                    <TaskCard
                      key={task.id}
                      task={task}
                      onMutate={fetchAll}
                      onReschedule={onReschedule}
                      showMoveToToday
                      showSnooze
                      section="upcoming"
                    />
                  ))}
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            )}
          </AnimatePresence>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* ── COMPLETED SECTION ── */}
      {completedTasks.length > 0 && (
        <div>
          <SectionHeader
            label={SECTION_LABEL.completed}
            count={completedTasks.length}
            color={colorLight.success}
            icon={CheckCircle2}
            collapsible
            collapsed={!showCompleted}
            onToggle={() => setShowCompleted((v) => !v)}
          />
          <AnimatePresence>
            {showCompleted && (
              <motion.div
                initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                animate={{ height: "auto", opacity: 1 }}
                exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                className="overflow-hidden"
              >
                <div className="space-y-2 mt-1">
                  {completedTasks.map((task) => (
                    <TaskCard
                      key={task.id}
                      task={task}
                      onMutate={fetchAll}
                      section="completed"
                    />
                  ))}
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            )}
          </AnimatePresence>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\planner\WeeklyView.tsx

"use client";

/**
 * WeeklyView — Saturdayâ€"Friday week strip with day columns.
 *
 * Each column shows the day's tasks in a compact layout.
 * Supports navigating to previous/next weeks.
 * Uses getWeekPlanAction to fetch data.
 */

import { useEffect, useState, useCallback } from "react";
import { motion } from "framer-motion";
import {
  ChevronRight,
  ChevronLeft,
  Loader2,
  CalendarCheck,
  Coffee,
  AlertTriangle,
  RefreshCw,
} from "lucide-react";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { TaskCard } from "./TaskCard";
import {
  n,
  getDowLabel,
  formatPersianDateShort,
  isToday,
  useVisibilityRefresh,
} from "./task-helpers";
import { getWeekPlanAction } from "@/lib/actions/planner-actions";
import type { WeekPlanResult } from "@/lib/db/queries/planner";

interface WeeklyViewProps {
  onReschedule?: (taskId: string) => void;
  onShowOverdue?: () => void;
}

function addWeeks(isoDate: string, weeks: number): string {
  const d = new Date(isoDate + "T00:00:00");
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + weeks * 7);
  return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
}

export function WeeklyView({ onReschedule, onShowOverdue }: WeeklyViewProps) {
  const [data, setData] = useState<WeekPlanResult | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [refDate, setRefDate] = useState<string | undefined>(undefined);

  const fetchWeek = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await getWeekPlanAction(refDate);
      if (res.ok) {
        setData(res.data);
        setError(null);
      } else {
        setData(null);
        setError(res.error?.message ?? "خطا در دریافت اطلاعات");
      }
    } catch {
      setData(null);
      setError("خطا در دریافت اطلاعات هفته");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, [refDate]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchWeek();
  }, [fetchWeek]);

  // Re-fetch when tab regains focus
  useVisibilityRefresh(fetchWeek, !loading);

  function goPrev() {
    const base = data?.weekStart ?? new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
    setRefDate(addWeeks(base, -1));
  }

  function goNext() {
    const base = data?.weekStart ?? new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
    setRefDate(addWeeks(base, 1));
  }

  function goThisWeek() {
    setRefDate(undefined);
  }

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-3 animate-pulse">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
          <div className="h-8 w-8 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
          <div className="h-4 w-32 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
          <div className="h-8 w-8 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
        </div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-2">
          {Array.from({ length: 7 }).map((_, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="h-32 rounded-xl" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (error) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3 py-6">
          <AlertTriangle size={28} style={{ color: colorLight.danger }} />
          <div className="text-sm text-center" style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}>
            {error}
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={() => { setError(null); fetchWeek(); }}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs font-semibold px-4 py-2
              rounded-lg transition-colors"
            style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft, color: colorLight.accent }}
          >
            <RefreshCw size={13} />
            تلاش مجدد
          </button>
        </div>
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  if (!data) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="subtle" padding="lg">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center text-center gap-3">
          <CalendarCheck size={32} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
          <div className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
            برنامه فعالی وجود ندارد
          </div>
        </div>
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  const progressPct =
    data.totalTasks > 0
      ? Math.round((data.completedTasks / data.totalTasks) * 100)
      : 0;

  // Check if we're currently viewing "this week"
  const todayStr = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
  const isCurrentWeek = todayStr >= data.weekStart && todayStr <= data.weekEnd;

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {/* ---- Week Navigation ---- */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <button
            onClick={goNext}
            className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors"
            title="هفته بعد"
          >
            <ChevronRight size={18} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={goPrev}
            className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors"
            title="هفته قبل"
          >
            <ChevronLeft size={18} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
          </button>
          {!isCurrentWeek && (
            <button
              onClick={goThisWeek}
              className="text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-md transition-colors"
              style={{ color: colorLight.accent, backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft }}
            >
              این هفته
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
        <div className="text-right">
          <span className="text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
            {formatPersianDateShort(data.weekStart)} — {formatPersianDateShort(data.weekEnd)}
          </span>
          <span className="text-xs mx-2" style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}>
            {n(progressPct)}%
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* ---- Week Progress Bar ---- */}
      <div className="h-1.5 rounded-full overflow-hidden" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}>
        <motion.div
          initial={{ width: 0 }}
          animate={{ width: `${progressPct}%` }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
          className="h-full rounded-full"
          style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accent }}
        />
      </div>

      {/* ---- Day Columns (responsive grid) ---- */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-7 gap-3">
        {data.days.map((day) => {
          const dayTasks = day.tasks ?? [];
          const dayCompleted = dayTasks.filter((t) => t.status === "completed").length;
          const dayTotal = dayTasks.length;
          const todayFlag = isToday(day.date);
          const isRest = day.isRestDay === 1;

          return (
            <motion.div
              key={day.id}
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
            >
              <Surface
                variant={todayFlag ? "elevated" : "default"}
                padding="sm"
                className={`min-h-[120px] ${todayFlag ? "ring-2" : ""}`}
                style={todayFlag ? { borderColor: colorLight.accent } : undefined}
              >
                {/* Day Header */}
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                    <span
                      className={`
                        text-xs font-bold w-6 h-6 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center
                        ${todayFlag ? "text-white" : ""}
                      `}
                      style={{
                        backgroundColor: todayFlag ? colorLight.accent : "transparent",
                        color: todayFlag ? "#fff" : colorLight.text,
                      }}
                    >
                      {getDowLabel(day.dayOfWeek, true)}
                    </span>
                    <span className="text-[10px]" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                      {formatPersianDateShort(day.date)}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  {dayTotal > 0 && (
                    <span className="text-[10px]" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                      {n(dayCompleted)}/{n(dayTotal)}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* Rest Day Indicator */}
                {isRest && dayTotal === 0 && (
                  <div className="flex flex-col items-center text-center py-3 opacity-40">
                    <Coffee size={14} />
                    <span className="text-[10px] mt-1">استراحت</span>
                  </div>
                )}

                {/* Compact Task Cards */}
                <div className="space-y-1.5">
                  {dayTasks.map((task) => (
                    <TaskCard
                      key={task.id}
                      task={{
                        ...task,
                        linkedChapter: undefined,
                        linkedChunk: undefined,
                        linkedExamSession: undefined,
                      }}
                      onMutate={fetchWeek}
                      onReschedule={onReschedule}
                      compact
                    />
                  ))}
                </div>

                {/* Empty non-rest day */}
                {!isRest && dayTotal === 0 && (
                  <div className="text-center py-3">
                    <span className="text-[10px]" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                      بدون تسک
                    </span>
                  </div>
                )}
              </Surface>
            </motion.div>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {/* ---- Overdue Tasks Summary ---- */}
      {data.overdueTasks.length > 0 && (
        <Surface variant="subtle" padding="sm" interactive={!!onShowOverdue}>
          <button
            onClick={onShowOverdue}
            disabled={!onShowOverdue}
            className="w-full flex items-center justify-between text-xs"
          >
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2" style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}>
              <AlertTriangle size={13} />
              <span className="font-semibold">{n(data.overdueTasks.length)} تسک عقب‌افتاده</span>
              <span style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>در این هفته</span>
            </div>
            {onShowOverdue && (
              <span className="text-[11px] font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}>
                مدیریت
              </span>
            )}
          </button>
        </Surface>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\planner\PlannerBucket.tsx

"use client";

/**
 * PlannerBucket — Collapsible section for a group of tasks (overdue, today, etc.)
 *
 * Renders a section header with title, task count, color indicator, and a
 * collapsible task list. Shows an empty-state message when no tasks exist.
 */

import { useState } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import { ChevronDown, ChevronUp } from "lucide-react";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { n } from "./task-helpers";
import type { PlannerSection } from "./task-helpers";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Section theme                                                      */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

const SECTION_THEME: Record<PlannerSection, { accent: string; emptyLabel: string }> = {
  overdue: { accent: colorLight.danger, emptyLabel: "هیچ تسک عقب‌افتاده‌ای نیست 🎉" },
  today: { accent: colorLight.accent, emptyLabel: "تسکی برای امروز نیست — استراحت کن!" },
  thisWeek: { accent: "#7C3AED", emptyLabel: "این هفته خالی است" },
  upcoming: { accent: colorLight.textMuted, emptyLabel: "تسک آینده‌ای وجود ندارد" },
  completed: { accent: colorLight.success, emptyLabel: "هنوز تسکی تکمیل نشده" },
};

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Props                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface PlannerBucketProps {
  section: PlannerSection;
  title: string;
  count: number;
  /** Start collapsed? Defaults to true for `completed`. */
  defaultCollapsed?: boolean;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Component                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function PlannerBucket({
  section,
  title,
  count,
  defaultCollapsed,
  children,
}: PlannerBucketProps) {
  const [collapsed, setCollapsed] = useState(
    defaultCollapsed ?? section === "completed",
  );

  const theme = SECTION_THEME[section];
  const ChevronIcon = collapsed ? ChevronDown : ChevronUp;

  return (
    <div className="mb-4">
      {/* Header */}
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => setCollapsed((v) => !v)}
        className="flex items-center gap-2 w-full py-2 px-1 text-left group"
      >
        {/* Colored dot */}
        <span
          className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full flex-shrink-0"
          style={{ backgroundColor: theme.accent }}
        />

        {/* Title */}
        <span
          className="text-sm font-semibold flex-1"
          style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
        >
          {title}
        </span>

        {/* Count badge */}
        <span
          className="text-xs font-bold tabular-nums px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full"
          style={{
            backgroundColor: count > 0 ? theme.accent + "18" : colorLight.border,
            color: count > 0 ? theme.accent : colorLight.textMuted,
          }}
        >
          {n(count)}
        </span>

        {/* Chevron */}
        <ChevronIcon
          size={14}
          className="transition-transform"
          style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
        />
      </button>

      {/* Collapsible content */}
      <AnimatePresence initial={false}>
        {!collapsed && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ height: "auto", opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
            className="overflow-hidden"
          >
            {count === 0 ? (
              <Surface variant="subtle" padding="sm" className="mt-1">
                <p
                  className="text-xs text-center py-3"
                  style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
                >
                  {theme.emptyLabel}
                </p>
              </Surface>
            ) : (
              <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-1">{children}</div>
            )}
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\planner\PlannerTaskCard.tsx
