"use client";

/**
 * PlannerTaskCard — Bucket-aware task card that wraps the existing TaskCard,
 * adding a source badge and bucket-specific quick actions.
 */

import { useState, useCallback, type CSSProperties } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import { useDraggable } from "@dnd-kit/core";
import { CSS } from "@dnd-kit/utilities";
import {
  CalendarCheck,
  CheckCircle2,
  ArrowLeft,
  Clock,
  Zap,
  AlertTriangle,
  Brain,
  ExternalLink,
  GripVertical,
  Check,
} from "lucide-react";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import {
  getTaskTypeLabel,
  getTaskTypeColor,
  getStatusColors,
  formatMinutes,
  n,
} from "./task-helpers";
import type { TaskBucket } from "@/lib/planner/types";
import type { DragTaskData } from "./dnd/PlannerDndContext";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Source type labels & colors                                        */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

const SOURCE_LABEL: Record<string, string> = {
  manual: "دستی",
  ai_generated: "هوش مصنوعی",
  fsrs_due: "FSRS",
  weak_area: "نقطه ضعف",
};

const SOURCE_COLOR: Record<string, { text: string; bg: string }> = {
  manual: { text: "#6B7280", bg: "#F3F4F6" },
  ai_generated: { text: "#7C3AED", bg: "#F5F3FF" },
  fsrs_due: { text: "#D97706", bg: "#FEF3C7" },
  weak_area: { text: "#DC2626", bg: "#FEE2E2" },
};

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Props                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface PlannerTaskCardProps {
  task: {
    id: string;
    taskType: string;
    status: string;
    title: string;
    description?: string | null;
    estimatedMinutes: number;
    priority: number;
    sourceType?: string | null;
    scheduledFor?: string | null;
    linkUrl?: string | null;
    linkLabel?: string | null;
  };
  bucket: TaskBucket;
  onComplete?: (taskId: string) => void;
  onReschedule?: (taskId: string) => void;
  onMoveToToday?: (taskId: string) => void;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Component                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function PlannerTaskCard({
  task,
  bucket,
  onComplete,
  onReschedule,
  onMoveToToday,
}: PlannerTaskCardProps) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [isCompleting, setIsCompleting] = useState(false);
  const typeColor = getTaskTypeColor(task.taskType);
  const statusColor = getStatusColors(task.status);

  /* ---- Drag & Drop ---- */
  const dragData: DragTaskData = {
    type: "task",
    taskId: task.id,
    sourceDate: task.scheduledFor ?? null,
    sourceBucket: bucket,
    taskTitle: task.title,
    taskType: task.taskType,
  };

  const {
    attributes,
    listeners,
    setNodeRef: dragRef,
    transform,
    isDragging,
  } = useDraggable({ id: task.id, data: dragData });
  const sourceLabel = task.sourceType ? SOURCE_LABEL[task.sourceType] : null;
  const sourceColor = task.sourceType
    ? SOURCE_COLOR[task.sourceType] ?? SOURCE_COLOR.manual
    : null;

  const isCompleted = task.status === "completed";

  const handleCompleteClick = useCallback(() => {
    if (!onComplete || isCompleting) return;
    setIsCompleting(true);
    // Brief delay for the checkmark animation, then fire the real callback
    setTimeout(() => onComplete(task.id), 250);
  }, [onComplete, isCompleting, task.id]);

  const dragStyle: CSSProperties = {
    transform: CSS.Translate.toString(transform),
    zIndex: isDragging ? 50 : undefined,
    boxShadow: isDragging
      ? "0 8px 24px rgba(15,23,42,0.18)"
      : undefined,
  };

  return (
    <div ref={dragRef} style={dragStyle} {...attributes}>
    <motion.div
      layout
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
      animate={{
        opacity: isDragging ? 0.4 : isCompleting ? 0.5 : isCompleted ? 0.6 : 1,
        y: 0,
        scale: isCompleting ? 0.97 : 1,
      }}
      exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.2, ease: "easeOut" }}
    >
    <Surface
      variant="default"
      padding="sm"
      className="group transition-all hover:shadow-[0_2px_8px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] hover:border-[#0EA5A4]/40"
    >
      <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
        {/* Drag handle */}
        <button
          type="button"
          className="mt-1 p-0.5 rounded cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors flex-shrink-0 touch-none"
          style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
          {...listeners}
        >
          <GripVertical size={14} />
        </button>

        {/* Status dot */}
        <span
          className="mt-1.5 w-2 h-2 rounded-full flex-shrink-0"
          style={{ backgroundColor: statusColor.dot }}
        />

        {/* Content */}
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
          {/* Title row */}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
            <span
              className="text-sm font-semibold truncate"
              style={{
                color: isCompleted ? colorLight.textMuted : colorLight.text,
                textDecoration: isCompleted ? "line-through" : "none",
              }}
            >
              {task.title}
            </span>

            {/* Type badge */}
            <span
              className="inline-flex items-center text-[10px] font-semibold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full"
              style={{ color: typeColor.text, backgroundColor: typeColor.bg }}
            >
              {getTaskTypeLabel(task.taskType)}
            </span>

            {/* Source badge */}
            {sourceLabel && sourceColor && (
              <span
                className="inline-flex items-center gap-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full"
                style={{ color: sourceColor.text, backgroundColor: sourceColor.bg }}
              >
                {task.sourceType === "ai_generated" && <Brain size={9} />}
                {task.sourceType === "fsrs_due" && <Zap size={9} />}
                {task.sourceType === "weak_area" && <AlertTriangle size={9} />}
                {sourceLabel}
              </span>
            )}

            {/* Priority */}
            {task.priority >= 2 && (
              <Badge variant="destructive" className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0">
                فوری
              </Badge>
            )}
            {task.priority === 1 && (
              <Badge variant="warning" className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0">
                مهم
              </Badge>
            )}

            {/* Linked concept label */}
            {task.linkLabel && (
              <span
                className="inline-flex items-center gap-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full truncate max-w-[140px]"
                style={{ color: colorLight.accent, backgroundColor: "#E0F2FE" }}
              >
                <ExternalLink size={8} />
                {task.linkLabel}
              </span>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Description (if present) */}
          {task.description && (
            <p
              className="text-xs mt-0.5 line-clamp-1"
              style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
            >
              {task.description}
            </p>
          )}

          {/* Meta row */}
          <div
            className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-1 text-[11px]"
            style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
          >
            {task.estimatedMinutes > 0 && (
              <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
                <Clock size={10} />
                {formatMinutes(task.estimatedMinutes)}
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Action buttons */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity flex-shrink-0">
          {/* Complete */}
          {!isCompleted && onComplete && (
            <button
              type="button"
              title="تکمیل"
              onClick={handleCompleteClick}
              disabled={isCompleting}
              className="p-1.5 rounded-lg hover:bg-emerald-50 transition-colors relative"
              style={{ color: colorLight.success }}
            >
              <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
                {isCompleting ? (
                  <motion.span
                    key="check"
                    initial={{ scale: 0 }}
                    animate={{ scale: 1.2 }}
                    transition={{ duration: 0.15, ease: "easeOut" }}
                  >
                    <Check size={16} strokeWidth={3} />
                  </motion.span>
                ) : (
                  <motion.span key="circle" initial={false}>
                    <CheckCircle2 size={16} />
                  </motion.span>
                )}
              </AnimatePresence>
            </button>
          )}

          {/* Move to today (for overdue / upcoming / thisWeek) */}
          {(bucket === "overdue" || bucket === "upcoming" || bucket === "thisWeek") &&
            !isCompleted &&
            onMoveToToday && (
              <button
                type="button"
                title="انتقال به امروز"
                onClick={() => onMoveToToday(task.id)}
                className="p-1.5 rounded-lg hover:bg-teal-50 transition-colors"
                style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}
              >
                <ArrowLeft size={16} />
              </button>
            )}

          {/* Reschedule */}
          {!isCompleted && onReschedule && (
            <button
              type="button"
              title="تغییر تاریخ"
              onClick={() => onReschedule(task.id)}
              className="p-1.5 rounded-lg hover:bg-amber-50 transition-colors"
              style={{ color: colorLight.warning }}
            >
              <CalendarCheck size={16} />
            </button>
          )}

          {/* Open link */}
          {task.linkUrl && (
            <button
              type="button"
              title={task.linkLabel ?? "باز کردن"}
              onClick={() => router.push(task.linkUrl!)}
              className="p-1.5 rounded-lg hover:bg-slate-50 transition-colors"
              style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}
            >
              <ExternalLink size={16} />
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </Surface>
    </motion.div>
    </div>
  );
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\components\planner\TaskCard.tsx
====================================================================================================

"use client";

/**
 * TaskCard — UWorld-style study task card with full action set.
 *
 * Renders a single study task with status badge, task type icon,
 * progress, and action buttons: complete, start, skip/snooze,
 * move to today, reschedule, open linked resource.
 *
 * Used in both Today/Section and Weekly views.
 */

import { useState, useTransition } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import {
  BookOpen,
  FileText,
  Target,
  CreditCard,
  GraduationCap,
  Notebook,
  Pencil,
  Check,
  SkipForward,
  Play,
  Clock,
  AlertTriangle,
  CalendarDays,
  ExternalLink,
  ArrowLeft,
  AlarmClock,
  MoreHorizontal,
  Trash2,
} from "lucide-react";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import {
  getTaskTypeLabel,
  getStatusColors,
  getTaskStatusLabel,
  getTaskTypeRoute,
  getTaskTypeColor,
  n,
  formatMinutes,
  formatElapsed,
  getPriorityLabel,
  getPriorityColor,
} from "./task-helpers";
import {
  completeTaskAction,
  skipTaskAction,
  startTaskAction,
  snoozeTaskAction,
  moveToTodayAction,
  removeTaskAction,
} from "@/lib/actions/planner-actions";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Icon resolver                                                      */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

const TASK_TYPE_ICONS: Record<string, React.ElementType> = {
  chapter_read: BookOpen,
  chunk_review: FileText,
  question_block: Target,
  flashcard_review: CreditCard,
  exam_block: GraduationCap,
  notebook_review: Notebook,
  custom_task: Pencil,
};

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Props                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface TaskCardProps {
  task: {
    id: string;
    taskType: string;
    status: string;
    title: string;
    description?: string | null;
    estimatedMinutes: number;
    actualMinutes: number;
    progressPercent: number;
    targetCount?: number | null;
    completedCount: number;
    priority: number;
    scheduledDate?: string | null;
    linkedChapter?: { id: string; title: string; chapterNo: number } | null;
    linkedChunk?: { id: string; title: string | null; chunkIndex: number } | null;
    linkedExamSession?: { id: string; title: string | null; status: string } | null;
  };
  /** Called after a mutation so parent can re-fetch */
  onMutate?: () => void;
  /** If provided, shows a reschedule trigger */
  onReschedule?: (taskId: string) => void;
  /** Compact rendering for weekly view cells */
  compact?: boolean;
  /** Show "move to today" action (for overdue/upcoming tasks) */
  showMoveToToday?: boolean;
  /** Show snooze action */
  showSnooze?: boolean;
  /** Section context — affects styling */
  section?: "overdue" | "today" | "thisWeek" | "upcoming" | "completed";
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Component                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function TaskCard({
  task,
  onMutate,
  onReschedule,
  compact,
  showMoveToToday,
  showSnooze,
  section,
}: TaskCardProps) {
  const [isPending, startTransition] = useTransition();
  const [showActions, setShowActions] = useState(false);
  const router = useRouter();

  const status = task.status;
  const isDone = status === "completed";
  const isSkipped = status === "skipped";
  const isOverdue = status === "overdue";
  const isActive = status === "in_progress";
  const isActionable = status === "pending" || isOverdue;

  const Icon = TASK_TYPE_ICONS[task.taskType] ?? Pencil;
  const statusColors = getStatusColors(status);

  // ---- Handlers ----

  function handleMutationError(res: { ok: false; error: { code: string; message: string } }) {
    if (res.error.code === "NOT_FOUND") {
      toast.error("این تسک دیگر وجود ندارد");
      onMutate?.();
    } else if (res.error.code === "INVALID_STATE") {
      toast.error("وضعیت تسک تغییر کرده — لیست بروزرسانی شد");
      onMutate?.();
    } else {
      toast.error(res.error.message);
    }
  }

  function handleComplete() {
    startTransition(async () => {
      const res = await completeTaskAction(task.id);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success("تسک تکمیل شد");
        onMutate?.();
      } else {
        handleMutationError(res);
      }
    });
  }

  function handleSkip() {
    startTransition(async () => {
      const res = await skipTaskAction(task.id);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success("تسک رد شد");
        onMutate?.();
      } else {
        handleMutationError(res);
      }
    });
  }

  function handleStart() {
    startTransition(async () => {
      const res = await startTaskAction(task.id);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success("شروع شد");
        onMutate?.();
      } else {
        handleMutationError(res);
      }
    });
  }

  function handleSnooze(days: number) {
    startTransition(async () => {
      const res = await snoozeTaskAction(task.id, days);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success(days === 1 ? "به فردا منتقل شد" : `${n(days)} روز به تعویق افتاد`);
        onMutate?.();
      } else {
        handleMutationError(res);
      }
    });
    setShowActions(false);
  }

  function handleMoveToToday() {
    startTransition(async () => {
      const res = await moveToTodayAction(task.id);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success("به امروز منتقل شد");
        onMutate?.();
      } else {
        handleMutationError(res);
      }
    });
    setShowActions(false);
  }

  function handleDelete() {
    startTransition(async () => {
      const res = await removeTaskAction(task.id);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success("تسک حذف شد");
        onMutate?.();
      } else {
        handleMutationError(res);
      }
    });
    setShowActions(false);
  }

  function handleNavigateToContent() {
    const route = getTaskTypeRoute(task.taskType, {
      chapter: task.linkedChapter,
      chunk: task.linkedChunk,
      examSession: task.linkedExamSession,
    });
    if (route) router.push(route);
  }

  // ---- Compact Card (weekly view) ----

  if (compact) {
    const typeColor = getTaskTypeColor(task.taskType);
    const hasLink = !!getTaskTypeRoute(task.taskType, {
      chapter: task.linkedChapter,
      chunk: task.linkedChunk,
      examSession: task.linkedExamSession,
    });

    return (
      <motion.div
        layout
        initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
        animate={{ opacity: isPending ? 0.5 : 1 }}
        className={`
          group flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs
          transition-all cursor-default
          ${isDone ? "opacity-60" : ""}
          ${isSkipped ? "opacity-50 line-through" : ""}
        `}
        style={{
          backgroundColor: statusColors.bg,
          color: statusColors.text,
        }}
      >
        <Icon size={13} />
        <span className="truncate flex-1 font-medium">{task.title}</span>
        {task.priority > 0 && (
          <AlertTriangle size={11} style={{ color: colorLight.danger }} />
        )}
        {(isActionable || isActive) && (
          <button
            onClick={handleComplete}
            disabled={isPending}
            className="opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 p-0.5 rounded transition-opacity hover:bg-white/30"
            title="تکمیل"
          >
            <Check size={11} />
          </button>
        )}
        {hasLink && (
          <button
            onClick={handleNavigateToContent}
            className="opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 p-0.5 rounded transition-opacity hover:bg-white/30"
            title="مشاهده محتوا"
          >
            <ExternalLink size={11} />
          </button>
        )}
      </motion.div>
    );
  }

  // ---- Full Card ----

  const contentRoute = getTaskTypeRoute(task.taskType, {
    chapter: task.linkedChapter,
    chunk: task.linkedChunk,
    examSession: task.linkedExamSession,
  });
  const typeColor = getTaskTypeColor(task.taskType);
  const priorityLabel = getPriorityLabel(task.priority);
  const priorityColor = getPriorityColor(task.priority);

  return (
    <motion.div
      layout
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 6 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -6 }}
    >
      <Surface
        variant={isDone ? "subtle" : "default"}
        padding="md"
        className={`
          relative group transition-all
          ${isDone ? "opacity-70" : ""}
          ${isSkipped ? "opacity-50" : ""}
          ${isOverdue ? "ring-1 ring-red-300" : ""}
          ${isPending ? "pointer-events-none" : ""}
        `}
        style={isOverdue ? { borderColor: colorLight.danger } : undefined}
      >
        {/* Pending overlay */}
        {isPending && (
          <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-white/50 rounded-xl z-10 flex items-center justify-center">
            <div
              className="w-5 h-5 border-2 border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin"
              style={{ borderColor: colorLight.accent, borderTopColor: "transparent" }}
            />
          </div>
        )}

        <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
          {/* Left — Icon + Check */}
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1 pt-0.5">
            <div
              className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0"
              style={{ backgroundColor: typeColor.bg }}
            >
              <Icon size={16} style={{ color: typeColor.text }} />
            </div>
            {(isActionable || isActive) && (
              <button
                onClick={handleComplete}
                disabled={isPending}
                className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full border-2 flex items-center justify-center
                  transition-colors hover:border-green-500 hover:bg-green-50"
                style={{ borderColor: colorLight.border }}
                title="تکمیل"
              >
                <Check size={12} className="opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-60 transition-opacity" />
              </button>
            )}
            {isDone && (
              <div
                className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center"
                style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.success, color: "#fff" }}
              >
                <Check size={12} />
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Center — Content */}
          <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-0.5">
              <span
                className={`text-sm font-semibold ${isDone || isSkipped ? "line-through" : ""}`}
                style={{ color: isDone || isSkipped ? colorLight.textMuted : colorLight.text }}
              >
                {task.title}
              </span>
              {priorityLabel && priorityColor && (
                <span
                  className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-bold"
                  style={{
                    backgroundColor: priorityColor.bg,
                    color: priorityColor.text,
                  }}
                >
                  {priorityLabel}
                </span>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Type + linked entity */}
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] mb-1 flex-wrap" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
              <span
                className="px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded"
                style={{ backgroundColor: typeColor.bg, color: typeColor.text }}
              >
                {getTaskTypeLabel(task.taskType)}
              </span>
              {task.linkedChapter && (
                contentRoute ? (
                  <button
                    onClick={handleNavigateToContent}
                    className="flex items-center gap-1 hover:underline transition-colors"
                    style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}
                  >
                    فصل {n(task.linkedChapter.chapterNo)} — {task.linkedChapter.title}
                    <ExternalLink size={10} />
                  </button>
                ) : (
                  <span>فصل {n(task.linkedChapter.chapterNo)} — {task.linkedChapter.title}</span>
                )
              )}
              {task.linkedChunk && task.linkedChunk.title && (
                <span>{task.linkedChunk.title}</span>
              )}
              {task.linkedExamSession && (
                contentRoute ? (
                  <button
                    onClick={handleNavigateToContent}
                    className="flex items-center gap-1 hover:underline transition-colors"
                    style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}
                  >
                    {task.linkedExamSession.title ?? "آزمون"}
                    <ExternalLink size={10} />
                  </button>
                ) : (
                  <span>{task.linkedExamSession.title ?? "آزمون"}</span>
                )
              )}
              {contentRoute && !task.linkedChapter && !task.linkedExamSession && (
                <button
                  onClick={handleNavigateToContent}
                  className="flex items-center gap-1 hover:underline transition-colors"
                  style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}
                >
                  مشاهده
                  <ExternalLink size={10} />
                </button>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Description */}
            {task.description && !isDone && (
              <p className="text-xs mt-1 leading-relaxed" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                {task.description}
              </p>
            )}

            {/* Progress bar */}
            {task.targetCount != null && task.targetCount > 0 && !isDone && (
              <div className="mt-2">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-[10px] mb-1" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                  <span>{n(task.completedCount)} از {n(task.targetCount)}</span>
                  <span>{n(task.progressPercent)}%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="h-1.5 rounded-full overflow-hidden" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}>
                  <div
                    className="h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-300"
                    style={{
                      width: `${task.progressPercent}%`,
                      backgroundColor: statusColors.text,
                    }}
                  />
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Duration + Status */}
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-2 text-[11px]" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
              {task.estimatedMinutes > 0 && (
                <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                  <Clock size={11} />
                  {formatMinutes(task.estimatedMinutes)}
                </span>
              )}
              <span
                className="flex items-center gap-1"
                style={{ color: statusColors.text }}
              >
                <span
                  className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full inline-block"
                  style={{ backgroundColor: statusColors.dot }}
                />
                {getTaskStatusLabel(status)}
              </span>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Right — Action buttons */}
          {(isActionable || isActive) && (
            <div className="flex flex-col gap-1 items-end relative">
              {isActionable && (
                <button
                  onClick={handleStart}
                  disabled={isPending}
                  className="p-1.5 rounded-md transition-colors hover:bg-teal-50"
                  title="شروع"
                >
                  <Play size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
                </button>
              )}

              {/* Move to Today — for overdue/upcoming tasks */}
              {showMoveToToday && (
                <button
                  onClick={handleMoveToToday}
                  disabled={isPending}
                  className="p-1.5 rounded-md transition-colors hover:bg-teal-50"
                  title="انتقال به امروز"
                >
                  <ArrowLeft size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
                </button>
              )}

              {/* Snooze — quick 1 day */}
              {showSnooze && (
                <button
                  onClick={() => handleSnooze(1)}
                  disabled={isPending}
                  className="p-1.5 rounded-md transition-colors hover:bg-amber-50"
                  title="تعویق به فردا"
                >
                  <AlarmClock size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.warning }} />
                </button>
              )}

              <button
                onClick={handleSkip}
                disabled={isPending}
                className="p-1.5 rounded-md transition-colors hover:bg-gray-100"
                title="رد کردن"
              >
                <SkipForward size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
              </button>

              {onReschedule && (
                <button
                  onClick={() => onReschedule(task.id)}
                  className="p-1.5 rounded-md transition-colors hover:bg-gray-100"
                  title="تغییر تاریخ"
                >
                  <CalendarDays size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
                </button>
              )}

              {/* More actions menu */}
              <div className="relative">
                <button
                  onClick={() => setShowActions(!showActions)}
                  className="p-1.5 rounded-md transition-colors hover:bg-gray-100
                    opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100"
                  title="عملیات بیشتر"
                >
                  <MoreHorizontal size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
                </button>

                <AnimatePresence>
                  {showActions && (
                    <>
                      {/* Click-away overlay */}
                      <div
                        className="fixed inset-0 z-10"
                        onClick={() => setShowActions(false)}
                      />
                      <motion.div
                        initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
                        animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
                        exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
                        className="absolute left-0 top-full mt-1 z-20 bg-white border rounded-xl shadow-lg
                          min-w-[160px] py-1 text-xs"
                        style={{ borderColor: colorLight.border }}
                      >
                        {showSnooze && (
                          <>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleSnooze(1)}
                              className="w-full text-right px-3 py-2 hover:bg-gray-50 flex items-center gap-2"
                              style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
                            >
                              <AlarmClock size={12} style={{ color: colorLight.warning }} />
                              تعویق ۱ روز
                            </button>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleSnooze(2)}
                              className="w-full text-right px-3 py-2 hover:bg-gray-50 flex items-center gap-2"
                              style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
                            >
                              <AlarmClock size={12} style={{ color: colorLight.warning }} />
                              تعویق ۲ روز
                            </button>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleSnooze(7)}
                              className="w-full text-right px-3 py-2 hover:bg-gray-50 flex items-center gap-2"
                              style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
                            >
                              <AlarmClock size={12} style={{ color: colorLight.warning }} />
                              تعویق ۱ هفته
                            </button>
                          </>
                        )}
                        {showMoveToToday && (
                          <button
                            onClick={handleMoveToToday}
                            className="w-full text-right px-3 py-2 hover:bg-gray-50 flex items-center gap-2"
                            style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
                          >
                            <ArrowLeft size={12} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
                            انتقال به امروز
                          </button>
                        )}
                        <div className="border-t my-1" style={{ borderColor: colorLight.border }} />
                        <button
                          onClick={handleDelete}
                          className="w-full text-right px-3 py-2 hover:bg-red-50 flex items-center gap-2"
                          style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}
                        >
                          <Trash2 size={12} />
                          حذف تسک
                        </button>
                      </motion.div>
                    </>
                  )}
                </AnimatePresence>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Completed/Skipped — open content only */}
          {(isDone || isSkipped) && contentRoute && (
            <button
              onClick={handleNavigateToContent}
              className="p-1.5 rounded-md transition-colors hover:bg-gray-100 self-start"
              title="مشاهده محتوا"
            >
              <ExternalLink size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </Surface>
    </motion.div>
  );
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\components\planner\RecommendationPanel.tsx
====================================================================================================

"use client";

/**
 * RecommendationPanel — Bucketed study recommendations UI.
 *
 * Displays categorised recommendations (Due Reviews, Missed Concepts,
 * Weak Areas, Exam Prep) and lets the user accept them as planner tasks.
 *
 * Persian RTL · restrained UWorld-style design · colorLight tokens.
 */

import { useState, useCallback, useEffect } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import {
  Brain,
  Zap,
  BookOpen,
  Target,
  AlertTriangle,
  CheckCircle2,
  ChevronDown,
  ChevronUp,
  Clock,
  Plus,
  RefreshCw,
  RotateCcw,
  Sparkles,
  XCircle,
} from "lucide-react";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { n } from "@/components/planner/task-helpers";
import {
  getRecommendationsAction,
  acceptRecommendationAction,
} from "@/lib/actions/planner-recommendation-actions";
import type {
  RecommendationResult,
  Recommendation,
  RecommendationBucket,
} from "@/lib/services/planner-recommendation-service";

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Constants                                                          */
/* ================================================================== */

const BUCKET_ICONS: Record<RecommendationBucket, React.ElementType> = {
  due_reviews: Zap,
  flashcard_lapses: RotateCcw,
  missed_concepts: XCircle,
  weak_areas: Target,
  exam_prep: BookOpen,
  custom: Sparkles,
};

const BUCKET_COLORS: Record<RecommendationBucket, string> = {
  due_reviews: colorLight.accent,
  flashcard_lapses: "#F97316", // orange
  missed_concepts: colorLight.danger,
  weak_areas: "#F59E0B", // amber
  exam_prep: "#8B5CF6", // violet
  custom: colorLight.textMuted,
};

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Props                                                              */
/* ================================================================== */

interface RecommendationPanelProps {
  /** Callback after a recommendation is accepted (e.g., refresh task list). */
  onTaskCreated?: () => void;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Component                                                          */
/* ================================================================== */

export function RecommendationPanel({ onTaskCreated }: RecommendationPanelProps) {
  const [data, setData] = useState<RecommendationResult | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [expandedBuckets, setExpandedBuckets] = useState<Set<string>>(
    new Set(["due_reviews", "missed_concepts", "weak_areas", "exam_prep"]),
  );
  const [acceptingId, setAcceptingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [acceptedIds, setAcceptedIds] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());

  const fetch = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      const res = await getRecommendationsAction();
      if (res.ok) {
        setData(res.data);
      } else {
        setError(res.error.message);
      }
    } catch {
      setError("خطا در دریافت پیشنهادها");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch();
  }, [fetch]);

  function toggleBucket(id: string) {
    setExpandedBuckets((prev) => {
      const next = new Set(prev);
      if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id);
      else next.add(id);
      return next;
    });
  }

  async function handleAccept(rec: Recommendation) {
    if (acceptedIds.has(rec.id)) return;
    setAcceptingId(rec.id);
    try {
      const res = await acceptRecommendationAction(rec);
      if (res.ok) {
        setAcceptedIds((prev) => new Set(prev).add(rec.id));
        toast.success("تسک به برنامه امروز اضافه شد");
        onTaskCreated?.();
      } else {
        if (res.error.code === "NO_ACTIVE_PLAN") {
          toast.error("ابتدا یک برنامه فعال ایجاد کنید");
        } else {
          toast.error(res.error.message);
        }
      }
    } catch {
      toast.error("خطا در ایجاد تسک");
    } finally {
      setAcceptingId(null);
    }
  }

  /* ---- Loading skeleton ---- */
  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-4">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
          <Brain size={18} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
          <span
            className="text-sm font-semibold"
            style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
          >
            پیشنهادهای هوشمند
          </span>
        </div>
        {[1, 2, 3].map((i) => (
          <Surface key={i} variant="subtle" padding="sm">
            <div className="animate-pulse space-y-2">
              <div
                className="h-4 rounded w-1/3"
                style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}
              />
              <div
                className="h-3 rounded w-2/3"
                style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}
              />
            </div>
          </Surface>
        ))}
      </div>
    );
  }

  /* ---- Error state ---- */
  if (error) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3 py-4">
          <AlertTriangle size={24} style={{ color: colorLight.danger }} />
          <div
            className="text-xs"
            style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
          >
            {error}
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={fetch}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg transition-colors"
            style={{
              backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft,
              color: colorLight.accent,
            }}
          >
            <RefreshCw size={12} />
            تلاش مجدد
          </button>
        </div>
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  /* ---- Empty state ---- */
  if (!data || data.totalRecommendations === 0) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3 py-6">
          <CheckCircle2
            size={28}
            style={{ color: colorLight.success }}
          />
          <div
            className="text-sm font-semibold"
            style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
          >
            همه چیز به‌روز است!
          </div>
          <div
            className="text-xs text-center"
            style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
          >
            در حال حاضر پیشنهاد خاصی وجود ندارد. با ادامه مطالعه و آزمون‌ها، پیشنهادهای شخصی‌سازی‌شده دریافت خواهید کرد.
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={fetch}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg transition-colors mt-1"
            style={{
              backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft,
              color: colorLight.accent,
            }}
          >
            <RefreshCw size={12} />
            بررسی مجدد
          </button>
        </div>
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  /* ---- Data content ---- */
  const nonEmptyBuckets = data.buckets.filter((b) => b.totalCount > 0);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Brain size={18} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
          <span
            className="text-sm font-semibold"
            style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
          >
            پیشنهادهای هوشمند
          </span>
          <span
            className="text-[10px] font-medium px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full"
            style={{
              backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft,
              color: colorLight.accent,
            }}
          >
            {n(data.totalRecommendations)} پیشنهاد
          </span>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={fetch}
          className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] px-2 py-1 rounded-lg transition-colors"
          style={{
            color: colorLight.textMuted,
          }}
        >
          <RefreshCw size={11} />
          بروزرسانی
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Active plan info */}
      {data.activePlan && (
        <div
          className="text-[10px] px-2 py-1 rounded-lg"
          style={{
            backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft,
            color: colorLight.textMuted,
          }}
        >
          تسک‌ها به برنامه «{data.activePlan.title}» اضافه می‌شوند
        </div>
      )}

      {!data.activePlan && (
        <div
          className="text-[10px] px-2 py-1.5 rounded-lg"
          style={{
            backgroundColor: `${colorLight.danger}15`,
            color: colorLight.danger,
          }}
        >
          برنامه فعالی وجود ندارد — برای اضافه کردن تسک ابتدا یک برنامه بسازید
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Buckets */}
      <div className="space-y-3">
        {nonEmptyBuckets.map((bucket) => {
          const BucketIcon = BUCKET_ICONS[bucket.id];
          const bucketColor = BUCKET_COLORS[bucket.id];
          const isExpanded = expandedBuckets.has(bucket.id);

          return (
            <Surface key={bucket.id} variant="default" padding="none">
              {/* Bucket header */}
              <button
                onClick={() => toggleBucket(bucket.id)}
                className="w-full flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 transition-colors"
                style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
              >
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <BucketIcon size={15} style={{ color: bucketColor }} />
                  <span className="text-[13px] font-semibold">
                    {bucket.label}
                  </span>
                  <span
                    className="text-[10px] font-medium px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full"
                    style={{
                      backgroundColor: `${bucketColor}20`,
                      color: bucketColor,
                    }}
                  >
                    {n(bucket.totalCount)}
                  </span>
                </div>
                {isExpanded ? (
                  <ChevronUp size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
                ) : (
                  <ChevronDown size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
                )}
              </button>

              {/* Bucket description */}
              {isExpanded && (
                <div
                  className="px-4 pb-1 text-[10px]"
                  style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
                >
                  {bucket.description}
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Recommendations */}
              <AnimatePresence initial={false}>
                {isExpanded && (
                  <motion.div
                    initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                    animate={{ height: "auto", opacity: 1 }}
                    exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                    transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
                    className="overflow-hidden"
                  >
                    <div className="px-3 pb-3 space-y-2">
                      {bucket.recommendations.map((rec) => (
                        <RecommendationCard
                          key={rec.id}
                          rec={rec}
                          bucketColor={bucketColor}
                          isAccepted={acceptedIds.has(rec.id)}
                          isAccepting={acceptingId === rec.id}
                          onAccept={() => handleAccept(rec)}
                          disabled={!data.activePlan}
                        />
                      ))}
                      {bucket.totalCount > bucket.recommendations.length && (
                        <div
                          className="text-center text-[10px] py-1"
                          style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
                        >
                          و {n(bucket.totalCount - bucket.recommendations.length)} پیشنهاد دیگر…
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </motion.div>
                )}
              </AnimatePresence>
            </Surface>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  RecommendationCard                                                 */
/* ================================================================== */

function RecommendationCard({
  rec,
  bucketColor,
  isAccepted,
  isAccepting,
  onAccept,
  disabled,
}: {
  rec: Recommendation;
  bucketColor: string;
  isAccepted: boolean;
  isAccepting: boolean;
  onAccept: () => void;
  disabled: boolean;
}) {
  return (
    <div
      className="rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 transition-all"
      style={{
        backgroundColor: isAccepted ? `${colorLight.success}10` : colorLight.surfaceSubtle,
        borderRight: `3px solid ${isAccepted ? colorLight.success : bucketColor}`,
        opacity: isAccepted ? 0.7 : 1,
      }}
    >
      <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
        {/* Content */}
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 space-y-1">
          <div
            className="text-[12px] font-semibold leading-snug"
            style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
          >
            {rec.title}
          </div>
          <div
            className="text-[10px] leading-relaxed"
            style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
          >
            {rec.description}
          </div>
          {/* Reason */}
          <div
            className="text-[10px] leading-relaxed"
            style={{ color: bucketColor }}
          >
            💡 {rec.reason}
          </div>
          {/* Meta */}
          <div
            className="flex items-center gap-3 text-[9px]"
            style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
          >
            <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
              <Clock size={9} />
              ~{n(rec.estimatedMinutes)} دقیقه
            </span>
            {rec.targetCount && (
              <span>
                {n(rec.targetCount)} آیتم
              </span>
            )}
            {rec.chapterTitle && (
              <span className="truncate max-w-[120px]">
                {rec.chapterTitle}
              </span>
            )}
            {rec.priority >= 2 && (
              <span
                className="font-semibold"
                style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}
              >
                فوری
              </span>
            )}
            {rec.priority === 1 && (
              <span
                className="font-semibold"
                style={{ color: "#F59E0B" }}
              >
                مهم
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Accept button */}
        <button
          onClick={onAccept}
          disabled={disabled || isAccepted || isAccepting}
          className="flex-shrink-0 flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] font-semibold px-2.5 py-1.5 rounded-lg transition-all"
          style={{
            backgroundColor: isAccepted
              ? `${colorLight.success}20`
              : colorLight.accentSoft,
            color: isAccepted ? colorLight.success : colorLight.accent,
            opacity: disabled ? 0.4 : 1,
            cursor: disabled || isAccepted ? "default" : "pointer",
          }}
        >
          {isAccepting ? (
            <RefreshCw size={11} className="animate-spin" />
          ) : isAccepted ? (
            <>
              <CheckCircle2 size={11} />
              اضافه شد
            </>
          ) : (
            <>
              <Plus size={11} />
              اضافه به برنامه
            </>
          )}
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\planner\PlannerRecommendationCard.tsx

"use client";

/**
 * PlannerRecommendationCard — Displays the recommendation engine output:
 * next best action, focus area, overload level, task mix, and suggestions.
 */

import {
  Lightbulb,
  Target,
  Gauge,
  BookOpen,
  CreditCard,
  AlertTriangle,
  FileText,
} from "lucide-react";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import type {
  Recommendation,
  OverloadLevel,
  TaskMix,
} from "@/lib/planner/recommendation-engine";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Props                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface PlannerRecommendationCardProps {
  recommendation: Recommendation;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Overload config                                                    */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

const OVERLOAD: Record<
  OverloadLevel,
  { label: string; color: string; bg: string; variant: "success" | "warning" | "destructive" }
> = {
  low: {
    label: "عادی",
    color: colorLight.success,
    bg: "#ECFDF5",
    variant: "success",
  },
  moderate: {
    label: "متوسط",
    color: colorLight.warning,
    bg: "#FFFBEB",
    variant: "warning",
  },
  high: {
    label: "سنگین",
    color: colorLight.danger,
    bg: "#FEF2F2",
    variant: "destructive",
  },
};

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Task mix bar                                                       */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

interface MixSegment {
  key: keyof TaskMix;
  label: string;
  color: string;
  icon: React.ElementType;
}

const MIX_SEGMENTS: MixSegment[] = [
  { key: "flashcardMinutes", label: "فلش‌کارت", color: "#F59E0B", icon: CreditCard },
  { key: "questionMinutes", label: "تست", color: colorLight.accent, icon: BookOpen },
  { key: "weakAreaMinutes", label: "نقطه ضعف", color: "#EF4444", icon: AlertTriangle },
  { key: "notebookMinutes", label: "دفترچه", color: "#8B5CF6", icon: FileText },
];

function TaskMixBar({ mix }: { mix: TaskMix }) {
  const total =
    mix.flashcardMinutes +
    mix.questionMinutes +
    mix.weakAreaMinutes +
    mix.notebookMinutes;

  if (total === 0) return null;

  return (
    <div>
      {/* Stacked bar */}
      <div className="flex h-2 rounded-full overflow-hidden" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}>
        {MIX_SEGMENTS.map((seg) => {
          const mins = mix[seg.key];
          if (mins <= 0) return null;
          const pct = (mins / total) * 100;
          return (
            <div
              key={seg.key}
              style={{ width: `${pct}%`, backgroundColor: seg.color }}
              className="transition-all duration-300"
            />
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {/* Legend */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-2 flex-wrap">
        {MIX_SEGMENTS.map((seg) => {
          const mins = mix[seg.key];
          if (mins <= 0) return null;
          const Icon = seg.icon;
          return (
            <div key={seg.key} className="flex items-center gap-1">
              <Icon size={10} style={{ color: seg.color }} />
              <span
                className="text-[10px]"
                style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
              >
                {seg.label}
              </span>
              <span
                className="text-[10px] font-bold tabular-nums"
                style={{ color: seg.color }}
              >
                {mins}د
              </span>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Component                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function PlannerRecommendationCard({
  recommendation,
}: PlannerRecommendationCardProps) {
  const {
    nextBestAction,
    recommendedFocusArea,
    overloadLevel,
    taskMix,
    suggestions,
  } = recommendation;

  const overload = OVERLOAD[overloadLevel];

  return (
    <Surface variant="default" padding="sm" className="mb-4">
      {/* Header row: icon + title + overload badge */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2 mb-3">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
          <Lightbulb size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.accent, flexShrink: 0 }} />
          <span
            className="text-[11px] font-semibold tracking-wider"
            style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
          >
            پیشنهاد مطالعه
          </span>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-shrink-0">
          {/* Focus area badge */}
          <span
            className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] font-semibold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full"
            style={{ color: colorLight.accent, backgroundColor: "#E0F2FE" }}
          >
            <Target size={9} />
            {recommendedFocusArea}
          </span>

          {/* Overload badge */}
          <Badge variant={overload.variant} className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0 gap-0.5">
            <Gauge size={9} />
            {overload.label}
          </Badge>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Next best action — prominent */}
      <div
        className="text-sm font-semibold leading-snug mb-3"
        style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
      >
        {nextBestAction}
      </div>

      {/* Task mix breakdown */}
      <TaskMixBar mix={taskMix} />

      {/* Suggestions */}
      {suggestions.length > 0 && (
        <div className="mt-3 pt-2" style={{ borderTop: `1px solid ${colorLight.border}` }}>
          <ul className="flex flex-col gap-1">
            {suggestions.map((tip, i) => (
              <li
                key={i}
                className="text-[11px] leading-relaxed flex items-start gap-1.5"
                style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}
              >
                <span className="mt-0.5 flex-shrink-0" style={{ color: colorLight.warning }}>•</span>
                {tip}
              </li>
            ))}
          </ul>
        </div>
      )}
    </Surface>
  );
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\components\planner\PlannerDashboardCard.tsx
====================================================================================================

"use client";

/**
 * PlannerDashboardCard — UWorld-style compact planner summary widget.
 *
 * Shows:
 * - Circular progress indicator
 * - Today's task count + completion
 * - Overdue alert badge
 * - Streak counter
 * - Upcoming next task preview
 * - Quick link to full planner
 *
 * Designed for the main dashboard. Clean, clinical aesthetic.
 */

import { useEffect, useState, useCallback } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { motion } from "framer-motion";
import {
  CalendarCheck,
  AlertTriangle,
  ArrowLeft,
  Flame,
  RefreshCw,
  Clock,
  Target,
  BookOpen,
  CreditCard,
  GraduationCap,
  ChevronLeft,
  Brain,
} from "lucide-react";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { useVisibilityRefresh } from "@/components/planner/task-helpers";
import { getPlannerSummaryAction } from "@/lib/actions/planner-actions";
import { getRecommendationCountAction } from "@/lib/actions/planner-recommendation-actions";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

interface SummaryData {
  plan: {
    title: string;
    progressPercent: number;
    completedTasks: number;
    totalTasks: number;
  } | null;
  today: {
    totalTasks: number;
    completedTasks: number;
    progressPercent: number;
    estimatedMinutes: number;
  } | null;
  streak: { current: number; longest: number };
  overdueTasks: number;
  upcomingTaskCount: number;
}

const nf = new Intl.NumberFormat("fa-IR");
const n = (v: number) => nf.format(v);

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Circular Progress Ring                                             */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function ProgressRing({ percent, size = 52 }: { percent: number; size?: number }) {
  const stroke = 4;
  const radius = (size - stroke) / 2;
  const circumference = 2 * Math.PI * radius;
  const offset = circumference - (percent / 100) * circumference;
  const color = percent >= 100 ? colorLight.success : colorLight.accent;

  return (
    <svg width={size} height={size} className="block -rotate-90">
      {/* Background track */}
      <circle
        cx={size / 2}
        cy={size / 2}
        r={radius}
        stroke={colorLight.border}
        strokeWidth={stroke}
        fill="none"
      />
      {/* Progress arc */}
      <motion.circle
        cx={size / 2}
        cy={size / 2}
        r={radius}
        stroke={color}
        strokeWidth={stroke}
        strokeLinecap="round"
        fill="none"
        strokeDasharray={circumference}
        initial={{ strokeDashoffset: circumference }}
        animate={{ strokeDashoffset: offset }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.8, delay: 0.3, ease: "easeOut" }}
      />
    </svg>
  );
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Component                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function PlannerDashboardCard() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [data, setData] = useState<SummaryData | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState(false);
  const [recCount, setRecCount] = useState(0);

  const fetchSummary = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const [summaryRes, recRes] = await Promise.all([
        getPlannerSummaryAction(),
        getRecommendationCountAction(),
      ]);
      if (summaryRes.ok) {
        setData(summaryRes.data);
        setError(false);
      } else {
        setError(true);
      }
      if (recRes.ok) {
        setRecCount(recRes.data);
      }
    } catch {
      setError(true);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchSummary();
  }, [fetchSummary]);

  useVisibilityRefresh(fetchSummary, !loading);

  // ---- Loading skeleton ----

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="default" padding="md" className="animate-pulse">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-3">
          <div className="w-[52px] h-[52px] rounded-full" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
          <div className="space-y-1.5 flex-1">
            <div className="h-4 w-24 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
            <div className="h-3 w-16 rounded" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="h-2 rounded-full" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }} />
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  // ---- Error state ----

  if (error) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div
              className="w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center"
              style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft }}
            >
              <CalendarCheck size={18} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
            </div>
            <div className="text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
              خطا در بارگذاری برنامه
            </div>
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={() => { setLoading(true); setError(false); fetchSummary(); }}
            className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5
              rounded-lg transition-colors"
            style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft, color: colorLight.accent }}
          >
            <RefreshCw size={12} />
            تلاش مجدد
          </button>
        </div>
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  // ---- No plan — CTA ----

  if (!data?.plan) {
    return (
      <Surface variant="subtle" padding="md" interactive>
        <button
          onClick={() => router.push("/planner")}
          className="w-full text-right"
        >
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-3">
            <div
              className="w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center"
              style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft }}
            >
              <CalendarCheck size={18} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
            </div>
            <div className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
              برنامه‌ریزی مطالعه
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
            هنوز برنامه‌ای ایجاد نکرده‌اید. یک برنامه مطالعه جدید بسازید.
          </div>
          <div
            className="mt-3 text-xs font-semibold flex items-center gap-1"
            style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}
          >
            ایجاد برنامه
            <ArrowLeft size={14} />
          </div>
        </button>
      </Surface>
    );
  }

  // ---- Active plan dashboard ----

  const todayPct = data.today?.progressPercent ?? 0;
  const todayDone = data.today?.completedTasks ?? 0;
  const todayTotal = data.today?.totalTasks ?? 0;
  const planPct = data.plan.progressPercent;

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.4, delay: 0.5 }}
    >
      <Surface variant="default" padding="md" interactive>
        <button
          onClick={() => router.push("/planner")}
          className="w-full text-right"
        >
          {/* Header Row — Ring + Info */}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-3">
            {/* Circular progress */}
            <div className="relative flex-shrink-0">
              <ProgressRing percent={todayPct} />
              <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center">
                <span
                  className="text-xs font-bold tabular-nums"
                  style={{ color: todayPct >= 100 ? colorLight.success : colorLight.accent }}
                >
                  {n(todayPct)}%
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Title + Plan name */}
            <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
              <div className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                برنامه امروز
              </div>
              <div className="text-[11px] mt-0.5 truncate" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                {data.plan.title}
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Navigate arrow */}
            <ChevronLeft size={16} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
          </div>

          {/* Plan-level progress bar (thin) */}
          <div className="mb-3">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-[10px] mb-1" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
              <span>پیشرفت کل</span>
              <span>{n(planPct)}%</span>
            </div>
            <div className="h-1.5 rounded-full overflow-hidden" style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.border }}>
              <motion.div
                initial={{ width: 0 }}
                animate={{ width: `${planPct}%` }}
                transition={{ duration: 0.8, delay: 0.6 }}
                className="h-full rounded-full"
                style={{ backgroundColor: planPct >= 100 ? colorLight.success : colorLight.accent }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Stats row */}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
            <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
              <CalendarCheck size={12} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
              {n(todayDone)}/{n(todayTotal)} تسک
            </span>
            {data.streak.current > 0 && (
              <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                <Flame size={12} style={{ color: colorLight.warning }} />
                {n(data.streak.current)} روز
              </span>
            )}
            {data.overdueTasks > 0 && (
              <span
                className="flex items-center gap-1 font-semibold"
                style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}
              >
                <AlertTriangle size={12} />
                {n(data.overdueTasks)} عقب‌افتاده
              </span>
            )}
            {data.today && data.today.estimatedMinutes > 0 && todayDone < todayTotal && (
              <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                <Clock size={12} />
                ~{n(Math.max(0, Math.round(data.today.estimatedMinutes * (todayTotal - todayDone) / Math.max(todayTotal, 1))))} دقیقه
              </span>
            )}
            {recCount > 0 && (
              <span className="flex items-center gap-1" style={{ color: colorLight.accent }}>
                <Brain size={12} />
                {n(recCount)} پیشنهاد
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
        </button>
      </Surface>
    </motion.div>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\planner\OverdueModal.tsx
