"use client";

/**
 * OverdueModal — dialog for managing overdue study tasks.
 *
 * Two strategies:
 * - Carry Over: move all overdue tasks to today
 * - Catch Up: create a focused catch-up session with a time budget
 *
 * Uses carryOverAction / createCatchUpAction server actions.
 */

import { useEffect, useState, useTransition, useCallback } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import {
  AlertTriangle,
  ArrowLeft,
  Clock,
  X,
  Loader2,
  CheckCircle2,
} from "lucide-react";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import {
  n,
  formatMinutes,
  getTaskTypeLabel,
  getStatusColors,
  formatPersianDate,
} from "./task-helpers";
import {
  getOverdueTasksAction,
  carryOverAction,
  createCatchUpAction,
} from "@/lib/actions/planner-actions";

interface OverdueTask {
  id: string;
  taskType: string;
  status: string;
  title: string;
  estimatedMinutes: number;
  priority: number;
  dayDate: string;
}

interface OverdueModalProps {
  open: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  /** Called after overdue tasks are handled */
  onResolved?: () => void;
}

export function OverdueModal({ open, onClose, onResolved }: OverdueModalProps) {
  const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<OverdueTask[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [fetchError, setFetchError] = useState(false);
  const [isPending, startTransition] = useTransition();
  const [strategy, setStrategy] = useState<"carry_over" | "catch_up" | null>(null);
  const [catchUpMinutes, setCatchUpMinutes] = useState(60);
  const [done, setDone] = useState(false);

  const fetchOverdue = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    setFetchError(false);
    try {
      const res = await getOverdueTasksAction();
      if (res.ok) {
        setTasks(res.data);
      } else {
        setFetchError(true);
      }
    } catch {
      setFetchError(true);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (open) {
      setDone(false);
      setStrategy(null);
      setFetchError(false);
      fetchOverdue();
    }
  }, [open, fetchOverdue]);

  function handleCarryOver() {
    startTransition(async () => {
      const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
      const res = await carryOverAction(today);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success(`${n(res.data.carriedTasks)} تسک به امروز منتقل شد`);
        setDone(true);
        onResolved?.();
      } else {
        toast.error(res.error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function handleCatchUp() {
    startTransition(async () => {
      const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
      const res = await createCatchUpAction(today, catchUpMinutes);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success(`جلسه جبرانی ایجاد شد`);
        setDone(true);
        onResolved?.();
      } else {
        toast.error(res.error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  if (!open) return null;

  const totalEstimated = tasks.reduce((s, t) => s + t.estimatedMinutes, 0);

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {open && (
        <>
          {/* Backdrop */}
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            onClick={onClose}
            className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/40"
          />

          {/* Panel */}
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 24 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 24 }}
            transition={{ type: "spring", damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
            className="fixed inset-x-4 bottom-4 top-auto z-50 max-w-lg mx-auto
                       sm:inset-auto sm:top-1/2 sm:left-1/2 sm:-translate-x-1/2 sm:-translate-y-1/2
                       max-h-[85vh] overflow-y-auto"
          >
            <Surface variant="elevated" padding="lg" className="rounded-2xl shadow-xl">
              {/* Header */}
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <div
                    className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center"
                    style={{ backgroundColor: "#FEE2E2" }}
                  >
                    <AlertTriangle size={20} style={{ color: colorLight.danger }} />
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <h2 className="text-base font-bold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                      تسک‌های عقب‌افتاده
                    </h2>
                    <p className="text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                      {n(tasks.length)} تسک — {formatMinutes(totalEstimated)}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <button
                  onClick={onClose}
                  className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors"
                >
                  <X size={18} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
                </button>
              </div>

              {/* Loading */}
              {loading && (
                <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-8">
                  <Loader2 size={24} className="animate-spin" style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Fetch Error */}
              {!loading && fetchError && (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3 py-8">
                  <AlertTriangle size={28} style={{ color: colorLight.danger }} />
                  <div className="text-sm" style={{ color: colorLight.danger }}>
                    خطا در دریافت تسک‌های عقب‌افتاده
                  </div>
                  <button
                    onClick={fetchOverdue}
                    className="text-xs px-4 py-2 rounded-lg transition-colors"
                    style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accentSoft, color: colorLight.accent }}
                  >
                    تلاش مجدد
                  </button>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Done State */}
              {done && (
                <motion.div
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
                  className="flex flex-col items-center text-center gap-3 py-8"
                >
                  <CheckCircle2 size={32} style={{ color: colorLight.success }} />
                  <div className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.success }}>
                    عقب‌افتادگی مدیریت شد!
                  </div>
                  <button
                    onClick={onClose}
                    className="text-xs mt-2 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg transition-colors"
                    style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accent, color: "#fff" }}
                  >
                    بستن
                  </button>
                </motion.div>
              )}

              {/* No overdue tasks */}
              {!loading && !done && tasks.length === 0 && (
                <div className="text-center py-8">
                  <div className="text-sm" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                    تسک عقب‌افتاده‌ای وجود ندارد 🎉
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Task list + strategies */}
              {!loading && !done && tasks.length > 0 && (
                <>
                  {/* Overdue Task List */}
                  <div className="space-y-2 mb-5 max-h-[200px] overflow-y-auto">
                    {tasks.map((task) => {
                      const sc = getStatusColors(task.status);
                      return (
                        <div
                          key={task.id}
                          className="flex items-center gap-3 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-xs"
                          style={{ backgroundColor: sc.bg }}
                        >
                          <span
                            className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full flex-shrink-0"
                            style={{ backgroundColor: sc.dot }}
                          />
                          <span className="flex-1 truncate font-medium" style={{ color: sc.text }}>
                            {task.title}
                          </span>
                          <span style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                            {getTaskTypeLabel(task.taskType)}
                          </span>
                          {task.estimatedMinutes > 0 && (
                            <span className="flex items-center gap-1" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                              <Clock size={10} />
                              {n(task.estimatedMinutes)}د
                            </span>
                          )}
                          <span className="text-[10px]" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                            {formatPersianDate(task.dayDate)}
                          </span>
                        </div>
                      );
                    })}
                  </div>

                  {/* Strategy Selection */}
                  <div className="border-t pt-4 space-y-3" style={{ borderColor: colorLight.border }}>
                    <h3 className="text-xs font-semibold mb-2" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                      راهکار مدیریت:
                    </h3>

                    {/* Option 1: Carry Over */}
                    <button
                      onClick={() => setStrategy("carry_over")}
                      className={`
                        w-full text-right rounded-xl px-4 py-3 transition-all border
                        ${strategy === "carry_over" ? "ring-2" : ""}
                      `}
                      style={{
                        borderColor: strategy === "carry_over" ? colorLight.accent : colorLight.border,
                        backgroundColor: strategy === "carry_over" ? colorLight.accentSoft : colorLight.surface,
                      }}
                    >
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                        انتقال به امروز
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-[11px] mt-0.5" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                        تمام تسک‌های عقب‌افتاده به لیست امروز اضافه می‌شوند.
                      </div>
                    </button>

                    {/* Option 2: Catch Up Block */}
                    <button
                      onClick={() => setStrategy("catch_up")}
                      className={`
                        w-full text-right rounded-xl px-4 py-3 transition-all border
                        ${strategy === "catch_up" ? "ring-2" : ""}
                      `}
                      style={{
                        borderColor: strategy === "catch_up" ? colorLight.accent : colorLight.border,
                        backgroundColor: strategy === "catch_up" ? colorLight.accentSoft : colorLight.surface,
                      }}
                    >
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                        جلسه جبرانی
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-[11px] mt-0.5" style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }}>
                        یک بلوک زمانی متمرکز برای جبران تسک‌های عقب‌افتاده.
                      </div>
                    </button>

                    {/* Catch-up time picker */}
                    {strategy === "catch_up" && (
                      <motion.div
                        initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                        animate={{ height: "auto", opacity: 1 }}
                        className="overflow-hidden"
                      >
                        <div
                          className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg"
                          style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.surfaceSubtle }}
                        >
                          <label className="text-xs" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                            سقف زمانی:
                          </label>
                          <div className="flex gap-2">
                            {[30, 60, 90, 120].map((mins) => (
                              <button
                                key={mins}
                                onClick={() => setCatchUpMinutes(mins)}
                                className={`
                                  text-xs px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md transition-colors
                                `}
                                style={{
                                  backgroundColor:
                                    catchUpMinutes === mins ? colorLight.accent : "transparent",
                                  color:
                                    catchUpMinutes === mins ? "#fff" : colorLight.textMuted,
                                }}
                              >
                                {n(mins)} دقیقه
                              </button>
                            ))}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </motion.div>
                    )}

                    {/* Action Button */}
                    {strategy && (
                      <motion.div
                        initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
                        animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
                      >
                        <button
                          onClick={strategy === "carry_over" ? handleCarryOver : handleCatchUp}
                          disabled={isPending}
                          className="w-full py-3 rounded-xl text-sm font-semibold text-white
                                     transition-colors flex items-center justify-center gap-2"
                          style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accent }}
                        >
                          {isPending ? (
                            <Loader2 size={16} className="animate-spin" />
                          ) : (
                            <>
                              {strategy === "carry_over" ? "انتقال همه به امروز" : "ایجاد جلسه جبرانی"}
                              <ArrowLeft size={14} />
                            </>
                          )}
                        </button>
                      </motion.div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </>
              )}
            </Surface>
          </motion.div>
        </>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\planner\RescheduleDialog.tsx

"use client";

/**
 * RescheduleDialog — a simple modal to pick a new date for a task.
 *
 * Uses rescheduleTaskAction to move the task to the chosen date.
 */

import { useState, useTransition, useEffect } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import { X, Loader2, CalendarDays, ArrowLeft } from "lucide-react";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { Surface } from "@/components/ui/surface";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { rescheduleTaskAction } from "@/lib/actions/planner-actions";

interface RescheduleDialogProps {
  open: boolean;
  taskId: string | null;
  onClose: () => void;
  onDone?: () => void;
}

export function RescheduleDialog({ open, taskId, onClose, onDone }: RescheduleDialogProps) {
  const [targetDate, setTargetDate] = useState("");
  const [isPending, startTransition] = useTransition();

  // Reset the target date each time the dialog opens
  useEffect(() => {
    if (open) setTargetDate("");
  }, [open]);

  function handleSubmit() {
    if (!taskId || !targetDate) return;
    startTransition(async () => {
      const res = await rescheduleTaskAction(taskId, targetDate);
      if (res.ok) {
        toast.success("تسک به تاریخ جدید منتقل شد");
        onDone?.();
        onClose();
      } else {
        if (res.error.code === "NOT_FOUND") {
          toast.error("این تسک دیگر وجود ندارد");
          onClose();
          onDone?.();
        } else {
          toast.error(res.error.message);
        }
      }
    });
  }

  if (!open) return null;

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {open && (
        <>
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            onClick={onClose}
            className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/40"
          />
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            transition={{ type: "spring", damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
            className="fixed z-50 inset-x-4 bottom-4 top-auto max-w-sm mx-auto
                       sm:inset-auto sm:top-1/2 sm:left-1/2 sm:-translate-x-1/2 sm:-translate-y-1/2"
          >
            <Surface variant="elevated" padding="lg" className="rounded-2xl shadow-xl">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <CalendarDays size={18} style={{ color: colorLight.accent }} />
                  <h2 className="text-sm font-bold" style={{ color: colorLight.text }}>
                    تغییر تاریخ تسک
                  </h2>
                </div>
                <button
                  onClick={onClose}
                  className="p-1 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors"
                >
                  <X size={16} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
                </button>
              </div>

              <div className="mb-4">
                <label
                  className="text-xs font-medium mb-1.5 block"
                  style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
                >
                  تاریخ جدید
                </label>
                <input
                  type="date"
                  value={targetDate}
                  onChange={(e) => setTargetDate(e.target.value)}
                  min={new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10)}
                  className="w-full rounded-lg border px-3 py-2 text-sm"
                  style={{
                    borderColor: colorLight.border,
                    color: colorLight.text,
                    backgroundColor: colorLight.surface,
                  }}
                />
              </div>

              <button
                onClick={handleSubmit}
                disabled={!targetDate || isPending}
                className="w-full py-2.5 rounded-xl text-sm font-semibold text-white
                           transition-colors flex items-center justify-center gap-2
                           disabled:opacity-50"
                style={{ backgroundColor: colorLight.accent }}
              >
                {isPending ? (
                  <Loader2 size={16} className="animate-spin" />
                ) : (
                  <>
                    انتقال
                    <ArrowLeft size={14} />
                  </>
                )}
              </button>
            </Surface>
          </motion.div>
        </>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Task Type Routes (linked-content navigation)                       */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Get the best navigation route for a task type + linked entity.
 * Returns null when no sensible route exists.
 */
export function getTaskTypeRoute(
  taskType: string,
  linked?: {
    chapter?: { id: string } | null;
    chunk?: { id: string } | null;
    examSession?: { id: string } | null;
  },
): string | null {
  switch (taskType) {
    case "chapter_read":
    case "chunk_review":
      // QBank is the closest chapter-browsing page
      return "/qbank";
    case "question_block":
      return "/qbank";
    case "flashcard_review":
      return "/flashcards";
    case "notebook_review":
      return "/notebooks";
    case "exam_block":
      if (linked?.examSession?.id) return `/exam/${linked.examSession.id}`;
      return "/history";
    default:
      return null;
  }
}

  bg: string;
  dot: string;
} {

      return { text: "#9CA3AF", bg: "#F3F4F6", dot: "#9CA3AF" };

    case "snoozed":
      return { text: "#D97706", bg: "#FEF3C7", dot: "#D97706" };

const PERSIAN_DOW: Record<string, string> = {
  saturday: "شنبه",
  sunday: "یک‌شنبه",
  monday: "دوشنبه",
  tuesday: "سه‌شنبه",
  wednesday: "چهارشنبه",
  thursday: "پنج‌شنبه",
  friday: "جمعه",
};

const PERSIAN_DOW_SHORT: Record<string, string> = {
  saturday: "ش",
  sunday: "ی",
  monday: "د",
  tuesday: "س",
  wednesday: "چ",
  thursday: "پ",
  friday: "ج",
};

export function getDowLabel(dow: string, short = false): string {
  return short
    ? PERSIAN_DOW_SHORT[dow] ?? dow
    : PERSIAN_DOW[dow] ?? dow;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Date formatting                                                    */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

const dateFmt = new Intl.DateTimeFormat("fa-IR", {
  day: "numeric",
  month: "long",
});

const dateShortFmt = new Intl.DateTimeFormat("fa-IR", {
  day: "numeric",
  month: "short",
});

export function formatPersianDate(isoDate: string): string {
  try {
    return dateFmt.format(new Date(isoDate + "T00:00:00"));
  } catch {
    return isoDate;
  }
}

export function formatPersianDateShort(isoDate: string): string {
  try {
    return dateShortFmt.format(new Date(isoDate + "T00:00:00"));
  } catch {
    return isoDate;
  }
}

export function isToday(isoDate: string): boolean {
  const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
  return isoDate === today;
}

/**
 * Returns a relative date label: "امروز"/"دیروز"/"فردا" or a formatted date.
 */
export function formatRelativeDate(isoDate: string): string {
  const today = new Date();
  const todayStr = today.toISOString().slice(0, 10);

  if (isoDate === todayStr) return "امروز";

  const yesterday = new Date(today);
  yesterday.setDate(today.getDate() - 1);
  if (isoDate === yesterday.toISOString().slice(0, 10)) return "دیروز";

  const tomorrow = new Date(today);
  tomorrow.setDate(today.getDate() + 1);
  if (isoDate === tomorrow.toISOString().slice(0, 10)) return "فردا";

  return formatPersianDate(isoDate);
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Duration formatting                                                */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function formatMinutes(minutes: number): string {
  if (minutes < 1) return "کمتر از ۱ دقیقه";
  if (minutes < 60) return `${n(minutes)} دقیقه`;
  const h = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
  const m = minutes % 60;
  if (m === 0) return `${n(h)} ساعت`;
  return `${n(h)} ساعت و ${n(m)} دقیقه`;
}

/**
 * Format elapsed time since a unix-ms timestamp.
 */
export function formatElapsed(startedAtMs: number | null | undefined): string | null {
  if (!startedAtMs) return null;
  const elapsed = Math.max(0, Date.now() - startedAtMs);
  const mins = Math.floor(elapsed / 60000);
  if (mins < 1) return "همین الان";
  return `${formatMinutes(mins)} گذشته`;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Hooks: useVisibilityRefresh                                        */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

import { useEffect, useRef } from "react";

/**
 * Re-invoke `callback` whenever the tab/window regains focus.
 * Debounced to avoid rapid re-fires (min 5s gap).
 */
export function useVisibilityRefresh(callback: () => void, enabled = true) {
  const lastRefresh = useRef(Date.now());

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!enabled) return;

    function handleVisibility() {
      if (document.visibilityState === "visible") {
        const now = Date.now();
        if (now - lastRefresh.current > 5000) {
          lastRefresh.current = now;
          callback();
        }
      }
    }

    document.addEventListener("visibilitychange", handleVisibility);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("visibilitychange", handleVisibility);
  }, [callback, enabled]);
}

"use client";

/**
 * PlannerDndContext — Wraps the planner layout in a DndContext from @dnd-kit.
 *
 * Handles drag-start (show overlay) and drag-end (reschedule task to new date).
 * Strict typing for drag/drop payloads via DragTaskData / DropCalendarData.
 */

import { useState, useCallback, type ReactNode } from "react";
import {
  DndContext,
  DragOverlay,
  useSensor,
  useSensors,
  PointerSensor,
  KeyboardSensor,
  type DragStartEvent,
  type DragEndEvent,
} from "@dnd-kit/core";
import { GripVertical } from "lucide-react";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";
import { getTaskTypeLabel, getTaskTypeColor } from "../task-helpers";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/* Shared drag-drop payload types                                      */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface DragTaskData {
  type: "task";
  taskId: string;
  sourceDate?: string | null;
  sourceBucket?: string;
  taskTitle: string;
  taskType: string;
}

export interface DropCalendarData {
  type: "calendar-day";
  /** Gregorian ISO date string, e.g. "2026-03-07" */
  targetDate: string;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/* Props                                                               */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

interface PlannerDndContextProps {
  children: ReactNode;
  onTaskReschedule: (taskId: string, targetDate: string) => void;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/* Drag overlay card (minimal preview shown while dragging)            */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function DragOverlayCard({
  title,
  taskType,
}: {
  title: string;
  taskType: string;
}) {
  const typeColor = getTaskTypeColor(taskType);
  return (
    <div
      className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-xl shadow-xl border max-w-[260px]"
      style={{
        backgroundColor: "#fff",
        borderColor: colorLight.border,
        transform: "rotate(2deg)",
        opacity: 0.92,
      }}
    >
      <GripVertical size={14} style={{ color: colorLight.textMuted }} />
      <span
        className="inline-flex items-center text-[10px] font-semibold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full"
        style={{ color: typeColor.text, backgroundColor: typeColor.bg }}
      >
        {getTaskTypeLabel(taskType)}
      </span>
      <span
        className="text-sm font-medium truncate"
        style={{ color: colorLight.text }}
      >
        {title}
      </span>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/* Context provider                                                    */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function PlannerDndContext({
  children,
  onTaskReschedule,
}: PlannerDndContextProps) {
  const [activeTask, setActiveTask] = useState<{
    title: string;
    taskType: string;
  } | null>(null);

  const sensors = useSensors(
    useSensor(PointerSensor, { activationConstraint: { distance: 8 } }),
    useSensor(KeyboardSensor),
  );

  const handleDragStart = useCallback((event: DragStartEvent) => {
    const data = event.active.data.current as DragTaskData | undefined;
    if (data?.type === "task") {
      setActiveTask({ title: data.taskTitle, taskType: data.taskType });
    }
  }, []);

  const handleDragEnd = useCallback(
    (event: DragEndEvent) => {
      setActiveTask(null);

      const { active, over } = event;
      if (!over) return;

      const dragData = active.data.current as DragTaskData | undefined;
      const dropData = over.data.current as DropCalendarData | undefined;

      if (dragData?.type !== "task" || dropData?.type !== "calendar-day") return;
      if (!dragData.taskId || !dropData.targetDate) return;

      onTaskReschedule(dragData.taskId, dropData.targetDate);
    },
    [onTaskReschedule],
  );

  return (
    <DndContext
      sensors={sensors}
      onDragStart={handleDragStart}
      onDragEnd={handleDragEnd}
    >
      {children}
      <DragOverlay dropAnimation={{ duration: 200, easing: "ease" }}>
        {activeTask ? (
          <DragOverlayCard
            title={activeTask.title}
            taskType={activeTask.taskType}
          />
        ) : null}
      </DragOverlay>
    </DndContext>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\planner\ui\ProgressRing.tsx

"use client";

/**
 * ProgressRing — Animated SVG circular progress indicator.
 *
 * Uses framer-motion to smoothly animate stroke-dashoffset when value changes.
 * Designed for the PlannerSummary component.
 */

import { motion } from "framer-motion";
import { colorLight } from "@/lib/theme/tokens";

interface ProgressRingProps {
  /** Progress percentage 0–100. */
  value: number;
  /** Diameter in px. Default 40. */
  size?: number;
  /** Stroke width in px. Default 3.5. */
  strokeWidth?: number;
  /** Track (background) color. */
  trackColor?: string;
  /** Active arc color. Defaults to accent or success when ≥100. */
  activeColor?: string;
  /** Optional label rendered in the center (e.g. "۷۵٪"). */
  label?: string;
}

export function ProgressRing({
  value,
  size = 40,
  strokeWidth = 3.5,
  trackColor = colorLight.border,
  activeColor,
  label,
}: ProgressRingProps) {
  const radius = (size - strokeWidth) / 2;
  const circumference = 2 * Math.PI * radius;
  const clamped = Math.min(100, Math.max(0, value));
  const offset = circumference - (clamped / 100) * circumference;

  const color =
    activeColor ?? (clamped >= 100 ? colorLight.success : colorLight.accent);

  return (
    <div
      className="relative flex-shrink-0"
      style={{ width: size, height: size }}
    >
      <svg
        width={size}
        height={size}
        viewBox={`0 0 ${size} ${size}`}
        className="block -rotate-90"
      >
        {/* Track */}
        <circle
          cx={size / 2}
          cy={size / 2}
          r={radius}
          fill="none"
          stroke={trackColor}
          strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
        />
        {/* Active arc */}
        <motion.circle
          cx={size / 2}
          cy={size / 2}
          r={radius}
          fill="none"
          stroke={color}
          strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
          strokeLinecap="round"
          strokeDasharray={circumference}
          initial={{ strokeDashoffset: circumference }}
          animate={{ strokeDashoffset: offset }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.25, ease: "easeOut" }}
        />
      </svg>
      {label && (
        <span
          className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center text-[9px] font-bold tabular-nums"
          style={{ color }}
        >
          {label}
        </span>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

"use client"

import { useState } from 'react'
import { ChevronRight, ChevronLeft } from 'lucide-react'
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'
import { 
  addMonths, 
  subMonths, 
  formatPersianMonth,
  toPersianNum 
} from '@/lib/utils/persian-calendar'
import { PlannerCalendarGrid } from './PlannerCalendarGrid'
import type { CalendarTask } from './CalendarDayCell'
import type { DailyStats } from '@/lib/planner/types'

interface PlannerCalendarProps {
  tasks: CalendarTask[]
  dailyStats: Record<string, DailyStats> // keyed by 'yyyy-MM-dd'
  onDayClick?: (date: Date) => void
  onTaskClick?: (task: CalendarTask) => void
}

export function PlannerCalendar({ 
  tasks, 
  dailyStats,
  onDayClick,
  onTaskClick 
}: PlannerCalendarProps) {
  const [currentMonth, setCurrentMonth] = useState(new Date())
  
  const goToPrevMonth = () => setCurrentMonth(prev => subMonths(prev, 1))
  const goToNextMonth = () => setCurrentMonth(prev => addMonths(prev, 1))
  const goToToday = () => setCurrentMonth(new Date())

  return (
    <div className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-200 bg-gray-50/50">
        {/* Navigation - Right side for RTL */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            onClick={goToNextMonth}
            className="h-8 w-8 hover:bg-gray-100"
          >
            <ChevronRight className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            onClick={goToPrevMonth}
            className="h-8 w-8 hover:bg-gray-100"
          >
            <ChevronLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>

        {/* Month/Year Title */}
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">
          {formatPersianMonth(currentMonth)}
        </h2>

        {/* Today Button */}
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="sm"
          onClick={goToToday}
          className="text-xs h-7 px-3"
        >
          امروز
        </Button>
      </div>

      {/* Calendar Grid */}
      <PlannerCalendarGrid
        month={currentMonth}
        tasks={tasks}
        dailyStats={dailyStats}
        onDayClick={onDayClick}
        onTaskClick={onTaskClick}
      />
    </div>
  )
}

FILE: src\components\planner\calendar\PlannerCalendarGrid.tsx

"use client"

import { useMemo } from 'react'
import { formatJalali } from '@/lib/utils/persian-calendar'
import { 
  getCalendarDays, 
  isSameMonth, 
  PERSIAN_WEEKDAYS 
} from '@/lib/utils/persian-calendar'
import { CalendarDayCell, type CalendarTask } from './CalendarDayCell'
import type { DailyStats } from '@/lib/planner/types'

interface PlannerCalendarGridProps {
  month: Date
  tasks: CalendarTask[]
  dailyStats: Record<string, DailyStats>
  onDayClick?: (date: Date) => void
  onTaskClick?: (task: CalendarTask) => void
}

export function PlannerCalendarGrid({
  month,
  tasks,
  dailyStats,
  onDayClick,
  onTaskClick,
}: PlannerCalendarGridProps) {
  const days = useMemo(() => getCalendarDays(month), [month])

  const tasksByDate = useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map<string, CalendarTask[]>()
    tasks.forEach(task => {
      if (task.scheduledFor) {
        const key = formatJalali(new Date(task.scheduledFor), 'yyyy-MM-dd')
        const existing = map.get(key) || []
        map.set(key, [...existing, task])
      }
    })
    return map
  }, [tasks])

  return (
    <div dir="rtl">
      {/* Weekday Headers */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-7 border-b border-gray-200 bg-gray-50">
        {PERSIAN_WEEKDAYS.map((day, index) => (
          <div
            key={day}
            className={`
              py-2 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500
              ${index === 6 ? 'text-red-500' : ''} 
            `}
          >
            {day}
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Days Grid */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-7 bg-gray-200 gap-px">
        {days.map((date) => {
          const dateKey = formatJalali(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd')
          const dayTasks = tasksByDate.get(dateKey) || []
          const stats = dailyStats[dateKey]

          return (
            <CalendarDayCell
              key={dateKey}
              date={date}
              tasks={dayTasks}
              stats={stats}
              isCurrentMonth={isSameMonth(date, month)}
              onDayClick={onDayClick}
              onTaskClick={onTaskClick}
            />
          )
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

"use client"

import { useMemo } from 'react'
import { useDroppable } from '@dnd-kit/core'
import { isToday, isBefore, startOfDay } from 'date-fns-jalali'
import { toPersianNum, formatPersianDay } from '@/lib/utils/persian-calendar'
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
import type { DropCalendarData } from '../dnd/PlannerDndContext'

/** Minimal task shape for calendar rendering — compatible with BucketTask. */
export interface CalendarTask {
  id: string
  title: string
  status: string
  taskType: string
  sourceType?: string | null
  scheduledFor?: string | null
}

interface CalendarDayCellProps {
  date: Date
  tasks: CalendarTask[]
  stats?: { targetMinutes: number; completedMinutes: number }
  isCurrentMonth: boolean
  onDayClick?: (date: Date) => void
  onTaskClick?: (task: CalendarTask) => void
}

// UWorld color mapping
const TASK_TYPE_COLORS = {
  flashcard_review: 'bg-blue-500',
  question_practice: 'bg-emerald-500',
  weak_area_review: 'bg-amber-500',
  concept_study: 'bg-purple-500',
  custom: 'bg-gray-500',
} as const

const SOURCE_TYPE_COLORS = {
  fsrs: 'bg-blue-500',
  weak_area: 'bg-amber-500',
  question_block: 'bg-emerald-500',
  notebook: 'bg-purple-500',
  manual: 'bg-gray-500',
} as const

export function CalendarDayCell({
  date,
  tasks,
  stats,
  isCurrentMonth,
  onDayClick,
  onTaskClick,
}: CalendarDayCellProps) {
  /* ---- Droppable ---- */
  const dateKey = date.toISOString().split('T')[0]
  const dropData: DropCalendarData = { type: 'calendar-day', targetDate: dateKey }
  const { setNodeRef: dropRef, isOver } = useDroppable({
    id: `calendar-day-${dateKey}`,
    data: dropData,
  })

  const today = isToday(date)
  const isPast = isBefore(date, startOfDay(new Date())) && !today
  const isFriday = date.getDay() === 5 // جمعه

  const hasOverdue = useMemo(() => {
    return isPast && tasks.some(t => t.status === 'pending')
  }, [isPast, tasks])

  const completedCount = tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'completed').length
  const totalCount = tasks.length
  const allCompleted = totalCount > 0 && completedCount === totalCount

  const progress = stats 
    ? Math.min((stats.completedMinutes / stats.targetMinutes) * 100, 100)
    : 0

  // Get unique task type dots (max 4)
  const taskDots = useMemo(() => {
    const types = new Set(tasks.map(t => t.sourceType))
    return Array.from(types).slice(0, 4)
  }, [tasks])

  return (
    <div
      ref={dropRef}
      onClick={() => onDayClick?.(date)}
      className={cn(
        'min-h-[100px] p-2 bg-white cursor-pointer transition-all duration-150 relative',
        'hover:bg-gray-50 hover:shadow-sm',
        'flex flex-col',
        // Not current month
        !isCurrentMonth && 'bg-gray-50 opacity-40',
        // Today highlight (UWorld blue border)
        today && 'ring-2 ring-inset ring-blue-500 bg-blue-50/30',
        // Has overdue tasks
        hasOverdue && 'bg-red-50/50',
        // All completed
        allCompleted && 'bg-emerald-50/30',
        // Drop target highlight
        isOver && 'ring-2 ring-inset ring-teal-400 bg-teal-50/60',
      )}
    >
      {/* Top Row: Date + Task Dots */}
      <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-1">
        {/* Date Number */}
        <span
          className={cn(
            'text-sm font-medium leading-none',
            today && 'text-blue-600 font-semibold',
            !isCurrentMonth && 'text-gray-400',
            isFriday && isCurrentMonth && 'text-red-500',
            hasOverdue && 'text-red-600',
          )}
        >
          {toPersianNum(parseInt(formatPersianDay(date)))}
        </span>

        {/* Task Type Dots */}
        <div className="flex gap-0.5">
          {taskDots.map((type, i) => (
            <div
              key={i}
              className={cn(
                'w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full',
                SOURCE_TYPE_COLORS[type as keyof typeof SOURCE_TYPE_COLORS] || 'bg-gray-400'
              )}
            />
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Task Previews (max 2) */}
      <div className="flex-1 space-y-0.5 overflow-hidden">
        {tasks.slice(0, 2).map((task) => (
          <div
            key={task.id}
            onClick={(e) => {
              e.stopPropagation()
              onTaskClick?.(task)
            }}
            className={cn(
              'text-[10px] leading-tight truncate px-1 py-0.5 rounded',
              'hover:bg-gray-100 cursor-pointer transition-colors',
              task.status === 'completed' && 'line-through text-gray-400',
            )}
          >
            <span
              className={cn(
                'inline-block w-1 h-1 rounded-full mr-1 align-middle',
                TASK_TYPE_COLORS[task.taskType as keyof typeof TASK_TYPE_COLORS] || 'bg-gray-400'
              )}
            />
            {task.title}
          </div>
        ))}

        {tasks.length > 2 && (
          <div className="text-[10px] text-gray-400 px-1">
            +{toPersianNum(tasks.length - 2)} مورد دیگر
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Bottom: Progress Bar */}
      {stats && stats.targetMinutes > 0 && (
        <div className="mt-auto pt-1">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
            <div className="flex-1 h-1 bg-gray-200 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
              <div
                className={cn(
                  'h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-300',
                  progress >= 100 ? 'bg-emerald-500' : 'bg-blue-500'
                )}
                style={{ width: `${progress}%` }}
              />
            </div>
            <span className="text-[9px] text-gray-400 tabular-nums">
              {toPersianNum(stats.completedMinutes)}/{toPersianNum(stats.targetMinutes)}
            </span>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Completion Indicator */}
      {allCompleted && totalCount > 0 && (
        <div className="absolute top-1 left-1">
          <div className="w-3 h-3 bg-emerald-500 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <svg className="w-2 h-2 text-white" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor">
              <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" strokeWidth={3} d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" />
            </svg>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

"use client"

import { formatPersianDate, toPersianNum } from '@/lib/utils/persian-calendar'
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
} from '@/components/ui/dialog'
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'
import { Plus, CheckCircle2 } from 'lucide-react'
import { PlannerTaskCard } from '../PlannerTaskCard'
import type { CalendarTask } from './CalendarDayCell'
import type { DailyStats } from '@/lib/planner/types'

/** Map a CalendarTask to the minimal shape PlannerTaskCard expects. */
function toCardTask(t: CalendarTask) {
  return {
    id: t.id,
    taskType: t.taskType,
    status: t.status,
    title: t.title,
    description: null as string | null,
    estimatedMinutes: 0,
    priority: 0,
    sourceType: t.sourceType ?? null,
    scheduledFor: t.scheduledFor ?? null,
  };
}

interface CalendarDayModalProps {
  open: boolean
  onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void
  date: Date
  tasks: CalendarTask[]
  stats?: DailyStats
  onAddTask?: () => void
  onCompleteAll?: () => void
}

export function CalendarDayModal({
  open,
  onOpenChange,
  date,
  tasks,
  stats,
  onAddTask,
  onCompleteAll,
}: CalendarDayModalProps) {
  const pendingTasks = tasks.filter(t => t.status !== 'completed')
  const completedTasks = tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'completed')

  return (
    <Dialog open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
      <DialogContent className="max-w-lg" dir="rtl">
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle className="text-right">
            {formatPersianDate(date)}
          </DialogTitle>
        </DialogHeader>

        {/* Stats Summary */}
        {stats && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-4 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg text-sm">
            <div>
              <span className="text-gray-500">تکمیل شده: </span>
              <span className="font-medium">
                {toPersianNum(stats.completedMinutes)} از {toPersianNum(stats.targetMinutes)} دقیقه
              </span>
            </div>
            <div>
              <span className="text-gray-500">تسک‌ها: </span>
              <span className="font-medium">
                {toPersianNum(completedTasks.length)} از {toPersianNum(tasks.length)}
              </span>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Actions */}
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            size="sm"
            onClick={onAddTask}
            className="flex-1"
          >
            <Plus className="w-4 h-4 ml-1" />
            افزودن تسک
          </Button>
          {pendingTasks.length > 0 && (
            <Button
              variant="outline"
              size="sm"
              onClick={onCompleteAll}
              className="flex-1"
            >
              <CheckCircle2 className="w-4 h-4 ml-1" />
              تکمیل همه
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Task Lists */}
        <div className="space-y-4 max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto">
          {/* Pending Tasks */}
          {pendingTasks.length > 0 && (
            <div>
              <h4 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">
                در انتظار ({toPersianNum(pendingTasks.length)})
              </h4>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                {pendingTasks.map(task => (
                  <PlannerTaskCard key={task.id} task={toCardTask(task)} bucket="today" />
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Completed Tasks */}
          {completedTasks.length > 0 && (
            <div>
              <h4 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-400 mb-2">
                تکمیل شده ({toPersianNum(completedTasks.length)})
              </h4>
              <div className="space-y-2 opacity-60">
                {completedTasks.map(task => (
                  <PlannerTaskCard key={task.id} task={toCardTask(task)} bucket="completed" />
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Empty State */}
          {tasks.length === 0 && (
            <div className="text-center py-8 text-gray-400">
              <p>هیچ تسکی برای این روز وجود ندارد</p>
              <Button
                variant="link"
                onClick={onAddTask}
                className="mt-2"
              >
                اولین تسک را اضافه کنید
              </Button>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  )
}

FILE: src\app\api\planner\_shared.ts

/**
 * Shared API response helpers for planner endpoints.
 */
import { NextResponse } from "next/server";

/** Build a success JSON response. */
export function ok<T>(data: T, status = 200) {
  return NextResponse.json({ ok: true, data }, { status });
}

/** Build a validation error response. */
export function validationError(message: string) {
  return NextResponse.json(
    { ok: false, error: { code: "VALIDATION_ERROR", message } },
    { status: 400 },
  );
}

/** Build a not-found error response. */
export function notFound(message: string) {
  return NextResponse.json(
    { ok: false, error: { code: "NOT_FOUND", message } },
    { status: 404 },
  );
}

/** Build an error response from a service-thrown error. */
export function fromServiceError(err: unknown) {
  if (err instanceof Error) {
    const msg = err.message;

    // Infer HTTP status from common error message patterns
    if (msg.includes("not found")) {
      return notFound(msg);
    }
    if (
      msg.includes("already") ||
      msg.includes("cannot be") ||
      msg.includes("Cannot move")
    ) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { ok: false, error: { code: "INVALID_STATE", message: msg } },
        { status: 409 },
      );
    }
    if (msg.includes("No valid chapters") || msg.includes("No overdue")) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { ok: false, error: { code: "PRECONDITION_FAILED", message: msg } },
        { status: 422 },
      );
    }
    if (msg.includes("No active plan")) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { ok: false, error: { code: "NO_ACTIVE_PLAN", message: msg } },
        { status: 404 },
      );
    }
  }

  console.error("[planner-api]", err);
  return NextResponse.json(
    {
      ok: false,
      error: { code: "INTERNAL_ERROR", message: "An internal error occurred." },
    },
    { status: 500 },
  );
}

/**
 * GET /api/planner/today
 *
 * Returns today's plan: active plan, today's day record, tasks with
 * resolved content links, overdue tasks, and planner settings.
 */
import { type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { getTodayPlan, detectAndMarkOverdue } from "@/lib/services/planner-service";
import { ok, fromServiceError, notFound } from "@/app/api/planner/_shared";

export async function GET(_req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    // Auto-detect overdue tasks on dashboard load
    detectAndMarkOverdue();

    const result = getTodayPlan();
    if (!result) {
      return notFound("No active study plan found.");
    }
    return ok(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return fromServiceError(err);
  }
}

FILE: src\app\api\planner\week\route.ts
====================================================================================================

/**
 * GET /api/planner/week?ref=YYYY-MM-DD
 *
 * Returns the full week view (Saturday–Friday) around a reference date.
 * Defaults to the current week if no `ref` query param is provided.
 */
import { type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { getWeekPlan, detectAndMarkOverdue } from "@/lib/services/planner-service";
import { ok, fromServiceError, notFound, validationError } from "@/app/api/planner/_shared";

export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    detectAndMarkOverdue();

    const refParam = req.nextUrl.searchParams.get("ref");
    let refDate: Date | undefined;

    if (refParam) {
      // Validate ISO date format
      if (!/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(refParam)) {
        return validationError("ref must be a valid ISO date (YYYY-MM-DD).");
      }
      const parsed = new Date(refParam + "T00:00:00");
      if (isNaN(parsed.getTime())) {
        return validationError("ref is not a valid date.");
      }
      refDate = parsed;
    }

    const result = getWeekPlan(refDate);
    if (!result) {
      return notFound("No active study plan found.");
    }
    return ok(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return fromServiceError(err);
  }
}

FILE: src\app\api\planner\overdue\route.ts
====================================================================================================

/**
 * GET  /api/planner/overdue — List overdue tasks with resolved links.
 * POST /api/planner/overdue — Carry over overdue tasks to a target date.
 */
import { type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import {
  getOverdueTasks,
  carryOverOverdueTasks,
  createCatchUpBlock,
} from "@/lib/services/planner-service";
import { ok, fromServiceError, validationError } from "@/app/api/planner/_shared";

/**
 * GET /api/planner/overdue
 *
 * Returns all overdue tasks in the active plan with resolved content links.
 */
export async function GET(_req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const tasks = getOverdueTasks();
    return ok(tasks);
  } catch (err) {
    return fromServiceError(err);
  }
}

/**
 * POST /api/planner/overdue
 *
 * Body: {
 *   action: "carry_over" | "catch_up",
 *   targetDate?: string,     // ISO date — defaults to today
 *   maxMinutes?: number       // only for "catch_up"
 * }
 */
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    const action = body.action;

    if (!action || !["carry_over", "catch_up"].includes(action)) {
      return validationError('action is required and must be "carry_over" or "catch_up".');
    }

    // Validate optional targetDate
    if (body.targetDate && !/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(body.targetDate)) {
      return validationError("targetDate must be a valid ISO date (YYYY-MM-DD).");
    }

    if (action === "carry_over") {
      const result = carryOverOverdueTasks(body.targetDate);
      return ok(result);
    }

    // catch_up
    const date = body.targetDate ?? new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
    if (body.maxMinutes !== undefined && (typeof body.maxMinutes !== "number" || body.maxMinutes < 1)) {
      return validationError("maxMinutes must be a positive number.");
    }
    const result = createCatchUpBlock(date, body.maxMinutes);
    return ok(result, 201);
  } catch (err) {
    return fromServiceError(err);
  }
}

/**
 * POST /api/planner/tasks/[id]/complete
 *
 * Mark a task as completed.
 *
 * Body: {
 *   actualMinutes?: number,
 *   resultJson?: Record<string, unknown>
 * }
 */
import { type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { markTaskComplete } from "@/lib/services/planner-service";
import { ok, fromServiceError, validationError } from "@/app/api/planner/_shared";

export async function POST(
  req: NextRequest,
  { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> },
) {
  try {
    const { id } = await params;
    if (!id) return validationError("Task ID is required.");

    const body = await req.json().catch(() => ({}));

    if (body.actualMinutes !== undefined && typeof body.actualMinutes !== "number") {
      return validationError("actualMinutes must be a number.");
    }

    const task = markTaskComplete(id, body.actualMinutes, body.resultJson);
    return ok(task);
  } catch (err) {
    return fromServiceError(err);
  }
}

/**
 * POST /api/planner/tasks/[id]/move
 *
 * Move a task to a different day within the same plan.
 *
 * Body: {
 *   targetDayId: string,
 *   sortOrder?: number
 * }
 */
import { type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { moveTask } from "@/lib/services/planner-service";
import { ok, fromServiceError, validationError } from "@/app/api/planner/_shared";

export async function POST(
  req: NextRequest,
  { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> },
) {
  try {
    const { id } = await params;
    if (!id) return validationError("Task ID is required.");

    const body = await req.json();

    if (!body.targetDayId || typeof body.targetDayId !== "string") {
      return validationError("targetDayId is required and must be a string.");
    }
    if (body.sortOrder !== undefined && typeof body.sortOrder !== "number") {
      return validationError("sortOrder must be a number.");
    }

    const result = moveTask(id, body.targetDayId, body.sortOrder);
    return ok(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return fromServiceError(err);
  }
}

/**
 * POST /api/planner/tasks/[id]/reschedule
 *
 * Reschedule a task to a different date. Creates a copy on the target
 * day and marks the original as rescheduled.
 *
 * Body: {
 *   targetDate: string   // ISO date YYYY-MM-DD
 * }
 */
import { type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { rescheduleTask } from "@/lib/services/planner-service";
import { ok, fromServiceError, validationError } from "@/app/api/planner/_shared";

export async function POST(
  req: NextRequest,
  { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> },
) {
  try {
    const { id } = await params;
    if (!id) return validationError("Task ID is required.");

    const body = await req.json();

    if (!body.targetDate || typeof body.targetDate !== "string") {
      return validationError("targetDate is required.");
    }
    if (!/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(body.targetDate)) {
      return validationError("targetDate must be a valid ISO date (YYYY-MM-DD).");
    }

    const task = rescheduleTask(id, body.targetDate);
    return ok(task);
  } catch (err) {
    return fromServiceError(err);
  }
}

FILE: src\lib\actions\planner-actions.ts

"use server";

/**
 * Server Actions for the study planner.
 *
 * Thin wrappers over the planner service layer. Each action validates
 * inputs and returns a consistent { ok, data?, error? } shape.
 *
 * Use these from React Server Components, forms, and client components
 * that call server actions directly.
 */
import {
  // Plan generation
  generateWeeklyPlan,
  generateDailyPlan,
  // Task lifecycle
  markTaskComplete,
  markTaskSkipped,
  startTaskWork,
  moveTask,
  rescheduleTask,
  updateTaskProgress,
  addTaskNote,
  // Overdue handling
  carryOverOverdueTasks,
  createCatchUpBlock,
  detectAndMarkOverdue,
  // Progress
  recalculatePlannerProgress,
  endOfDayRoutine,
  // Plan management
  activatePlan,
  pausePlan,
  completePlan,
  archivePlan,
  removePlan,
  // Settings
  updatePlannerSettings,
  // Task CRUD
  createManualTask,
  removeTask,
  reorderTasks,
  // Reads
  getTodayPlan,
  getWeekPlan,
  getOverdueTasks,
  getUpcomingTasks,
  getPlannerSummary,
  getTasksForDate,
  getTaskByIdResolved,
  getActivePlan,
  listPlans,
  getSettings,
  // Types
  type CreatePlanParams,
  type TaskLinkBlueprint,
} from "@/lib/services/planner-service";

import type {
  TaskTypeValue,
} from "@/lib/db/queries/planner";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Result type                                                        */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

type ActionResult<T> =
  | { ok: true; data: T }
  | { ok: false; error: { code: string; message: string } };

function succeed<T>(data: T): ActionResult<T> {
  return { ok: true, data };
}

function fail(code: string, message: string): ActionResult<never> {
  return { ok: false, error: { code, message } };
}

function handleError(err: unknown): ActionResult<never> {
  if (err instanceof Error) {
    const msg = err.message;
    if (msg.includes("not found")) return fail("NOT_FOUND", msg);
    if (msg.includes("already") || msg.includes("cannot be") || msg.includes("Cannot move")) {
      return fail("INVALID_STATE", msg);
    }
    if (msg.includes("No active plan")) return fail("NO_ACTIVE_PLAN", msg);
    return fail("SERVICE_ERROR", msg);
  }
  console.error("[planner-actions]", err);
  return fail("INTERNAL_ERROR", "An unexpected error occurred.");
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  READ ACTIONS                                                       */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Get today's planner dashboard data. */
export async function getTodayPlanAction() {
  try {
    detectAndMarkOverdue();
    const result = getTodayPlan();
    if (!result) return fail("NO_ACTIVE_PLAN", "No active study plan found.");
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Get the week view. */
export async function getWeekPlanAction(refDate?: string) {
  try {
    detectAndMarkOverdue();
    const ref = refDate ? new Date(refDate + "T00:00:00") : undefined;
    const result = getWeekPlan(ref);
    if (!result) return fail("NO_ACTIVE_PLAN", "No active study plan found.");
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Get overdue tasks. */
export async function getOverdueTasksAction() {
  try {
    const tasks = getOverdueTasks();
    return succeed(tasks);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Get upcoming tasks. */
export async function getUpcomingTasksAction(limit?: number) {
  try {
    const tasks = getUpcomingTasks(limit);
    return succeed(tasks);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Get the planner summary (dashboard overview widget). */
export async function getPlannerSummaryAction() {
  try {
    detectAndMarkOverdue();
    const summary = getPlannerSummary();
    return succeed(summary);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Get tasks for a specific date. */
export async function getTasksForDateAction(date: string) {
  try {
    if (!date || !/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(date)) {
      return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "date must be a valid ISO date (YYYY-MM-DD).");
    }
    const result = getTasksForDate(date);
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Get a single task with full context. */
export async function getTaskAction(taskId: string) {
  try {
    if (!taskId) return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "taskId is required.");
    const result = getTaskByIdResolved(taskId);
    if (!result) return fail("NOT_FOUND", `Task ${taskId} not found.`);
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** List all plans. */
export async function listPlansAction() {
  try {
    const plans = listPlans();
    return succeed(plans);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Get planner settings. */
export async function getSettingsAction() {
  try {
    const settings = getSettings();
    return succeed(settings ?? null);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  PLAN GENERATION ACTIONS                                            */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Generate a full weekly study plan. */
export async function generateWeeklyPlanAction(params: CreatePlanParams) {
  try {
    if (!params.title?.trim()) {
      return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "title is required.");
    }
    if (!params.startDate || !/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(params.startDate)) {
      return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "startDate must be a valid ISO date (YYYY-MM-DD).");
    }
    if (!Array.isArray(params.chapterIds) || params.chapterIds.length === 0) {
      return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "chapterIds must be a non-empty array.");
    }
    if (params.endDate && !/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(params.endDate)) {
      return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "endDate must be a valid ISO date (YYYY-MM-DD).");
    }

    const result = generateWeeklyPlan(params);
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Generate a single day's plan on the fly. */
export async function generateDailyPlanAction(
  planId: string,
  date: string,
  chapterIds?: string[],
) {
  try {
    if (!planId) return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "planId is required.");
    if (!date || !/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(date)) {
      return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "date must be a valid ISO date (YYYY-MM-DD).");
    }

    const result = generateDailyPlan(planId, date, chapterIds);
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Create a focused catch-up block from overdue tasks. */
export async function createCatchUpAction(date: string, maxMinutes?: number) {
  try {
    if (!date || !/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(date)) {
      return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "date must be a valid ISO date (YYYY-MM-DD).");
    }
    if (maxMinutes !== undefined && (typeof maxMinutes !== "number" || maxMinutes < 1)) {
      return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "maxMinutes must be a positive number.");
    }
    const result = createCatchUpBlock(date, maxMinutes);
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

      return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "taskIds must be a non-empty array.");

/* ================================================================== */
/*  SNOOZE / MOVE-TO-TODAY ACTIONS                                     */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Snooze a task by N days from today.
 * This is a convenience wrapper over rescheduleTask.
 */
export async function snoozeTaskAction(taskId: string, days: number = 1) {
  try {
    if (!taskId) return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "taskId is required.");
    if (days < 1 || days > 30) return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "days must be between 1 and 30.");
    const target = new Date();
    target.setDate(target.getDate() + days);
    const targetDate = target.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
    const task = rescheduleTask(taskId, targetDate);
    return succeed(task);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/**
 * Move a task to today by rescheduling it to today's date.
 */
export async function moveToTodayAction(taskId: string) {
  try {
    if (!taskId) return fail("VALIDATION_ERROR", "taskId is required.");
    const todayStr = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
    const task = rescheduleTask(taskId, todayStr);
    return succeed(task);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

"use server";

/**
 * Server Actions for the planner recommendation engine.
 *
 * Exposes recommendation retrieval and acceptance to the client.
 * Uses the same ActionResult pattern as planner-actions.ts.
 */

import {
  getRecommendations,
  acceptRecommendation,
  getRecommendationCount,
  type RecommendationResult,
  type Recommendation,
} from "@/lib/services/planner-recommendation-service";

import {
  getStudyIntelligence,
  generateSmartWeeklyPlan,
  generateExamRecovery,
  type CreatePlanParams,
  type SmartPlanResult,
  type ExamRecoveryResult,
} from "@/lib/services/planner-service";

import type { OrchestratorIntelligence } from "@/lib/services/study-orchestrator-service";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Result type                                                        */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

type ActionResult<T> =
  | { ok: true; data: T }
  | { ok: false; error: { code: string; message: string } };

function succeed<T>(data: T): ActionResult<T> {
  return { ok: true, data };
}

function fail(code: string, message: string): ActionResult<never> {
  return { ok: false, error: { code, message } };
}

function handleError(err: unknown): ActionResult<never> {
  if (err instanceof Error) {
    const msg = err.message;
    if (msg.includes("not found")) return fail("NOT_FOUND", msg);
    if (msg.includes("No active plan")) return fail("NO_ACTIVE_PLAN", msg);
    return fail("SERVICE_ERROR", msg);
  }
  console.error("[recommendation-actions]", err);
  return fail("INTERNAL_ERROR", "An unexpected error occurred.");
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Recommendation Actions                                             */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Get categorised study recommendations for the active plan. */
export async function getRecommendationsAction(): Promise<ActionResult<RecommendationResult>> {
  try {
    const result = getRecommendations();
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/**
 * Accept a recommendation — creates a planner task for today.
 *
 * The client sends the full recommendation object; the service
 * creates the task + links and returns the new task id.
 */
export async function acceptRecommendationAction(
  recommendation: Recommendation,
): Promise<ActionResult<{ taskId: string; dayId: string }>> {
  try {
    const result = acceptRecommendation(recommendation);
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Lightweight count for dashboard badge (avoids sending full payload). */
export async function getRecommendationCountAction(): Promise<ActionResult<number>> {
  try {
    return succeed(getRecommendationCount());
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Intelligence Actions (bridge to orchestrator)                      */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Get the full orchestrator intelligence payload. */
export async function getStudyIntelligenceAction(): Promise<ActionResult<OrchestratorIntelligence | null>> {
  try {
    const result = getStudyIntelligence();
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Generate a smart weekly plan (FSRS + weak-topic enriched). */
export async function generateSmartPlanAction(
  params: CreatePlanParams,
): Promise<ActionResult<SmartPlanResult>> {
  try {
    const result = generateSmartWeeklyPlan(params);
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/** Generate an exam recovery plan. */
export async function generateExamRecoveryAction(
  examSessionId: string,
): Promise<ActionResult<ExamRecoveryResult>> {
  try {
    const result = generateExamRecovery(examSessionId);
    return succeed(result);
  } catch (err) {
    return handleError(err);
  }
}

/**
 * Study planner query layer.
 *
 * All planner-related data access goes here.
 * Pages, routes, and services should never query planner tables directly.
 */
import { eq, and, gte, lte, lt, asc, desc, sql, count, inArray } from "drizzle-orm";
import { db } from "@/db/index";
import {
  studyPlans,
  studyPlanDays,
  studyTasks,
  studyTaskLinks,
  studyTaskEvents,
  studyPlannerSettings,
  chapters,
  chunks,
  questions,
  flashcards,
  examSessions,
  type planStatus,
  type taskStatus,
  type taskType,
  type taskEventKind,
} from "@/db/schema";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export type StudyPlan = typeof studyPlans.$inferSelect;
export type StudyPlanInsert = typeof studyPlans.$inferInsert;

export type StudyPlanDay = typeof studyPlanDays.$inferSelect;
export type StudyPlanDayInsert = typeof studyPlanDays.$inferInsert;

export type StudyTask = typeof studyTasks.$inferSelect;
export type StudyTaskInsert = typeof studyTasks.$inferInsert;

export type StudyTaskLink = typeof studyTaskLinks.$inferSelect;
export type StudyTaskLinkInsert = typeof studyTaskLinks.$inferInsert;

export type StudyTaskEvent = typeof studyTaskEvents.$inferSelect;
export type StudyTaskEventInsert = typeof studyTaskEvents.$inferInsert;

export type StudyPlannerSetting = typeof studyPlannerSettings.$inferSelect;
export type StudyPlannerSettingInsert = typeof studyPlannerSettings.$inferInsert;

export type PlanStatusValue = (typeof planStatus)[keyof typeof planStatus];
export type TaskStatusValue = (typeof taskStatus)[keyof typeof taskStatus];
export type TaskTypeValue = (typeof taskType)[keyof typeof taskType];
export type TaskEventKindValue = (typeof taskEventKind)[keyof typeof taskEventKind];

export interface StudyPlanWithDays extends StudyPlan {
  days: StudyPlanDay[];
}

export interface StudyPlanDayWithTasks extends StudyPlanDay {
  tasks: StudyTask[];
}

export interface StudyTaskWithLinks extends StudyTask {
  links: StudyTaskLink[];
}

export interface StudyTaskWithEvents extends StudyTask {
  events: StudyTaskEvent[];
}

export interface StudyTaskWithLinksResolved extends StudyTask {
  links: StudyTaskLink[];
  linkedChapter?: { id: string; title: string; chapterNo: number } | null;
  linkedChunk?: { id: string; title: string | null; chunkIndex: number } | null;
  linkedExamSession?: { id: string; title: string | null; status: string } | null;
}

export interface TodayPlanResult {
  plan: StudyPlan;
  day: StudyPlanDay | null;
  tasks: StudyTaskWithLinksResolved[];
  overdueTasks: StudyTaskWithLinksResolved[];
  settings: StudyPlannerSetting | null;
}

export interface WeekPlanResult {
  plan: StudyPlan;
  days: (StudyPlanDay & { tasks: StudyTask[] })[];
  weekStart: string;
  weekEnd: string;
  overdueTasks: StudyTask[];
  totalTasks: number;
  completedTasks: number;
}

export interface PlannerSummary {
  plan: PlanSummary | null;
  today: DailyProgress | null;
  streak: { current: number; longest: number };
  overdueTasks: number;
  statusCounts: Record<string, number>;
  upcomingTaskCount: number;
}

export interface DailyProgress {
  date: string;
  totalTasks: number;
  completedTasks: number;
  estimatedMinutes: number;
  actualMinutes: number;
  progressPercent: number;
}

export interface PlanSummary {
  planId: string;
  title: string;
  status: PlanStatusValue;
  totalTasks: number;
  completedTasks: number;
  progressPercent: number;
  startDate: string;
  endDate: string | null;
  totalDays: number;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  STUDY PLANS                                                        */
/* ================================================================== */

/* ---- Reads ---- */

/** Get a study plan by its primary key. */
export function getPlanById(id: string): StudyPlan | undefined {
  return db.select().from(studyPlans).where(eq(studyPlans.id, id)).get();
}

/** List all plans, newest first. */
export function listPlans(): StudyPlan[] {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyPlans)
    .orderBy(desc(studyPlans.createdAt))
    .all();
}

/** List plans by status. */
export function listPlansByStatus(status: PlanStatusValue): StudyPlan[] {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyPlans)
    .where(eq(studyPlans.status, status))
    .orderBy(desc(studyPlans.createdAt))
    .all();
}

/** Get the currently active plan (most recent active). */
export function getActivePlan(): StudyPlan | undefined {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyPlans)
    .where(eq(studyPlans.status, "active"))
    .orderBy(desc(studyPlans.updatedAt))
    .limit(1)
    .get();
}

/** Get a plan with all its days. */
export function getPlanWithDays(planId: string): StudyPlanWithDays | undefined {
  const plan = getPlanById(planId);
  if (!plan) return undefined;
  const days = db
    .select()
    .from(studyPlanDays)
    .where(eq(studyPlanDays.planId, planId))
    .orderBy(asc(studyPlanDays.date))
    .all();
  return { ...plan, days };
}

/** Get plan summary with aggregated stats. */
export function getPlanSummary(planId: string): PlanSummary | undefined {
  const plan = getPlanById(planId);
  if (!plan) return undefined;
  const dayCount = db
    .select({ c: count() })
    .from(studyPlanDays)
    .where(eq(studyPlanDays.planId, planId))
    .get();
  return {
    planId: plan.id,
    title: plan.title,
    status: plan.status as PlanStatusValue,
    totalTasks: plan.totalTasks,
    completedTasks: plan.completedTasks,
    progressPercent: plan.progressPercent,
    startDate: plan.startDate,
    endDate: plan.endDate,
    totalDays: dayCount?.c ?? 0,
  };
}

/* ---- Writes ---- */

/** Create a new study plan. */
export function createPlan(data: StudyPlanInsert): StudyPlan {
  return db.insert(studyPlans).values(data).returning().get();
}

/** Update a study plan. */
export function updatePlan(
  id: string,
  data: Partial<Omit<StudyPlanInsert, "id">>,
): StudyPlan | undefined {
  return db
    .update(studyPlans)
    .set({ ...data, updatedAt: Date.now() })
    .where(eq(studyPlans.id, id))
    .returning()
    .get();
}

/** Delete a study plan (cascades to days, tasks, links, events). */
export function deletePlan(id: string): void {
  db.delete(studyPlans).where(eq(studyPlans.id, id)).run();
}

/** Recalculate plan progress from its tasks. */
export function recalcPlanProgress(planId: string): void {
  const row = db
    .select({
      total: count(),
      completed: sql<number>`sum(case when ${studyTasks.status} = 'completed' then 1 else 0 end)`,
    })
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(eq(studyTasks.planId, planId))
    .get();

  const total = row?.total ?? 0;
  const completed = row?.completed ?? 0;
  const pct = total > 0 ? Math.round((completed / total) * 100) : 0;

  db.update(studyPlans)
    .set({
      totalTasks: total,
      completedTasks: completed,
      progressPercent: pct,
      updatedAt: Date.now(),
    })
    .where(eq(studyPlans.id, planId))
    .run();
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  STUDY PLAN DAYS                                                    */
/* ================================================================== */

/* ---- Reads ---- */

/** Get a plan day by its primary key. */
export function getDayById(id: string): StudyPlanDay | undefined {
  return db.select().from(studyPlanDays).where(eq(studyPlanDays.id, id)).get();
}

/** Get the plan day for a specific date. */
export function getDayByDate(planId: string, date: string): StudyPlanDay | undefined {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyPlanDays)
    .where(and(eq(studyPlanDays.planId, planId), eq(studyPlanDays.date, date)))
    .get();
}

/** List all days for a plan, sorted by date. */
export function listDaysByPlan(planId: string): StudyPlanDay[] {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyPlanDays)
    .where(eq(studyPlanDays.planId, planId))
    .orderBy(asc(studyPlanDays.date))
    .all();
}

/** List days in a date range (inclusive). */
export function listDaysInRange(
  planId: string,
  from: string,
  to: string,
): StudyPlanDay[] {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyPlanDays)
    .where(
      and(
        eq(studyPlanDays.planId, planId),
        gte(studyPlanDays.date, from),
        lte(studyPlanDays.date, to),
      ),
    )
    .orderBy(asc(studyPlanDays.date))
    .all();
}

/** Get a day with its tasks preloaded. */
export function getDayWithTasks(dayId: string): StudyPlanDayWithTasks | undefined {
  const day = getDayById(dayId);
  if (!day) return undefined;
  const tasks = db
    .select()
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(eq(studyTasks.dayId, dayId))
    .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.sortOrder))
    .all();
  return { ...day, tasks };
}

/** Get today's day for a plan. */
export function getTodayDay(planId: string): StudyPlanDay | undefined {
  const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
  return getDayByDate(planId, today);
}

/* ---- Writes ---- */

/** Create a plan day. */
export function createDay(data: StudyPlanDayInsert): StudyPlanDay {
  return db.insert(studyPlanDays).values(data).returning().get();
}

/** Batch-insert multiple plan days. */
export function createDaysBatch(rows: StudyPlanDayInsert[]): void {
  if (rows.length === 0) return;
  db.insert(studyPlanDays).values(rows).run();
}

/** Update a plan day. */
export function updateDay(
  id: string,
  data: Partial<Omit<StudyPlanDayInsert, "id">>,
): StudyPlanDay | undefined {
  return db
    .update(studyPlanDays)
    .set({ ...data, updatedAt: Date.now() })
    .where(eq(studyPlanDays.id, id))
    .returning()
    .get();
}

/** Delete a plan day (cascades to tasks). */
export function deleteDay(id: string): void {
  db.delete(studyPlanDays).where(eq(studyPlanDays.id, id)).run();
}

/** Recalculate day-level aggregates from its tasks. */
export function recalcDayProgress(dayId: string): void {
  const row = db
    .select({
      total: count(),
      completed: sql<number>`sum(case when ${studyTasks.status} = 'completed' then 1 else 0 end)`,
      estMins: sql<number>`sum(${studyTasks.estimatedMinutes})`,
      actMins: sql<number>`sum(${studyTasks.actualMinutes})`,
    })
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(eq(studyTasks.dayId, dayId))
    .get();

  db.update(studyPlanDays)
    .set({
      totalTasks: row?.total ?? 0,
      completedTasks: row?.completed ?? 0,
      estimatedMinutes: row?.estMins ?? 0,
      actualMinutes: row?.actMins ?? 0,
      updatedAt: Date.now(),
    })
    .where(eq(studyPlanDays.id, dayId))
    .run();
}

/** Get a task by its primary key. */
export function getTaskById(id: string): StudyTask | undefined {
  return db.select().from(studyTasks).where(eq(studyTasks.id, id)).get();
}

export function listTasksByDay(dayId: string): StudyTask[] {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(eq(studyTasks.dayId, dayId))
    .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.sortOrder))
    .all();
}

export function listTasksByStatus(
  planId: string,
