): StudyTask[] {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(and(eq(studyTasks.planId, planId), eq(studyTasks.status, status)))
    .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.sortOrder))
    .all();
}

/** List tasks by type across a plan. */
export function listTasksByType(
  planId: string,
  type: TaskTypeValue,
): StudyTask[] {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(and(eq(studyTasks.planId, planId), eq(studyTasks.taskType, type)))
    .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.createdAt))
    .all();
}

/**
 * List overdue tasks in a plan (status = "overdue").
 *
 * Call markOverdueTasks() first to ensure pending/in-progress tasks on
 * past days have been transitioned to "overdue" status.
 */
export function listOverdueTasks(planId: string): StudyTask[] {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(
      and(
        eq(studyTasks.planId, planId),
        eq(studyTasks.status, "overdue"),
      ),
    )
    .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.sortOrder))
    .all();
}

/** Get a task with its content links. */
export function getTaskWithLinks(taskId: string): StudyTaskWithLinks | undefined {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) return undefined;
  const links = db
    .select()
    .from(studyTaskLinks)
    .where(eq(studyTaskLinks.taskId, taskId))
    .orderBy(asc(studyTaskLinks.sortOrder))
    .all();
  return { ...task, links };
}

/** Get a task with its event history. */
export function getTaskWithEvents(taskId: string): StudyTaskWithEvents | undefined {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) return undefined;
  const events = db
    .select()
    .from(studyTaskEvents)
    .where(eq(studyTaskEvents.taskId, taskId))
    .orderBy(desc(studyTaskEvents.occurredAt))
    .all();
  return { ...task, events };
}

/** Count tasks by status for a plan. */
export function countTasksByStatus(planId: string): Record<string, number> {
  const rows = db
    .select({
      status: studyTasks.status,
      c: count(),
    })
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(eq(studyTasks.planId, planId))
    .groupBy(studyTasks.status)
    .all();
  return Object.fromEntries(rows.map((r) => [r.status, r.c]));
}

/* ---- Writes ---- */

/** Create a new task. Auto-computes dueAt from day date when not provided. */
export function createTask(data: StudyTaskInsert): StudyTask {
  // Auto-compute dueAt from the scheduled day when not explicitly provided
  if (data.dueAt == null && data.dayId) {
    const day = getDayById(data.dayId);
    if (day) {
      data = { ...data, dueAt: new Date(day.date + "T23:59:59Z").getTime() };
    }
  }
  return db.insert(studyTasks).values(data).returning().get();
}

/** Batch-insert multiple tasks. */
export function createTasksBatch(rows: StudyTaskInsert[]): void {
  if (rows.length === 0) return;
  db.insert(studyTasks).values(rows).run();
}

/** Update a task. */
export function updateTask(
  id: string,
  data: Partial<Omit<StudyTaskInsert, "id">>,
): StudyTask | undefined {
  return db
    .update(studyTasks)
    .set({ ...data, updatedAt: Date.now() })
    .where(eq(studyTasks.id, id))
    .returning()
    .get();
}

/** Delete a task (cascades to links and events). */
export function deleteTask(id: string): void {
  db.delete(studyTasks).where(eq(studyTasks.id, id)).run();
}

/** Mark a task as started. */
export function startTask(id: string): StudyTask | undefined {
  const now = Date.now();
  const result = db
    .update(studyTasks)
    .set({ status: "in_progress", startedAt: now, updatedAt: now })
    .where(eq(studyTasks.id, id))
    .returning()
    .get();
  if (result) {
    createTaskEvent({
      id: `evt_${now}_${id}`,
      taskId: id,
      eventKind: "started",
      occurredAt: now,
    });
  }
  return result;
}

/** Mark a task as completed. */
export function completeTask(
  id: string,
  actualMinutes?: number,
  resultJson?: Record<string, unknown>,
): StudyTask | undefined {
  const now = Date.now();
  const updates: Partial<StudyTaskInsert> = {
    status: "completed",
    completedAt: now,
    progressPercent: 100,
    updatedAt: now,
  };
  if (actualMinutes !== undefined) updates.actualMinutes = actualMinutes;
  if (resultJson !== undefined) updates.resultJson = resultJson;

  const result = db
    .update(studyTasks)
    .set(updates)
    .where(eq(studyTasks.id, id))
    .returning()
    .get();
  if (result) {
    createTaskEvent({
      id: `evt_${now}_${id}`,
      taskId: id,
      eventKind: "completed",
      payload: resultJson ?? null,
      occurredAt: now,
    });
  }
  return result;
}

/** Mark a task as skipped. */
export function skipTask(id: string): StudyTask | undefined {
  const now = Date.now();
  const result = db
    .update(studyTasks)
    .set({ status: "skipped", updatedAt: now })
    .where(eq(studyTasks.id, id))
    .returning()
    .get();
  if (result) {
    createTaskEvent({
      id: `evt_${now}_${id}`,
      taskId: id,
      eventKind: "skipped",
      occurredAt: now,
    });
  }
  return result;
}

/** Reschedule a task to a different day. */
export function rescheduleTask(
  id: string,
  newDayId: string,
): StudyTask | undefined {
  const now = Date.now();
  const original = getTaskById(id);
  if (!original) return undefined;

  const result = db
    .update(studyTasks)
    .set({
      status: "rescheduled",
      rescheduledTo: newDayId,
      updatedAt: now,
    })
    .where(eq(studyTasks.id, id))
    .returning()
    .get();

  if (result) {
    // Create a copy in the new day
    const newTask = createTask({
      id: `${id}_rs_${now}`,
      planId: original.planId,
      dayId: newDayId,
      taskType: original.taskType as TaskTypeValue,
      status: "pending",
      title: original.title,
      description: original.description,
      sortOrder: original.sortOrder,
      estimatedMinutes: original.estimatedMinutes,
      targetCount: original.targetCount,
      priority: original.priority,
    });

    // Copy links to the new task
    const links = db
      .select()
      .from(studyTaskLinks)
      .where(eq(studyTaskLinks.taskId, id))
      .all();
    if (links.length > 0) {
      createTaskLinksBatch(
        links.map((l, i) => ({
          id: `${newTask.id}_link_${i}`,
          taskId: newTask.id,
          chapterId: l.chapterId,
          chunkId: l.chunkId,
          questionId: l.questionId,
          flashcardId: l.flashcardId,
          examSessionId: l.examSessionId,
          sortOrder: l.sortOrder,
          metadataJson: l.metadataJson,
        })),
      );
    }

    createTaskEvent({
      id: `evt_${now}_${id}`,
      taskId: id,
      eventKind: "rescheduled",
      payload: { newDayId, newTaskId: newTask.id },
      occurredAt: now,
    });
  }
  return result;
}

/**
 * Detect and mark overdue tasks in a plan.
 *
 * Finds pending / in_progress tasks whose scheduled day is strictly
 * before today, OR whose explicit dueAt has passed, and transitions
 * them to "overdue" status.
 */
export function markOverdueTasks(planId: string): number {
  const now = Date.now();
  const today = toISODate(new Date());

  // 1. Day-based: pending/in_progress tasks on past days
  const pastDayIds = db
    .select({ id: studyPlanDays.id })
    .from(studyPlanDays)
    .where(
      and(
        eq(studyPlanDays.planId, planId),
        lt(studyPlanDays.date, today),
      ),
    )
    .all()
    .map((d) => d.id);

  const dayBasedTasks =
    pastDayIds.length > 0
      ? db
          .select()
          .from(studyTasks)
          .where(
            and(
              eq(studyTasks.planId, planId),
              inArray(studyTasks.dayId, pastDayIds),
              inArray(studyTasks.status, ["pending", "in_progress"]),
            ),
          )
          .all()
      : [];

  // 2. dueAt-based: explicit deadline in the past
  const dueAtTasks = db
    .select()
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(
      and(
        eq(studyTasks.planId, planId),
        inArray(studyTasks.status, ["pending", "in_progress"]),
        lte(studyTasks.dueAt, now),
      ),
    )
    .all();

  // Merge and deduplicate
  const merged = new Map<string, StudyTask>();
  for (const t of dayBasedTasks) merged.set(t.id, t);
  for (const t of dueAtTasks) merged.set(t.id, t);

  const tasksToMark = [...merged.values()];
  if (tasksToMark.length === 0) return 0;

  const ids = tasksToMark.map((t) => t.id);
  db.update(studyTasks)
    .set({ status: "overdue", updatedAt: now })
    .where(inArray(studyTasks.id, ids))
    .run();

  for (const t of tasksToMark) {
    createTaskEvent({
      id: `evt_${now}_${t.id}`,
      taskId: t.id,
      eventKind: "overdue_marked",
      occurredAt: now,
    });
  }
  return tasksToMark.length;
}

/** List events for a task, newest first. */
export function listEventsByTask(taskId: string): StudyTaskEvent[] {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyTaskEvents)
    .where(eq(studyTaskEvents.taskId, taskId))
    .orderBy(desc(studyTaskEvents.occurredAt))
    .all();
}

/** List events across a plan in a date range. */
export function listEventsByPlanInRange(
  planId: string,
  from: number,
  to: number,
): StudyTaskEvent[] {
  return db
    .select({
      id: studyTaskEvents.id,
      taskId: studyTaskEvents.taskId,
      eventKind: studyTaskEvents.eventKind,
      payload: studyTaskEvents.payload,
      occurredAt: studyTaskEvents.occurredAt,
      createdAt: studyTaskEvents.createdAt,
    })
    .from(studyTaskEvents)
    .innerJoin(studyTasks, eq(studyTaskEvents.taskId, studyTasks.id))
    .where(
      and(
        eq(studyTasks.planId, planId),
        gte(studyTaskEvents.occurredAt, from),
        lte(studyTaskEvents.occurredAt, to),
      ),
    )
    .orderBy(desc(studyTaskEvents.occurredAt))
    .all();
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  STUDY PLANNER SETTINGS                                             */
/* ================================================================== */

const SETTINGS_SINGLETON_ID = "default";

/** Get the global planner settings. */
export function getSettings(): StudyPlannerSetting | undefined {
  return db
    .select()
    .from(studyPlannerSettings)
    .where(eq(studyPlannerSettings.id, SETTINGS_SINGLETON_ID))
    .get();
}

/** Upsert planner settings. */
export function upsertSettings(
  data: Partial<Omit<StudyPlannerSettingInsert, "id">>,
): StudyPlannerSetting {
  const existing = getSettings();
  if (existing) {
    return db
      .update(studyPlannerSettings)
      .set({ ...data, updatedAt: Date.now() })
      .where(eq(studyPlannerSettings.id, SETTINGS_SINGLETON_ID))
      .returning()
      .get();
  }
  return db
    .insert(studyPlannerSettings)
    .values({ id: SETTINGS_SINGLETON_ID, ...data })
    .returning()
    .get();
}

/** Update streak after a study session. */
export function updateStreak(): void {
  const settings = getSettings();
  const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);

  if (!settings) {
    upsertSettings({
      streakCurrent: 1,
      streakLongest: 1,
      lastStudyDate: today,
    });
    return;
  }

  if (settings.lastStudyDate === today) return; // already counted today

  const yesterday = new Date(Date.now() - 86_400_000).toISOString().slice(0, 10);
  const isConsecutive = settings.lastStudyDate === yesterday;
  const newStreak = isConsecutive ? settings.streakCurrent + 1 : 1;
  const longest = Math.max(newStreak, settings.streakLongest);

  upsertSettings({
    streakCurrent: newStreak,
    streakLongest: longest,
    lastStudyDate: today,
  });
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  AGGREGATE HELPERS                                                  */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Get daily progress for a plan within a date range. */
export function getDailyProgress(
  planId: string,
  from: string,
  to: string,
): DailyProgress[] {
  return db
    .select({
      date: studyPlanDays.date,
      totalTasks: studyPlanDays.totalTasks,
      completedTasks: studyPlanDays.completedTasks,
      estimatedMinutes: studyPlanDays.estimatedMinutes,
      actualMinutes: studyPlanDays.actualMinutes,
      progressPercent: sql<number>`case when ${studyPlanDays.totalTasks} > 0
        then round(${studyPlanDays.completedTasks} * 100.0 / ${studyPlanDays.totalTasks})
        else 0 end`,
    })
    .from(studyPlanDays)
    .where(
      and(
        eq(studyPlanDays.planId, planId),
        gte(studyPlanDays.date, from),
        lte(studyPlanDays.date, to),
      ),
    )
    .orderBy(asc(studyPlanDays.date))
    .all();
}

/** Get task-type distribution for a plan. */
export function getTaskTypeDistribution(
  planId: string,
): { taskType: string; count: number }[] {
  return db
    .select({
      taskType: studyTasks.taskType,
      count: count(),
    })
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(eq(studyTasks.planId, planId))
    .groupBy(studyTasks.taskType)
    .all();
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  HIGH-LEVEL PLANNER-READY QUERIES                                   */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Resolve linked entities for a list of tasks. */
function resolveTaskLinks(
  tasks: StudyTask[],
): StudyTaskWithLinksResolved[] {
  if (tasks.length === 0) return [];

  const taskIds = tasks.map((t) => t.id);
  const allLinks = db
    .select()
    .from(studyTaskLinks)
    .where(inArray(studyTaskLinks.taskId, taskIds))
    .orderBy(asc(studyTaskLinks.sortOrder))
    .all();

  // Collect unique FK ids for batch lookups
  const chapterIds = new Set<string>();
  const chunkIds = new Set<string>();
  const examIds = new Set<string>();

  for (const l of allLinks) {
    if (l.chapterId) chapterIds.add(l.chapterId);
    if (l.chunkId) chunkIds.add(l.chunkId);
    if (l.examSessionId) examIds.add(l.examSessionId);
  }

  // Batch-fetch linked entities
  const chapterMap = chapterIds.size > 0
    ? new Map(
        db
          .select({ id: chapters.id, title: chapters.title, chapterNo: chapters.chapterNo })
          .from(chapters)
          .where(inArray(chapters.id, [...chapterIds]))
          .all()
          .map((c) => [c.id, c]),
      )
    : new Map<string, { id: string; title: string; chapterNo: number }>();

  const chunkMap = chunkIds.size > 0
    ? new Map(
        db
          .select({ id: chunks.id, title: chunks.title, chunkIndex: chunks.chunkIndex })
          .from(chunks)
          .where(inArray(chunks.id, [...chunkIds]))
          .all()
          .map((c) => [c.id, c]),
      )
    : new Map<string, { id: string; title: string | null; chunkIndex: number }>();

  const examMap = examIds.size > 0
    ? new Map(
        db
          .select({ id: examSessions.id, title: examSessions.title, status: examSessions.status })
          .from(examSessions)
          .where(inArray(examSessions.id, [...examIds]))
          .all()
          .map((e) => [e.id, e]),
      )
    : new Map<string, { id: string; title: string | null; status: string }>();

  // Group links by task
  const linksByTask = new Map<string, StudyTaskLink[]>();
  for (const l of allLinks) {
    const arr = linksByTask.get(l.taskId) ?? [];
    arr.push(l);
    linksByTask.set(l.taskId, arr);
  }

  return tasks.map((task) => {
    const links = linksByTask.get(task.id) ?? [];
    // Pick first linked entity of each type for convenience
    const firstChapterId = links.find((l) => l.chapterId)?.chapterId;
    const firstChunkId = links.find((l) => l.chunkId)?.chunkId;
    const firstExamId = links.find((l) => l.examSessionId)?.examSessionId;

    return {
      ...task,
      links,
      linkedChapter: firstChapterId ? chapterMap.get(firstChapterId) ?? null : null,
      linkedChunk: firstChunkId ? chunkMap.get(firstChunkId) ?? null : null,
      linkedExamSession: firstExamId ? examMap.get(firstExamId) ?? null : null,
    };
  });
}

/** ISO date helper. */
function toISODate(d: Date): string {
  return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
}

/** Compute Saturday-based week boundaries for a date. */
function getWeekBounds(refDate: Date): { weekStart: string; weekEnd: string } {
  const day = refDate.getDay(); // 0=Sun … 6=Sat
  const diffToSat = day === 6 ? 0 : day + 1; // days since last Saturday
  const start = new Date(refDate);
  start.setDate(refDate.getDate() - diffToSat);
  const end = new Date(start);
  end.setDate(start.getDate() + 6);
  return { weekStart: toISODate(start), weekEnd: toISODate(end) };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getTodayPlan()                                                     */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Get everything a planner dashboard needs for today:
 * active plan, today's day record, today's tasks with resolved links,
 * overdue tasks, and planner settings.
 */
export function getTodayPlan(): TodayPlanResult | null {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) return null;

  const today = toISODate(new Date());
  const day = getDayByDate(plan.id, today) ?? null;

  const rawTasks = day
    ? db
        .select()
        .from(studyTasks)
        .where(eq(studyTasks.dayId, day.id))
        .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.sortOrder))
        .all()
    : [];

  const tasks = resolveTaskLinks(rawTasks);
  const rawOverdue = listOverdueTasks(plan.id);
  const overdueTasks = resolveTaskLinks(rawOverdue);
  const settings = getSettings() ?? null;

  return { plan, day, tasks, overdueTasks, settings };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getWeekPlan()                                                      */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Get the full week view (Saturday–Friday) around a reference date.
 * Returns the plan, all days in the week with their tasks, and overdue items.
 */
export function getWeekPlan(refDate?: Date): WeekPlanResult | null {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) return null;

  const { weekStart, weekEnd } = getWeekBounds(refDate ?? new Date());

  const days = listDaysInRange(plan.id, weekStart, weekEnd);

  // Batch-fetch tasks for all days in the week
  const dayIds = days.map((d) => d.id);
  const allTasks =
    dayIds.length > 0
      ? db
          .select()
          .from(studyTasks)
          .where(inArray(studyTasks.dayId, dayIds))
          .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.sortOrder))
          .all()
      : [];

  const tasksByDay = new Map<string, StudyTask[]>();
  for (const t of allTasks) {
    const arr = tasksByDay.get(t.dayId) ?? [];
    arr.push(t);
    tasksByDay.set(t.dayId, arr);
  }

  const daysWithTasks = days.map((d) => ({
    ...d,
    tasks: tasksByDay.get(d.id) ?? [],
  }));

  const overdueTasks = listOverdueTasks(plan.id);
  const totalTasks = allTasks.length;
  const completedTasks = allTasks.filter((t) => t.status === "completed").length;

  return {
    plan,
    days: daysWithTasks,
    weekStart,
    weekEnd,
    overdueTasks,
    totalTasks,
    completedTasks,
  };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getOverdueTasks()                                                  */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * All overdue tasks in the active plan, with resolved content links
 * and their originating day date.
 */
export function getOverdueTasks(): (StudyTaskWithLinksResolved & { dayDate: string })[] {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) return [];

  const raw = listOverdueTasks(plan.id);
  if (raw.length === 0) return [];

  const resolved = resolveTaskLinks(raw);

  // Fetch day dates for each task
  const dayIds = [...new Set(raw.map((t) => t.dayId))];
  const dayRows = db
    .select({ id: studyPlanDays.id, date: studyPlanDays.date })
    .from(studyPlanDays)
    .where(inArray(studyPlanDays.id, dayIds))
    .all();
  const dayDateMap = new Map(dayRows.map((d) => [d.id, d.date]));

  return resolved.map((t) => ({
    ...t,
    dayDate: dayDateMap.get(t.dayId) ?? "",
  }));
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getUpcomingTasks()                                                 */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Get the next N pending/in-progress tasks from today onward,
 * with resolved content links and their day dates.
 */
export function getUpcomingTasks(
  limit = 10,
): (StudyTaskWithLinksResolved & { dayDate: string })[] {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) return [];

  const today = toISODate(new Date());

  // Find upcoming days
  const upcomingDays = db
    .select({ id: studyPlanDays.id, date: studyPlanDays.date })
    .from(studyPlanDays)
    .where(
      and(
        eq(studyPlanDays.planId, plan.id),
        gte(studyPlanDays.date, today),
      ),
    )
    .orderBy(asc(studyPlanDays.date))
    .all();

  if (upcomingDays.length === 0) return [];

  const dayIds = upcomingDays.map((d) => d.id);
  const dayDateMap = new Map(upcomingDays.map((d) => [d.id, d.date]));

  const raw = db
    .select()
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(
      and(
        inArray(studyTasks.dayId, dayIds),
        inArray(studyTasks.status, ["pending", "in_progress"]),
      ),
    )
    .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.dueAt), asc(studyTasks.sortOrder))
    .limit(limit)
    .all();

  const resolved = resolveTaskLinks(raw);

  return resolved.map((t) => ({
    ...t,
    dayDate: dayDateMap.get(t.dayId) ?? "",
  }));
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getPlannerSummary()                                                */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * A single call that gives the UI everything it needs for a planner
 * overview widget: plan summary, today's progress, streak, overdue count,
 * status distribution, and upcoming task count.
 */
export function getPlannerSummary(): PlannerSummary {
  const plan = getActivePlan();

  const summary = plan ? getPlanSummary(plan.id) ?? null : null;

  const today = toISODate(new Date());
  let todayProgress: DailyProgress | null = null;
  let overdueCount = 0;
  let statusCounts: Record<string, number> = {};
  let upcomingCount = 0;

  if (plan) {
    // Today's day stats
    const dayRow = getDayByDate(plan.id, today);
    if (dayRow) {
      const pct =
        dayRow.totalTasks > 0
          ? Math.round((dayRow.completedTasks / dayRow.totalTasks) * 100)
          : 0;
      todayProgress = {
        date: today,
        totalTasks: dayRow.totalTasks,
        completedTasks: dayRow.completedTasks,
        estimatedMinutes: dayRow.estimatedMinutes,
        actualMinutes: dayRow.actualMinutes,
        progressPercent: pct,
      };
    }

    overdueCount = listOverdueTasks(plan.id).length;
    statusCounts = countTasksByStatus(plan.id);

    // Count pending tasks from today onward
    const upcoming = db
      .select({ c: count() })
      .from(studyTasks)
      .innerJoin(studyPlanDays, eq(studyTasks.dayId, studyPlanDays.id))
      .where(
        and(
          eq(studyTasks.planId, plan.id),
          gte(studyPlanDays.date, today),
          inArray(studyTasks.status, ["pending", "in_progress"]),
        ),
      )
      .get();
    upcomingCount = upcoming?.c ?? 0;
  }

  const settings = getSettings();
  const streak = {
    current: settings?.streakCurrent ?? 0,
    longest: settings?.streakLongest ?? 0,
  };

  return { plan: summary, today: todayProgress, streak, overdueTasks: overdueCount, statusCounts, upcomingTaskCount: upcomingCount };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getTasksForDate(date)                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Get all tasks for a specific date in the active plan,
 * with resolved content links.
 */
export function getTasksForDate(
  date: string,
): { day: StudyPlanDay | null; tasks: StudyTaskWithLinksResolved[] } {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) return { day: null, tasks: [] };

  const day = getDayByDate(plan.id, date) ?? null;
  if (!day) return { day: null, tasks: [] };

  const raw = db
    .select()
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(eq(studyTasks.dayId, day.id))
    .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.sortOrder))
    .all();

  return { day, tasks: resolveTaskLinks(raw) };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getTasksForDateRange(start, end)                                   */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Get all tasks for a date range in the active plan,
 * grouped by day with resolved content links.
 */
export function getTasksForDateRange(
  start: string,
  end: string,
): { days: (StudyPlanDay & { tasks: StudyTaskWithLinksResolved[] })[] } {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) return { days: [] };

  const dayRows = listDaysInRange(plan.id, start, end);
  if (dayRows.length === 0) return { days: [] };

  const dayIds = dayRows.map((d) => d.id);
  const allTasks = db
    .select()
    .from(studyTasks)
    .where(inArray(studyTasks.dayId, dayIds))
    .orderBy(asc(studyTasks.sortOrder))
    .all();

  const resolved = resolveTaskLinks(allTasks);
  const tasksByDay = new Map<string, StudyTaskWithLinksResolved[]>();
  for (const t of resolved) {
    const arr = tasksByDay.get(t.dayId) ?? [];
    arr.push(t);
    tasksByDay.set(t.dayId, arr);
  }

  return {
    days: dayRows.map((d) => ({
      ...d,
      tasks: tasksByDay.get(d.id) ?? [],
    })),
  };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getTaskByIdResolved(id)                                            */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Get a single task by ID with fully resolved content links,
 * event history, and the parent day/plan context.
 */
export function getTaskByIdResolved(
  id: string,
): (StudyTaskWithLinksResolved & {
  events: StudyTaskEvent[];
  day: StudyPlanDay | null;
  plan: StudyPlan | null;
}) | null {
  const task = getTaskById(id);
  if (!task) return null;

  const [resolved] = resolveTaskLinks([task]);

  const events = db
    .select()
    .from(studyTaskEvents)
    .where(eq(studyTaskEvents.taskId, id))
    .orderBy(desc(studyTaskEvents.occurredAt))
    .all();

  const day = getDayById(task.dayId) ?? null;
  const plan = getPlanById(task.planId) ?? null;

  return { ...resolved, events, day, plan };
}

// src/lib/planner/utils.ts — Pure helpers for planner task logic

import type { PlannerTask, TaskBucket } from "./types";

/**
 * A task is overdue when it has a dueAt timestamp in the past
 * and is not already completed, skipped, or rescheduled.
 */
export function isTaskOverdue(task: PlannerTask, now: number = Date.now()): boolean {
  if (task.status === "completed" || task.status === "skipped" || task.status === "rescheduled") {
    return false;
  }
  return task.dueAt != null && task.dueAt < now;
}

export function isTaskCompleted(task: PlannerTask): boolean {
  return task.status === "completed";
}

/** ISO date string (YYYY-MM-DD) for a given unix-ms timestamp. */
function toISODate(ms: number): string {
  return new Date(ms).toISOString().slice(0, 10);
}

/** End of day + 6 days from `todayMs` (i.e. the 7-day window boundary). */
function endOfWeekMs(todayMs: number): number {
  const d = new Date(todayMs);
  d.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + 6);
  return d.getTime();
}

export function getTaskBucket(task: PlannerTask, today: number = Date.now()): TaskBucket {
  if (isTaskCompleted(task)) return "completed";

  const todayStr = toISODate(today);

  // Overdue: past due OR scheduled for a past date (and not done)
  if (isTaskOverdue(task, today)) return "overdue";
  if (task.scheduledFor && task.scheduledFor < todayStr) return "overdue";

  // Today: scheduledFor matches today, or dueAt is within today
  if (task.scheduledFor === todayStr) return "today";
  if (task.dueAt != null) {
    const dueDate = toISODate(task.dueAt);
    if (dueDate === todayStr) return "today";
  }

  // This week: within the next 7 days
  const weekEnd = endOfWeekMs(today);
  if (task.scheduledFor) {
    const scheduledMs = new Date(task.scheduledFor + "T23:59:59").getTime();
    if (scheduledMs <= weekEnd) return "thisWeek";
  }
  if (task.dueAt != null && task.dueAt <= weekEnd) return "thisWeek";

  return "upcoming";
}

export function groupTasksByBucket(
  tasks: PlannerTask[],
  today: number = Date.now(),
): Record<TaskBucket, PlannerTask[]> {
  const buckets: Record<TaskBucket, PlannerTask[]> = {
    overdue: [],
    today: [],
    thisWeek: [],
    upcoming: [],
    completed: [],
  };

  for (const task of tasks) {
    buckets[getTaskBucket(task, today)].push(task);
  }

  return buckets;
}

/**
 * Planner page data queries.
 *
 * Composes lower-level query/service functions into the shapes
 * needed by the PlannerPage component. Never accesses db directly —
 * always goes through the existing query layer in src/lib/db/queries/planner.
 */

import {
  getActivePlan,
  getPlannerSummary as getRawSummary,
  getTasksForDateRange,
  listOverdueTasks,
  type StudyPlan,
  type StudyTask,
  type StudyTaskWithLinksResolved,
} from "@/lib/db/queries/planner";
import { db } from "@/db/index";
import { weakAreas } from "@/db/schema";
import { eq, count } from "drizzle-orm";
import type { PlannerSummaryProps } from "@/components/planner/PlannerSummary";
import type { BucketTask } from "@/components/planner/PlannerPage";
import type { TaskBucket } from "@/lib/planner/types";
import {
  getDueFlashcardLoad,
  generateFsrsPlannerTasks,
} from "@/lib/planner/fsrs-integration";
import { generateWeakAreaTasks } from "@/lib/planner/weak-area-engine";
import {
  resolveTaskLinkInfo,
  getTaskTypeFallbackLink,
} from "@/lib/planner/concept-links";
import {
  computeRecommendation,
  type Recommendation,
  type RecommendationInput,
} from "@/lib/planner/recommendation-engine";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Helpers                                                            */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function toISODate(d: Date): string {
  return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
}

function addDays(d: Date, n: number): Date {
  const r = new Date(d);
  r.setDate(r.getDate() + n);
  return r;
}

/** Map a task (base or resolved) to the slim BucketTask shape used by the UI. */
function toBucketTask(
  t: StudyTask | StudyTaskWithLinksResolved,
  scheduledDate?: string | null,
): BucketTask {
  // Resolve link info for tasks that have resolved links
  let linkUrl: string | null = null;
  let linkLabel: string | null = null;
  if ("linkedChapter" in t) {
    const info = resolveTaskLinkInfo(t as StudyTaskWithLinksResolved);
    if (info) {
      linkUrl = info.url;
      linkLabel = info.label;
    }
  }
  if (!linkUrl) {
    const fallback = getTaskTypeFallbackLink(t.taskType);
    if (fallback) {
      linkUrl = fallback.url;
      linkLabel = linkLabel ?? fallback.label;
    }
  }

  return {
    id: t.id,
    taskType: t.taskType,
    status: t.status,
    title: t.title,
    description: t.description,
    estimatedMinutes: t.estimatedMinutes,
    priority: t.priority,
    sourceType: t.sourceType ?? null,
    scheduledFor: t.scheduledFor ?? scheduledDate ?? null,
    linkUrl,
    linkLabel,
  };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getActivePlanForUser                                               */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Get the active study plan. Currently user-agnostic (single-user app),
 * but accepts userId for forward-compatibility.
 */
export function getActivePlanForUser(
  _userId?: string,
): StudyPlan | undefined {
  return getActivePlan();
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getPlannerTasksInRange                                             */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Get all tasks for a date range in the active plan, bucketed by
 * overdue / today / thisWeek / upcoming / completed.
 */
export function getPlannerTasksInRange(
  _userId?: string,
  range?: { start: string; end: string },
): Record<TaskBucket, BucketTask[]> {
  const empty: Record<TaskBucket, BucketTask[]> = {
    overdue: [],
    today: [],
    thisWeek: [],
    upcoming: [],
    completed: [],
  };

  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) return empty;

  const today = toISODate(new Date());
  const weekEnd = toISODate(addDays(new Date(), 6));
  const start = range?.start ?? today;
  const end = range?.end ?? toISODate(addDays(new Date(), 30));

  // Overdue tasks (status = "overdue" in db)
  const rawOverdue = listOverdueTasks(plan.id);
  empty.overdue = rawOverdue.map((t) => toBucketTask(t));

  // Date-range tasks
  const { days } = getTasksForDateRange(start, end);

  for (const day of days) {
    for (const task of day.tasks) {
      // Already counted as overdue by status
      if (task.status === "overdue") continue;

      if (task.status === "completed" || task.status === "skipped") {
        empty.completed.push(toBucketTask(task, day.date));
      } else if (day.date === today) {
        empty.today.push(toBucketTask(task, day.date));
      } else if (day.date <= weekEnd && day.date > today) {
        empty.thisWeek.push(toBucketTask(task, day.date));
      } else if (day.date > weekEnd) {
        empty.upcoming.push(toBucketTask(task, day.date));
      } else {
        // Past days with non-completed, non-overdue tasks → treat as overdue
        empty.overdue.push(toBucketTask(task, day.date));
      }
    }
  }

  // Merge virtual FSRS tasks into the appropriate buckets
  const fsrsTasks = generateFsrsPlannerTasks();
  for (const ft of fsrsTasks) {
    if (ft.status === "overdue") {
      empty.overdue.push(ft);
    } else {
      empty.today.push(ft);
    }
  }

  // Merge virtual weak-area tasks
  const weakTasks = generateWeakAreaTasks();
  for (const wt of weakTasks) {
    if (wt.status === "overdue") {
      empty.overdue.push(wt);
    } else {
      empty.today.push(wt);
    }
  }

  return empty;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getPlannerPageSummary                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Build the summary props for PlannerSummary component.
 */
export function getPlannerPageSummary(
  _userId?: string,
): PlannerSummaryProps {
  const raw = getRawSummary();

  // Due flashcards count (from FSRS integration)
  const fsrsLoad = getDueFlashcardLoad();
  const dueFlashcardsCount = fsrsLoad.dueCount;

  // Active weak areas count
  const weakAreaCountRow = db
    .select({ c: count() })
    .from(weakAreas)
    .where(eq(weakAreas.active, 1))
    .get();
  const activeWeakAreasCount = weakAreaCountRow?.c ?? 0;

  // Exam date from active plan
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  const examDate = plan?.examDate ?? null;

  return {
    todayPlannedMinutes: raw.today?.estimatedMinutes ?? 0,
    todayCompletedMinutes: raw.today?.actualMinutes ?? 0,
    dueFlashcardsCount,
    activeWeakAreasCount,
    examDate,
  };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getPlannerPageData — all-in-one for the server component            */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface PlannerPageData {
  summary: PlannerSummaryProps;
  buckets: Record<TaskBucket, BucketTask[]>;
  recommendation: Recommendation;
  hasPlan: boolean;
}

/**
 * Single entry point for the planner page server component.
 * Returns everything needed to render PlannerPage.
 */
export function getPlannerPageData(userId?: string): PlannerPageData {
  const plan = getActivePlanForUser(userId);
  const summary = getPlannerPageSummary(userId);
  const buckets = getPlannerTasksInRange(userId);

  // Build recommendation input from data already fetched
  const fsrsLoad = getDueFlashcardLoad(userId);
  const weakCount = db
    .select({ c: count() })
    .from(weakAreas)
    .where(eq(weakAreas.active, 1))
    .get();

  const recInput: RecommendationInput = {
    overdueTasks: buckets.overdue,
    todayTasks: buckets.today,
    fsrsLoad,
    activeWeakAreaCount: weakCount?.c ?? 0,
    examDate: plan?.examDate ?? null,
    completedMinutesToday: summary.todayCompletedMinutes,
    dailyBudgetMinutes: plan?.dailyTimeBudgetMin ?? 120,
  };

  const recommendation = computeRecommendation(recInput);

  return {
    summary,
    buckets,
    recommendation,
    hasPlan: !!plan,
  };
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\lib\planner\recommendation-engine.ts
====================================================================================================

/**
 * Recommendation Engine — deterministic, rule-based study advisor.
 *
 * Computes the next best study action from overdue tasks, today's tasks,
 * FSRS due load, active weak areas, exam proximity, and time budget.
 *
 * NO AI/LLM. Pure functions. Easy to test and adjust.
 */

import type { BucketTask } from "@/components/planner/PlannerPage";
import type { DueFlashcardLoad } from "@/lib/planner/fsrs-integration";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface RecommendationInput {
  overdueTasks: BucketTask[];
  todayTasks: BucketTask[];
  fsrsLoad: DueFlashcardLoad;
  activeWeakAreaCount: number;
  examDate: string | null; // ISO YYYY-MM-DD or null
  completedMinutesToday: number;
  dailyBudgetMinutes: number;
}

export interface TaskMix {
  flashcardMinutes: number;
  questionMinutes: number;
  weakAreaMinutes: number;
  notebookMinutes: number;
}

export type OverloadLevel = "low" | "moderate" | "high";

export interface Recommendation {
  nextBestAction: string;
  recommendedFocusArea: string;
  overloadLevel: OverloadLevel;
  taskMix: TaskMix;
  suggestions: string[];
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Constants                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

const EXAM_CLOSE_DAYS = 7;
const FSRS_HIGH_DUE = 50;
const BUDGET_CONSUMED_THRESHOLD = 0.85; // 85 %

/* Baseline daily distribution weights  (sum = 1) */
const BASE_WEIGHTS = {
  flashcard: 0.30,
  question: 0.35,
  weakArea: 0.15,
  notebook: 0.20,
};

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Pure helpers                                                       */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function daysUntilExam(examDate: string | null): number | null {
  if (!examDate) return null;
  const now = new Date();
  now.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  const target = new Date(examDate + "T00:00:00");
  const diff = Math.ceil((target.getTime() - now.getTime()) / 86_400_000);
  return Math.max(0, diff);
}

function sumMinutesByType(
  tasks: BucketTask[],
  types: string[],
): number {
  return tasks
    .filter((t) => types.includes(t.taskType))
    .reduce((sum, t) => sum + t.estimatedMinutes, 0);
}

function budgetConsumedRatio(completed: number, budget: number): number {
  return budget > 0 ? completed / budget : 0;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Scoring & weights                                                  */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

interface AdjustedWeights {
  flashcard: number;
  question: number;
  weakArea: number;
  notebook: number;
}

function adjustWeights(input: RecommendationInput): AdjustedWeights {
  const w = { ...BASE_WEIGHTS };
  const daysLeft = daysUntilExam(input.examDate);

  // Rule 2: Exam < 7 days → boost questions, reduce notebook
  if (daysLeft !== null && daysLeft < EXAM_CLOSE_DAYS) {
    const boost = 0.15;
    w.question += boost;
    w.notebook = Math.max(0.05, w.notebook - boost);
  }

  // Rule 3: FSRS due > 50 → boost flashcard review
  if (input.fsrsLoad.dueCount > FSRS_HIGH_DUE) {
    const boost = 0.10;
    w.flashcard += boost;
    w.question = Math.max(0.10, w.question - boost * 0.5);
    w.notebook = Math.max(0.05, w.notebook - boost * 0.5);
  }

  // Rule 4: Active weak areas → boost remediation
  if (input.activeWeakAreaCount > 0) {
    const boost = Math.min(0.10, input.activeWeakAreaCount * 0.03);
    w.weakArea += boost;
    w.notebook = Math.max(0.05, w.notebook - boost);
  }

  // Normalise to sum = 1
  const total = w.flashcard + w.question + w.weakArea + w.notebook;
  w.flashcard /= total;
  w.question /= total;
  w.weakArea /= total;
  w.notebook /= total;

  return w;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Task mix                                                           */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function computeTaskMix(
  remaining: number,
  weights: AdjustedWeights,
): TaskMix {
  return {
    flashcardMinutes: Math.round(remaining * weights.flashcard),
    questionMinutes: Math.round(remaining * weights.question),
    weakAreaMinutes: Math.round(remaining * weights.weakArea),
    notebookMinutes: Math.round(remaining * weights.notebook),
  };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Overload level                                                     */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function computeOverloadLevel(input: RecommendationInput): OverloadLevel {
  const pendingMinutes =
    input.overdueTasks.reduce((s, t) => s + t.estimatedMinutes, 0) +
    input.todayTasks
      .filter((t) => t.status !== "completed")
      .reduce((s, t) => s + t.estimatedMinutes, 0) +
    input.fsrsLoad.estimatedMinutes;

  const remaining = input.dailyBudgetMinutes - input.completedMinutesToday;

  if (remaining <= 0 || pendingMinutes > remaining * 2) return "high";
  if (pendingMinutes > remaining * 1.2) return "moderate";
  return "low";
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Next best action                                                   */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function pickNextBestAction(input: RecommendationInput): string {
  const consumed = budgetConsumedRatio(
    input.completedMinutesToday,
    input.dailyBudgetMinutes,
  );

  // Rule 5: Budget nearly consumed → lighter tasks
  if (consumed >= BUDGET_CONSUMED_THRESHOLD) {
    return "بودجه امروز تقریباً تمام شده — مرور سبک فلش‌کارت پیشنهاد می‌شود";
  }

  // Rule 1: Overdue tasks get highest priority
  if (input.overdueTasks.length > 0) {
    const top = input.overdueTasks[0];
    return `${input.overdueTasks.length} تسک عقب‌افتاده — ابتدا «${top.title}» را انجام دهید`;
  }

  // Rule 3: FSRS due > 50
  if (input.fsrsLoad.dueCount > FSRS_HIGH_DUE) {
    return `مرور ${input.fsrsLoad.dueCount} فلش‌کارت موعد — ابتدا کارت‌ها را مرور کنید`;
  }

  // Rule 2: Exam < 7 days
  const daysLeft = daysUntilExam(input.examDate);
  if (daysLeft !== null && daysLeft < EXAM_CLOSE_DAYS) {
    return `${daysLeft} روز تا آزمون — تمرکز روی تست‌زنی`;
  }

  // Rule 4: Active weak areas
  if (input.activeWeakAreaCount > 0) {
    return `${input.activeWeakAreaCount} نقطه ضعف فعال — تقویت مباحث ضعیف را شروع کنید`;
  }

  // FSRS due (any count)
  if (input.fsrsLoad.dueCount > 0) {
    return `مرور ${input.fsrsLoad.dueCount} فلش‌کارت موعد`;
  }

  // Default: pick first today task
  const pending = input.todayTasks.filter((t) => t.status !== "completed");
  if (pending.length > 0) {
    return `ادامه برنامه امروز — «${pending[0].title}»`;
  }

  return "همه تسک‌ها تکمیل شده — آفرین! 🎉";
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Focus area                                                         */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function pickFocusArea(input: RecommendationInput): string {
  const daysLeft = daysUntilExam(input.examDate);

  if (input.overdueTasks.length >= 3) return "تسک‌های عقب‌افتاده";
  if (daysLeft !== null && daysLeft < EXAM_CLOSE_DAYS) return "تست‌زنی آزمون";
  if (input.fsrsLoad.dueCount > FSRS_HIGH_DUE) return "مرور فلش‌کارت";
  if (input.activeWeakAreaCount >= 2) return "تقویت نقاط ضعف";
  if (input.fsrsLoad.dueCount > 0) return "مرور فلش‌کارت";
  return "مطالعه عمومی";
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Suggestions                                                        */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function buildSuggestions(input: RecommendationInput): string[] {
  const tips: string[] = [];
  const daysLeft = daysUntilExam(input.examDate);
  const consumed = budgetConsumedRatio(
    input.completedMinutesToday,
    input.dailyBudgetMinutes,
  );
  const remaining = input.dailyBudgetMinutes - input.completedMinutesToday;

  if (input.overdueTasks.length > 5) {
    tips.push(
      "تسک‌های عقب‌افتاده زیاد شده — اولویت‌بندی کنید یا تسک‌های کم‌اهمیت را حذف کنید",
    );
  }

  if (daysLeft !== null && daysLeft <= 3) {
    tips.push("آزمون خیلی نزدیک است — فقط تست بزنید و مرور کنید");
  } else if (daysLeft !== null && daysLeft < EXAM_CLOSE_DAYS) {
    tips.push("هفته آزمون — حجم مطالعه جدید را کاهش دهید، مرور بیشتر کنید");
  }

  if (input.fsrsLoad.dueCount > FSRS_HIGH_DUE) {
    tips.push(
      `${input.fsrsLoad.dueCount} فلش‌کارت معوق — هر روز حداقل ۵۰ کارت مرور کنید`,
    );
  }

  if (input.activeWeakAreaCount > 0) {
    tips.push(
      `${input.activeWeakAreaCount} فصل ضعیف شناسایی شده — تست‌های هدفمند بزنید`,
    );
  }

  if (consumed >= BUDGET_CONSUMED_THRESHOLD) {
    tips.push("استراحت بعد از مطالعه طولانی — مرور سبک یا دفترچه یادداشت");
  } else if (remaining > 60) {
    tips.push(`هنوز ${Math.round(remaining)} دقیقه باقی مانده — وقت کافی دارید`);
  }

  return tips;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Main entry point                                                   */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export function computeRecommendation(
  input: RecommendationInput,
): Recommendation {
  const remaining = Math.max(
    0,
    input.dailyBudgetMinutes - input.completedMinutesToday,
  );

  const weights = adjustWeights(input);

  return {
    nextBestAction: pickNextBestAction(input),
    recommendedFocusArea: pickFocusArea(input),
    overloadLevel: computeOverloadLevel(input),
    taskMix: computeTaskMix(remaining, weights),
    suggestions: buildSuggestions(input),
  };
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\lib\planner\weak-area-engine.ts
====================================================================================================

/**
 * Weak Area Engine — analyses question performance, maintains weak_areas
 * records, and generates virtual planner tasks for weak-area remediation.
 *
 * Read-only from question_attempts + questions tables.
 * Writes only to weak_areas / weak_area_events tables.
 */

import { db } from "@/db/index";
import {
  questionAttempts,
  questions,
  weakAreas,
  weakAreaEvents,
  weakAreaEventType,
  taskType,
  taskSourceType,
  originRefType,
} from "@/db/schema";
import { eq, and, gte, sql, desc, count, asc } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getChapterById } from "@/lib/db/queries/chapters";
import type { BucketTask } from "@/components/planner/PlannerPage";
import { resolveVirtualTaskLink } from "@/lib/planner/concept-links";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface ChapterPerformance {
  chapterId: string;
  chapterTitle: string;
  totalAttempts: number;
  incorrectCount: number;
  weaknessScore: number; // 0–1, ratio of incorrect/total
  recentIncorrectQuestionIds: string[];
}

export interface PerformanceAnalysis {
  byChapter: ChapterPerformance[];
  /** Only chapters above the activation threshold. */
  weak: ChapterPerformance[];
  analysedAt: number; // unix ms
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Constants                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/** Weakness score above this marks a chapter as an active weak area. */
const WEAKNESS_THRESHOLD = 0.3;

/** Only analyse attempts from the last N days. */
const LOOKBACK_DAYS = 30;

/** Average minutes per weak-area review task. */
const AVG_REVIEW_MINUTES = 15;

/** Stable prefix for virtual weak-area tasks. */
const WEAK_TASK_ID_PREFIX = "weak-virtual-";

/** Default user ID for single-user mode. */
const DEFAULT_USER = "default";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Helpers                                                            */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function generateId(prefix: string): string {
  return `${prefix}_${Date.now().toString(36)}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  analyzeQuestionPerformance                                         */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Query recent incorrect attempts, group by chapter, and compute
 * weakness scores.  Read-only — never writes.
 */
export function analyzeQuestionPerformance(
  userId?: string,
): PerformanceAnalysis {
  const cutoff = Date.now() - LOOKBACK_DAYS * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;

  // Aggregate attempts per chapter
  const rows = db.all<{
    chapter_id: string;
    total: number;
    incorrect: number;
  }>(sql`
    SELECT
      q.chapter_id,
      COUNT(*)                                                 AS total,
      SUM(CASE WHEN qa.outcome = 'incorrect' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS incorrect
    FROM question_attempts qa
    INNER JOIN questions q ON qa.question_id = q.id
    WHERE qa.attempted_at >= ${cutoff}
      AND q.chapter_id IS NOT NULL
    GROUP BY q.chapter_id
    HAVING total >= 3
  `);

  // Recent incorrect question IDs per chapter (max 10)
  const recentByChapter = new Map<string, string[]>();
  for (const row of rows) {
    if (row.incorrect === 0) continue;
    const ids = db.all<{ question_id: string }>(sql`
      SELECT DISTINCT qa.question_id
      FROM question_attempts qa
      INNER JOIN questions q ON qa.question_id = q.id
      WHERE qa.outcome = 'incorrect'
        AND qa.attempted_at >= ${cutoff}
        AND q.chapter_id = ${row.chapter_id}
      ORDER BY qa.attempted_at DESC
      LIMIT 10
    `);
    recentByChapter.set(
      row.chapter_id,
      ids.map((r) => r.question_id),
    );
  }

  const byChapter: ChapterPerformance[] = rows.map((r) => {
    const chapter = getChapterById(r.chapter_id);
    const score = r.total > 0 ? r.incorrect / r.total : 0;
    return {
      chapterId: r.chapter_id,
      chapterTitle: chapter?.title ?? "فصل نامشخص",
      totalAttempts: r.total,
      incorrectCount: r.incorrect,
      weaknessScore: Math.round(score * 100) / 100,
      recentIncorrectQuestionIds: recentByChapter.get(r.chapter_id) ?? [],
    };
  });

  const weak = byChapter.filter((c) => c.weaknessScore > WEAKNESS_THRESHOLD);

  return { byChapter, weak, analysedAt: Date.now() };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  updateWeakAreas                                                    */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Upsert weak_areas records and insert weak_area_events based on the
 * latest performance analysis. Safe to call repeatedly — idempotent
 * per chapter.
 */
export function updateWeakAreas(
  analysis: PerformanceAnalysis,
  userId: string = DEFAULT_USER,
): void {
  const now = Date.now();

  for (const perf of analysis.byChapter) {
    const weaknessInt = Math.round(perf.weaknessScore * 100);
    const strengthInt = 100 - weaknessInt;
    const isActive = perf.weaknessScore > WEAKNESS_THRESHOLD ? 1 : 0;

    // Check for existing record
    const existing = db
      .select()
      .from(weakAreas)
      .where(
        and(
          eq(weakAreas.userId, userId),
          eq(weakAreas.chapterId, perf.chapterId),
        ),
      )
      .get();

    if (existing) {
      const wasActive = existing.active === 1;

      db.update(weakAreas)
        .set({
          weaknessScore: weaknessInt,
          strengthScore: strengthInt,
          active: isActive,
          lastSeenAt: now,
          updatedAt: now,
        })
        .where(eq(weakAreas.id, existing.id))
        .run();

      // Log event on status transitions
      if (!wasActive && isActive === 1) {
        db.insert(weakAreaEvents)
          .values({
            id: generateId("wae"),
            weakAreaId: existing.id,
            eventType: weakAreaEventType.detected,
            sourceRefType: originRefType.chapter,
            sourceRefId: perf.chapterId,
            weight: weaknessInt,
            createdAt: now,
          })
          .run();
      } else if (wasActive && isActive === 0) {
        db.insert(weakAreaEvents)
          .values({
            id: generateId("wae"),
            weakAreaId: existing.id,
            eventType: weakAreaEventType.recovered,
            sourceRefType: originRefType.chapter,
            sourceRefId: perf.chapterId,
            weight: weaknessInt,
            createdAt: now,
          })
          .run();
      } else if (wasActive && isActive === 1 && weaknessInt > (existing.weaknessScore ?? 0)) {
        db.insert(weakAreaEvents)
          .values({
            id: generateId("wae"),
            weakAreaId: existing.id,
            eventType: weakAreaEventType.worsened,
            sourceRefType: originRefType.chapter,
            sourceRefId: perf.chapterId,
            weight: weaknessInt,
            createdAt: now,
          })
          .run();
      }
    } else if (isActive === 1) {
      // Create new weak area only if it crosses threshold
      const waId = generateId("wa");

      db.insert(weakAreas)
        .values({
          id: waId,
          userId,
          chapterId: perf.chapterId,
          weaknessScore: weaknessInt,
          strengthScore: strengthInt,
          active: 1,
          lastSeenAt: now,
          createdAt: now,
          updatedAt: now,
        })
        .run();

      db.insert(weakAreaEvents)
        .values({
          id: generateId("wae"),
          weakAreaId: waId,
          eventType: weakAreaEventType.detected,
          sourceRefType: originRefType.chapter,
          sourceRefId: perf.chapterId,
          weight: weaknessInt,
          createdAt: now,
        })
        .run();
    }
  }
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  generateWeakAreaTasks                                               */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Generate virtual (non-persisted) planner tasks for active weak areas.
 * Each active weak_area with a linked chapter produces one task.
 *
 * Read-only from weak_areas — does not persist tasks.
 */
export function generateWeakAreaTasks(
  userId: string = DEFAULT_USER,
): BucketTask[] {
  const areas = db
    .select()
    .from(weakAreas)
    .where(
      and(eq(weakAreas.userId, userId), eq(weakAreas.active, 1)),
    )
    .orderBy(desc(weakAreas.weaknessScore))
    .all();

  if (areas.length === 0) return [];

  const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);

  return areas
    .filter((a) => a.chapterId != null)
    .map((a) => {
      const chapter = getChapterById(a.chapterId!);
      const title = chapter?.title ?? "فصل نامشخص";
      const score = a.weaknessScore ?? 50;

      return {
        id: `${WEAK_TASK_ID_PREFIX}${a.id}`,
        taskType: taskType.weakAreaReview,
        status: score >= 60 ? "overdue" : "pending",
        title: `تقویت نقطه ضعف — ${title}`,
        description: `امتیاز ضعف: ${score}٪`,
        estimatedMinutes: AVG_REVIEW_MINUTES,
        priority: score >= 60 ? 2 : 1,
        sourceType: taskSourceType.weakArea,
        scheduledFor: today,
        ...(() => {
          const link = resolveVirtualTaskLink(taskType.weakAreaReview, a.chapterId!, title);
          return { linkUrl: link.url, linkLabel: link.label };
        })(),
      };
    });
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Utilities                                                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/** Check whether a task ID belongs to a virtual weak-area task. */
export function isWeakAreaVirtualTask(taskId: string): boolean {
  return taskId.startsWith(WEAK_TASK_ID_PREFIX);
}

/**
 * Run the full pipeline: analyse → update → return tasks.
 * Convenience wrapper for cron / page-load usage.
 */
export function refreshWeakAreasAndGetTasks(
  userId: string = DEFAULT_USER,
): BucketTask[] {
  const analysis = analyzeQuestionPerformance(userId);
  updateWeakAreas(analysis, userId);
  return generateWeakAreaTasks(userId);
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\lib\planner\fsrs-integration.ts
====================================================================================================

/**
 * FSRS Planner Integration — read-only bridge between the FSRS spaced
 * repetition engine and the planner task system.
 *
 * Generates virtual (non-persisted) BucketTasks from FSRS due-card data
 * so they appear alongside study-plan tasks in the planner UI.
 *
 * CRITICAL: Does NOT modify any flashcard or review data.
 */

import {
  getDueCardsByChapter,
  estimateReviewWorkload,
  type ChapterDueSummary,
  type ReviewWorkload,
} from "@/lib/services/fsrs-service";
import { getChapterById } from "@/lib/db/queries/chapters";
import { taskType, taskSourceType } from "@/db/schema";
import type { BucketTask } from "@/components/planner/PlannerPage";
import { resolveVirtualTaskLink } from "@/lib/planner/concept-links";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface DueFlashcardLoad {
  dueCount: number;
  estimatedMinutes: number;
  byChapter: {
    chapterId: string;
    chapterTitle: string;
    dueCount: number;
    overdueCount: number;
    newCount: number;
    estimatedMinutes: number;
  }[];
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  getDueFlashcardLoad                                                */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Returns a summary of the current FSRS review workload, broken down
 * by chapter. Read-only — never writes.
 */
export function getDueFlashcardLoad(
  _userId?: string,
): DueFlashcardLoad {
  const byChapterRaw = getDueCardsByChapter();

  const byChapter = byChapterRaw.map((c) => {
    const chapter = getChapterById(c.chapterId);
    return {
      chapterId: c.chapterId,
      chapterTitle: chapter?.title ?? "فصل نامشخص",
      dueCount: c.dueCount,
      overdueCount: c.overdueCount,
      newCount: c.newCount,
      estimatedMinutes: c.estimatedMinutes,
    };
  });

  const dueCount = byChapter.reduce((s, c) => s + c.dueCount, 0);
  const estimatedMinutes = byChapter.reduce(
    (s, c) => s + c.estimatedMinutes,
    0,
  );

  return { dueCount, estimatedMinutes, byChapter };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  generateFsrsPlannerTasks                                           */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/** Stable prefix so we can identify FSRS virtual tasks in the UI. */
const FSRS_TASK_ID_PREFIX = "fsrs-virtual-";

/**
 * Generate virtual planner tasks from FSRS due-card data.
 *
 * One task per chapter that has due cards, so the user sees
 * "مرور ۱۲ کارت — آناتومی کلیه" as a single actionable task.
 *
 * These tasks are NOT persisted in study_tasks — they are computed
 * on every page load and merged into the bucket view.
 */
export function generateFsrsPlannerTasks(
  _userId?: string,
): BucketTask[] {
  const load = getDueFlashcardLoad(_userId);
  if (load.dueCount === 0) return [];

  const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);

  return load.byChapter
    .filter((c) => c.dueCount > 0)
    .map((c, idx) => ({
      id: `${FSRS_TASK_ID_PREFIX}${c.chapterId}`,
      taskType: taskType.flashcardReview,
      status: c.overdueCount > 0 ? "overdue" : "pending",
      title: `مرور ${c.dueCount} کارت — ${c.chapterTitle}`,
      description: c.newCount > 0
        ? `${c.newCount} کارت جدید، ${c.dueCount - c.newCount} مرور`
        : null,
      estimatedMinutes: c.estimatedMinutes,
      priority: c.overdueCount > 0 ? 1 : 0,
      sourceType: taskSourceType.fsrsDue,
      scheduledFor: today,
      ...(() => {
        const link = resolveVirtualTaskLink(taskType.flashcardReview, c.chapterId, c.chapterTitle);
        return { linkUrl: link.url, linkLabel: link.label };
      })(),
    }));
}

/**
 * Check whether a task ID belongs to a virtual FSRS task
 * (not persisted in the DB).
 */
export function isFsrsVirtualTask(taskId: string): boolean {
  return taskId.startsWith(FSRS_TASK_ID_PREFIX);
}

/**
 * Extract the chapter ID from a virtual FSRS task ID.
 */
export function chapterIdFromFsrsTask(taskId: string): string | null {
  if (!isFsrsVirtualTask(taskId)) return null;
  return taskId.slice(FSRS_TASK_ID_PREFIX.length);
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\lib\planner\concept-links.ts
====================================================================================================

/**
 * Concept Links — resolves study task links into navigable URLs
 * and human-readable labels for the planner UI.
 *
 * Works with both persisted tasks (via StudyTaskWithLinksResolved)
 * and virtual tasks (FSRS / weak-area) by extracting chapter IDs from
 * their synthetic task IDs.
 */

import type { StudyTaskWithLinksResolved } from "@/lib/db/queries/planner";

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

export interface TaskLinkInfo {
  url: string;
  label: string;
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Route builders                                                     */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Build a URL for a linked study entity.
 */
export function getStudyTargetUrl(
  linkType: "chapter" | "chunk" | "question" | "flashcard" | "exam" | "notebook" | "weak_area",
  linkRefId: string,
): string {
  switch (linkType) {
    case "chapter":
      return `/qbank?chapterId=${encodeURIComponent(linkRefId)}`;
    case "chunk":
      return `/qbank?chunkId=${encodeURIComponent(linkRefId)}`;
    case "question":
      return `/qbank?questionId=${encodeURIComponent(linkRefId)}`;
    case "flashcard":
      return `/flashcards?cardId=${encodeURIComponent(linkRefId)}`;
    case "exam":
      return `/exam/${encodeURIComponent(linkRefId)}`;
    case "notebook":
      return `/notebooks/${encodeURIComponent(linkRefId)}`;
    case "weak_area":
      // Navigate to analytics/qbank filtered by chapter
      return `/qbank?chapterId=${encodeURIComponent(linkRefId)}`;
    default:
      return "/planner";
  }
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  resolveTaskLinkInfo — for persisted tasks                          */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Extract the best link (URL + label) from a fully resolved task.
 *
 * Priority: linkedChapter > linkedChunk > linkedExamSession > task type fallback
 */
export function resolveTaskLinkInfo(
  task: StudyTaskWithLinksResolved,
): TaskLinkInfo | null {
  // Chapter link
  if (task.linkedChapter) {
    return {
      url: getStudyTargetUrl("chapter", task.linkedChapter.id),
      label: task.linkedChapter.title,
    };
  }

  // Chunk link (with title fallback)
  if (task.linkedChunk) {
    return {
      url: getStudyTargetUrl("chunk", task.linkedChunk.id),
      label: task.linkedChunk.title ?? `بخش ${task.linkedChunk.chunkIndex}`,
    };
  }

  // Exam session link
  if (task.linkedExamSession) {
    return {
      url: getStudyTargetUrl("exam", task.linkedExamSession.id),
      label: task.linkedExamSession.title ?? "آزمون",
    };
  }

  // originRef fallback (task-level, no batch resolution needed)
  if (task.originRefType && task.originRefId) {
    const type = task.originRefType as Parameters<typeof getStudyTargetUrl>[0];
    return {
      url: getStudyTargetUrl(type, task.originRefId),
      label: getOriginLabel(task.originRefType),
    };
  }

  // Task-type fallback — generic route
  return getTaskTypeFallbackLink(task.taskType);
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  resolveVirtualTaskLink — for FSRS / weak-area virtual tasks        */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

/**
 * Build a link for a virtual (non-persisted) task given its chapter ID.
 * Virtual tasks always link to the chapter (qbank or flashcards).
 */
export function resolveVirtualTaskLink(
  taskType: string,
  chapterId: string,
  chapterTitle: string,
): TaskLinkInfo {
  if (taskType === "flashcard_review") {
    return {
      url: `/flashcards?chapterId=${encodeURIComponent(chapterId)}`,
      label: chapterTitle,
    };
  }
  // weak_area_review → qbank for that chapter
  return {
    url: getStudyTargetUrl("chapter", chapterId),
    label: chapterTitle,
  };
}

/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
/*  Helpers                                                            */
/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

function getOriginLabel(refType: string): string {
  const map: Record<string, string> = {
    chapter: "فصل",
    chunk: "بخش",
    question: "سؤال",
    flashcard: "فلش‌کارت",
    weak_area: "نقطه ضعف",
    concept: "مفهوم",
  };
  return map[refType] ?? refType;
}

export function getTaskTypeFallbackLink(taskType: string): TaskLinkInfo | null {
  const map: Record<string, TaskLinkInfo> = {
    chapter_read: { url: "/qbank", label: "بانک سؤال" },
    chunk_review: { url: "/qbank", label: "بانک سؤال" },
    question_block: { url: "/qbank", label: "بانک سؤال" },
    flashcard_review: { url: "/flashcards", label: "فلش‌کارت‌ها" },
    exam_block: { url: "/history", label: "تاریخچه آزمون" },
    notebook_review: { url: "/notebooks", label: "نوت‌بوک‌ها" },
    weak_area_review: { url: "/qbank", label: "بانک سؤال" },
  };
  return map[taskType] ?? null;
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\lib\services\planner-service.ts
====================================================================================================

/**
 * Planner Service — orchestrates study plan lifecycle and daily study workflows.
 *
 * Business logic layer for the study planner. Delegates all DB access to the
 * planner query layer. Pages and routes should call this service, never the
 * query layer directly.
 *
 * Key responsibilities:
 * - Plan generation (daily / weekly / custom)
 * - Task lifecycle (complete, skip, move, reschedule)
 * - Overdue handling and catch-up blocks
 * - Progress recalculation and streak tracking
 */

import {
  taskType,
  taskStatus,
  planStatus,
  dayOfWeek,
  type taskEventKind,
} from "@/db/schema";

import {
  // Plan reads
  getActivePlan,
  getPlanById,
  getPlanWithDays,
  getPlanSummary,
  listPlans,
  // Plan writes
  createPlan,
  updatePlan,
  deletePlan,
  recalcPlanProgress,
  // Day reads
