/* ================================================================== */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ================================================================== */

type DayOfWeekValue = (typeof dayOfWeek)[keyof typeof dayOfWeek];

/** Input for creating a new study plan. */
export interface CreatePlanParams {
  title: string;
  description?: string;
  startDate: string; // ISO date YYYY-MM-DD
  endDate?: string; // ISO date YYYY-MM-DD
  chapterIds: string[];
  /** Which days of week are rest days (default: Friday). */
  restDays?: DayOfWeekValue[];
  /** Daily study budget in minutes (default: from settings or 120). */
  dailyMinutes?: number;
  /** Task types to include. Default: all applicable. */
  includeTaskTypes?: TaskTypeValue[];
  /** Goal overrides per chapter. */
  goalJson?: Record<string, unknown>;
  /** Repeat pattern like "weekly" or "custom". */
  repeatPattern?: string;
}

/** A single task blueprint for plan generation. */
export interface TaskBlueprint {
  taskType: TaskTypeValue;
  title: string;
  description?: string;
  estimatedMinutes: number;
  priority: number; // 0=normal, 1=high, 2=critical
  targetCount?: number;
  /** Content to link to this task. */
  links: TaskLinkBlueprint[];
}

export interface TaskLinkBlueprint {
  chapterId?: string;
  chunkId?: string;
  questionId?: string;
  flashcardId?: string;
  examSessionId?: string;
  metadataJson?: Record<string, unknown> | null;
}

/** Result of plan generation. */
export interface GeneratePlanResult {
  plan: StudyPlan;
  daysCreated: number;
  tasksCreated: number;
  linksCreated: number;
}

/** Result of daily plan generation. */
export interface GenerateDailyPlanResult {
  day: StudyPlanDay;
  tasksCreated: number;
  linksCreated: number;
}

/** Result of carry-over operation. */
export interface CarryOverResult {
  carriedTasks: number;
  targetDay: StudyPlanDay;
}

/** Result of catch-up block creation. */
export interface CatchUpBlockResult {
  day: StudyPlanDay;
  tasksCreated: number;
  linksCreated: number;
  overdueProcessed: number;
}

/** Result of moving a task to another day. */
export interface MoveTaskResult {
  task: StudyTask;
  fromDayId: string;
  toDayId: string;
}

/** Result of recalculation. */
export interface RecalcResult {
  planId: string;
  totalTasks: number;
  completedTasks: number;
  progressPercent: number;
  daysRecalculated: number;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Helpers                                                            */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Generate a prefixed unique ID. */
function generateId(prefix: string): string {
  return `${prefix}_${Date.now().toString(36)}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`;
}

/** Parse ISO date to a Date object (midnight local). */
function parseDate(iso: string): Date {
  const [y, m, d] = iso.split("-").map(Number);
  return new Date(y, m - 1, d);
}

/** ISO date from a Date. */
function toISODate(d: Date): string {
  const y = d.getFullYear();
  const m = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0");
  const day = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, "0");
  return `${y}-${m}-${day}`;
}

/** Map JS day index (0=Sun) to our dayOfWeek value. */
const JS_DAY_TO_DOW: DayOfWeekValue[] = [
  dayOfWeek.sunday,
  dayOfWeek.monday,
  dayOfWeek.tuesday,
  dayOfWeek.wednesday,
  dayOfWeek.thursday,
  dayOfWeek.friday,
  dayOfWeek.saturday,
];

function getDayOfWeek(d: Date): DayOfWeekValue {
  return JS_DAY_TO_DOW[d.getDay()];
}

/** Add N days to a date (pure, returns new Date). */
function addDays(d: Date, n: number): Date {
  const result = new Date(d);
  result.setDate(result.getDate() + n);
  return result;
}

/** End-of-day timestamp for a given ISO date. */
function endOfDayMs(isoDate: string): number {
  const d = parseDate(isoDate);
  d.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
  return d.getTime();
}

/** Default rest days if none specified: Friday. */
const DEFAULT_REST_DAYS: DayOfWeekValue[] = [dayOfWeek.friday];

/* ================================================================== */
/*  PLAN GENERATION                                                    */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Generate a full study plan with days and tasks over a date range.
 *
 * Strategy:
 * 1. Create the plan container
 * 2. Create day records for each calendar day (marking rest days)
 * 3. Distribute chapter tasks across non-rest days
 * 4. Create task links pointing to chapters/chunks
 * 5. Recalculate aggregates
 */
export function generateWeeklyPlan(params: CreatePlanParams): GeneratePlanResult {
  const settings = getSettings();
  const dailyBudget = params.dailyMinutes ?? settings?.defaultTaskDurationMinutes ?? 120;
  const restDays = params.restDays ?? (settings?.restDaysJson as DayOfWeekValue[] | null) ?? DEFAULT_REST_DAYS;

  // Resolve chapters
  const selectedChapters = params.chapterIds
    .map((id) => getChapterById(id))
    .filter((ch): ch is Chapter => ch !== undefined);

  if (selectedChapters.length === 0) {
    throw new Error("No valid chapters selected for plan generation.");
  }

  // Determine date range
  const startDate = params.startDate;
  const endDate = params.endDate ?? computeEndDate(startDate, selectedChapters.length, restDays);

  // Deactivate any existing active plan
  const currentActive = getActivePlan();
  if (currentActive) {
    updatePlan(currentActive.id, { status: planStatus.paused });
  }

  // Create plan
  const plan = createPlan({
    id: generateId("plan"),
    title: params.title,
    description: params.description ?? null,
    status: planStatus.active,
    startDate,
    endDate,
    selectedChapterIdsJson: params.chapterIds,
    goalJson: params.goalJson ?? null,
    repeatPattern: params.repeatPattern ?? null,
  });

  // Generate days
  const dayRows = generateDayRows(plan.id, startDate, endDate, restDays);
  createDaysBatch(dayRows);

  // Get study days (non-rest)
  const studyDays = dayRows.filter((d) => !d.isRestDay);

  // Generate task blueprints from chapters
  const includeTypes = params.includeTaskTypes ?? [
    taskType.chapterRead,
    taskType.chunkReview,
    taskType.questionBlock,
    taskType.flashcardReview,
  ];
  const blueprints = generateBlueprintsFromChapters(selectedChapters, includeTypes, dailyBudget);

  // Distribute tasks across study days
  const { tasksCreated, linksCreated } = distributeTasksAcrossDays(
    plan.id,
    studyDays,
    blueprints,
    dailyBudget,
  );

  // Recalculate all day and plan aggregates
  for (const d of dayRows) {
    recalcDayProgress(d.id);
  }
  recalcPlanProgress(plan.id);

  return {
    plan: getPlanById(plan.id)!,
    daysCreated: dayRows.length,
    tasksCreated,
    linksCreated,
  };
}

/**
 * Generate a single day's plan on the fly (for dynamic planning).
 *
 * Useful when the user hasn't pre-planned the whole week but wants
 * today's tasks generated from their selected chapters and settings.
 */
export function generateDailyPlan(
  planId: string,
  date: string,
  chapterIds?: string[],
): GenerateDailyPlanResult {
  const plan = getPlanById(planId);
  if (!plan) throw new Error(`Plan ${planId} not found.`);

  // Check if day already exists
  const existingDay = getDayByDate(planId, date);
  if (existingDay) {
    const existingTasks = listTasksByDay(existingDay.id);
    if (existingTasks.length > 0) {
      throw new Error(`Day ${date} already has ${existingTasks.length} tasks. Use carryOverOverdueTasks() or createCatchUpBlock() to modify.`);
    }
  }

  const settings = getSettings();
  const dailyBudget = settings?.defaultTaskDurationMinutes ?? 120;
  const restDays = (settings?.restDaysJson as DayOfWeekValue[] | null) ?? DEFAULT_REST_DAYS;

  // Check if this is a rest day
  const dayDate = parseDate(date);
  const dow = getDayOfWeek(dayDate);
  const isRest = restDays.includes(dow);

  // Create or reuse day
  const day = existingDay ?? createDay({
    id: generateId("day"),
    planId,
    date,
    dayOfWeek: dow,
    isRestDay: isRest ? 1 : 0,
  });

  if (isRest) {
    return { day, tasksCreated: 0, linksCreated: 0 };
  }

  // Resolve chapters
  const chapIds = chapterIds ?? (plan.selectedChapterIdsJson as string[] | null) ?? [];
  const chapters = chapIds
    .map((id) => getChapterById(id))
    .filter((ch): ch is Chapter => ch !== undefined);

  if (chapters.length === 0) {
    return { day, tasksCreated: 0, linksCreated: 0 };
  }

  // Generate blueprints
  const blueprints = generateBlueprintsFromChapters(
    chapters,
    [taskType.chapterRead, taskType.chunkReview, taskType.questionBlock, taskType.flashcardReview],
    dailyBudget,
  );

  // Take only enough to fill one day's budget
  const oneDayBlueprints = fitBlueprintsToDay(blueprints, dailyBudget);

  // Create tasks
  let tasksCreated = 0;
  let linksCreated = 0;

  for (let i = 0; i < oneDayBlueprints.length; i++) {
    const bp = oneDayBlueprints[i];
    const { linkCount } = insertTaskFromBlueprint(plan.id, day.id, bp, i);
    tasksCreated++;
    linksCreated += linkCount;
  }

  recalcDayProgress(day.id);
  recalcPlanProgress(planId);

  return { day, tasksCreated, linksCreated };
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  TASK LIFECYCLE                                                     */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Mark a task as complete with optional actual time and result data.
 *
 * Also updates the day and plan aggregates and tracks the streak.
 */
export function markTaskComplete(
  taskId: string,
  actualMinutes?: number,
  resultJson?: Record<string, unknown>,
): StudyTask {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} not found.`);
  const completionBlockedStatuses: TaskStatusValue[] = ["completed", "skipped", "rescheduled"];
  if (completionBlockedStatuses.includes(task.status as TaskStatusValue)) {
    throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} has status "${task.status}" and cannot be completed.`);
  }

  const result = qCompleteTask(taskId, actualMinutes, resultJson);
  if (!result) throw new Error(`Failed to complete task ${taskId}.`);

  // Recalculate aggregates
  recalcDayProgress(task.dayId);
  recalcPlanProgress(task.planId);

  // Update streak
  updateStreak();

  return result;
}

/**
 * Mark a task as skipped.
 *
 * Skipped tasks count as "done" for scheduling but not for success metrics.
 */
export function markTaskSkipped(taskId: string): StudyTask {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} not found.`);

  const terminalStatuses: TaskStatusValue[] = ["completed", "skipped", "rescheduled"];
  if (terminalStatuses.includes(task.status as TaskStatusValue)) {
    throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} has status "${task.status}" and cannot be skipped.`);
  }

  const result = qSkipTask(taskId);
  if (!result) throw new Error(`Failed to skip task ${taskId}.`);

  recalcDayProgress(task.dayId);
  recalcPlanProgress(task.planId);

  return result;
}

/**
 * Start a task (transition: pending/overdue → in_progress).
 */
export function startTaskWork(taskId: string): StudyTask {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} not found.`);

  if (task.status !== "pending" && task.status !== "overdue") {
    throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} has status "${task.status}" and cannot be started.`);
  }

  const result = qStartTask(taskId);
  if (!result) throw new Error(`Failed to start task ${taskId}.`);

  return result;
}

/**
 * Move a task from one day to another (within the same plan).
 *
 * Unlike reschedule, this is a simple move — the original task is updated
 * in place rather than creating a copy. Use this for drag-and-drop reordering.
 */
export function moveTask(
  taskId: string,
  targetDayId: string,
  sortOrder?: number,
): MoveTaskResult {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} not found.`);

  const targetDay = getDayById(targetDayId);
  if (!targetDay) throw new Error(`Target day ${targetDayId} not found.`);

  if (task.planId !== targetDay.planId) {
    throw new Error("Cannot move tasks between different plans.");
  }

  const fromDayId = task.dayId;

  // Determine sort order
  const newSortOrder = sortOrder ?? getNextSortOrder(targetDayId);

  const updated = updateTask(taskId, {
    dayId: targetDayId,
    sortOrder: newSortOrder,
  });
  if (!updated) throw new Error(`Failed to move task ${taskId}.`);

  // Log event
  createTaskEvent({
    id: generateId("evt"),
    taskId,
    eventKind: "rescheduled",
    payload: { action: "moved", fromDayId, toDayId: targetDayId },
    occurredAt: Date.now(),
  });

  // Recalculate both days
  recalcDayProgress(fromDayId);
  recalcDayProgress(targetDayId);
  recalcPlanProgress(task.planId);

  return { task: updated, fromDayId, toDayId: targetDayId };
}

/**
 * Reschedule a task to a different day by creating a copy on the target
 * day and marking the original as rescheduled.
 *
 * This preserves history: the original task stays with "rescheduled" status.
 */
export function rescheduleTask(
  taskId: string,
  targetDate: string,
): StudyTask {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} not found.`);

  const plan = getPlanById(task.planId);
  if (!plan) throw new Error(`Plan ${task.planId} not found.`);

  // Find or create the target day
  let targetDay = getDayByDate(plan.id, targetDate);
  if (!targetDay) {
    const date = parseDate(targetDate);
    targetDay = createDay({
      id: generateId("day"),
      planId: plan.id,
      date: targetDate,
      dayOfWeek: getDayOfWeek(date),
      isRestDay: 0,
    });
  }

  const result = qRescheduleTask(taskId, targetDay.id);
  if (!result) throw new Error(`Failed to reschedule task ${taskId}.`);

  // Recalculate
  recalcDayProgress(task.dayId);
  recalcDayProgress(targetDay.id);
  recalcPlanProgress(task.planId);

  return result;
}

/**
 * Update a task's progress (e.g., completed 15 of 20 questions).
 */
export function updateTaskProgress(
  taskId: string,
  completedCount: number,
  actualMinutes?: number,
): StudyTask {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} not found.`);

  const targetCount = task.targetCount ?? 0;
  const pct = targetCount > 0
    ? Math.min(100, Math.round((completedCount / targetCount) * 100))
    : 0;

  const updates: Partial<StudyTaskInsert> = {
    completedCount,
    progressPercent: pct,
  };
  if (actualMinutes !== undefined) updates.actualMinutes = actualMinutes;

  const updated = updateTask(taskId, updates);
  if (!updated) throw new Error(`Failed to update task progress.`);

  // Log event
  createTaskEvent({
    id: generateId("evt"),
    taskId,
    eventKind: "progress_updated",
    payload: { completedCount, targetCount, progressPercent: pct },
    occurredAt: Date.now(),
  });

  // Auto-complete if reached 100%
  if (pct >= 100 && task.status !== "completed") {
    return markTaskComplete(taskId, actualMinutes);
  }

  return updated;
}

/**
 * Add a note to a task.
 */
export function addTaskNote(taskId: string, noteText: string): StudyTask {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} not found.`);

  const existing = task.notesText ?? "";
  const separator = existing ? "\n---\n" : "";
  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
  const updated = updateTask(taskId, {
    notesText: `${existing}${separator}[${timestamp}]\n${noteText}`,
  });
  if (!updated) throw new Error(`Failed to add note to task ${taskId}.`);

  createTaskEvent({
    id: generateId("evt"),
    taskId,
    eventKind: "note_added",
    payload: { noteText, timestamp },
    occurredAt: Date.now(),
  });

  return updated;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  OVERDUE HANDLING                                                   */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Carry over all overdue tasks to today (or a specified target date).
 *
 * Overdue tasks from past days are moved to the target day, preserving
 * their links and priorities. Original tasks are marked as "rescheduled".
 */
export function carryOverOverdueTasks(
  targetDate?: string,
): CarryOverResult {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) throw new Error("No active plan found.");

  const target = targetDate ?? toISODate(new Date());
  const overdueTasks = listOverdueTasks(plan.id);

  if (overdueTasks.length === 0) {
    const day = getDayByDate(plan.id, target) ?? createDay({
      id: generateId("day"),
      planId: plan.id,
      date: target,
      dayOfWeek: getDayOfWeek(parseDate(target)),
      isRestDay: 0,
    });
    return { carriedTasks: 0, targetDay: day };
  }

  // Find or create the target day
  let targetDay = getDayByDate(plan.id, target);
  if (!targetDay) {
    targetDay = createDay({
      id: generateId("day"),
      planId: plan.id,
      date: target,
      dayOfWeek: getDayOfWeek(parseDate(target)),
      isRestDay: 0,
    });
  }

  const affectedDayIds = new Set<string>();
  let carried = 0;

  for (const task of overdueTasks) {
    affectedDayIds.add(task.dayId);

    // Use the query layer's reschedule which creates the copy + marks original
    qRescheduleTask(task.id, targetDay.id);
    carried++;
  }

  // Recalculate affected days
  for (const dayId of affectedDayIds) {
    recalcDayProgress(dayId);
  }
  recalcDayProgress(targetDay.id);
  recalcPlanProgress(plan.id);

  return {
    carriedTasks: carried,
    targetDay: getDayById(targetDay.id)!,
  };
}

/**
 * Create a catch-up study block from overdue tasks.
 *
 * Unlike carry-over (which just moves tasks), this creates a focused
 * catch-up day with prioritized tasks — highest priority first, capped
 * at the daily time budget.
 */
export function createCatchUpBlock(
  date: string,
  maxMinutes?: number,
): CatchUpBlockResult {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) throw new Error("No active plan found.");

  const settings = getSettings();
  const budget = maxMinutes ?? settings?.dailyGoalMinutes ?? 120;
  const overdueTasks = listOverdueTasks(plan.id);

  if (overdueTasks.length === 0) {
    throw new Error("No overdue tasks to create a catch-up block from.");
  }

  // Find or create the target day
  let day = getDayByDate(plan.id, date);
  if (!day) {
    day = createDay({
      id: generateId("day"),
      planId: plan.id,
      date,
      dayOfWeek: getDayOfWeek(parseDate(date)),
      label: "بلوک جبرانی", // "Catch-up block" in Persian
      isRestDay: 0,
    });
  }

  // Sort overdue tasks by priority (descending) then by original sort order
  const sorted = [...overdueTasks].sort((a, b) => {
    if (b.priority !== a.priority) return b.priority - a.priority;
    return a.sortOrder - b.sortOrder;
  });

  // Pick tasks that fit within budget
  let usedMinutes = 0;
  const pickedTasks: StudyTask[] = [];
  for (const t of sorted) {
    const est = t.estimatedMinutes || 30; // fallback
    if (usedMinutes + est > budget && pickedTasks.length > 0) break;
    pickedTasks.push(t);
    usedMinutes += est;
  }

  const affectedDayIds = new Set<string>();
  let tasksCreated = 0;
  let linksCreated = 0;

  for (let i = 0; i < pickedTasks.length; i++) {
    const original = pickedTasks[i];
    affectedDayIds.add(original.dayId);

    // Create new task in the catch-up day
    const newTask = createTask({
      id: generateId("task"),
      planId: plan.id,
      dayId: day.id,
      taskType: original.taskType as TaskTypeValue,
      status: "pending",
      title: original.title,
      description: original.description,
      sortOrder: i,
      estimatedMinutes: original.estimatedMinutes,
      targetCount: original.targetCount,
      priority: Math.min(original.priority + 1, 2), // bump priority
    });
    tasksCreated++;

    // Copy links
    const links = getTaskWithLinks(original.id)?.links ?? [];
    if (links.length > 0) {
      createTaskLinksBatch(
        links.map((l, idx) => ({
          id: generateId("lnk"),
          taskId: newTask.id,
          chapterId: l.chapterId,
          chunkId: l.chunkId,
          questionId: l.questionId,
          flashcardId: l.flashcardId,
          examSessionId: l.examSessionId,
          sortOrder: idx,
          metadataJson: l.metadataJson,
        })),
      );
      linksCreated += links.length;
    }

    // Mark original as rescheduled
    updateTask(original.id, {
      status: "rescheduled",
      rescheduledTo: day.id,
    });
    createTaskEvent({
      id: generateId("evt"),
      taskId: original.id,
      eventKind: "rescheduled",
      payload: { action: "catch_up", newTaskId: newTask.id, targetDate: date },
      occurredAt: Date.now(),
    });
  }

  // Recalculate
  for (const dayId of affectedDayIds) {
    recalcDayProgress(dayId);
  }
  recalcDayProgress(day.id);
  recalcPlanProgress(plan.id);

  return {
    day: getDayById(day.id)!,
    tasksCreated,
    linksCreated,
    overdueProcessed: pickedTasks.length,
  };
}

/**
 * Detect and mark overdue tasks in the active plan.
 *
 * Call this periodically (e.g., on app load, or from a cron-like mechanism)
 * to keep task statuses up to date.
 */
export function detectAndMarkOverdue(): { planId: string; markedCount: number } | null {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) return null;

  const markedCount = markOverdueTasks(plan.id);
  return { planId: plan.id, markedCount };
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  PROGRESS & AGGREGATES                                              */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Full recalculation of all day and plan aggregates.
 *
 * Use after bulk operations or data repair.
 */
export function recalculatePlannerProgress(planId?: string): RecalcResult {
  const targetPlanId = planId ?? getActivePlan()?.id;
  if (!targetPlanId) throw new Error("No plan found for recalculation.");

  const days = listDaysByPlan(targetPlanId);
  for (const day of days) {
    recalcDayProgress(day.id);
  }
  recalcPlanProgress(targetPlanId);

  const plan = getPlanById(targetPlanId)!;
  return {
    planId: targetPlanId,
    totalTasks: plan.totalTasks,
    completedTasks: plan.completedTasks,
    progressPercent: plan.progressPercent,
    daysRecalculated: days.length,
  };
}

/**
 * End-of-day routine: detect overdue, update streak, recalculate.
 *
 * Call once per day (e.g., at midnight or on first app open of the day).
 */
export function endOfDayRoutine(): {
  overdue: number;
  recalc: RecalcResult | null;
} {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) return { overdue: 0, recalc: null };

  const overdue = markOverdueTasks(plan.id);
  updateStreak();
  const recalc = recalculatePlannerProgress(plan.id);

  return { overdue, recalc };
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  PLAN MANAGEMENT                                                    */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Activate a plan (pausing any currently active plan).
 */
export function activatePlan(planId: string): StudyPlan {
  const plan = getPlanById(planId);
  if (!plan) throw new Error(`Plan ${planId} not found.`);

  if (plan.status === "active") return plan;

  // Pause current active
  const current = getActivePlan();
  if (current && current.id !== planId) {
    updatePlan(current.id, { status: planStatus.paused });
  }

  const updated = updatePlan(planId, { status: planStatus.active });
  if (!updated) throw new Error(`Failed to activate plan ${planId}.`);

  // Update default plan in settings
  upsertSettings({ defaultPlanId: planId });

  return updated;
}

/**
 * Pause the active plan.
 */
export function pausePlan(planId: string): StudyPlan {
  const plan = getPlanById(planId);
  if (!plan) throw new Error(`Plan ${planId} not found.`);
  if (plan.status !== "active") throw new Error(`Plan is not active (status: ${plan.status}).`);

  const updated = updatePlan(planId, { status: planStatus.paused });
  if (!updated) throw new Error(`Failed to pause plan ${planId}.`);
  return updated;
}

/**
 * Complete a plan (marks it as completed, prevents further task changes).
 */
export function completePlan(planId: string): StudyPlan {
  const plan = getPlanById(planId);
  if (!plan) throw new Error(`Plan ${planId} not found.`);

  // Final recalculation
  recalculatePlannerProgress(planId);

  const updated = updatePlan(planId, { status: planStatus.completed });
  if (!updated) throw new Error(`Failed to complete plan ${planId}.`);
  return updated;
}

/**
 * Archive a plan.
 */
export function archivePlan(planId: string): StudyPlan {
  const plan = getPlanById(planId);
  if (!plan) throw new Error(`Plan ${planId} not found.`);

  const updated = updatePlan(planId, { status: planStatus.archived });
  if (!updated) throw new Error(`Failed to archive plan ${planId}.`);
  return updated;
}

/**
 * Delete a plan and all its data.
 */
export function removePlan(planId: string): void {
  const plan = getPlanById(planId);
  if (!plan) throw new Error(`Plan ${planId} not found.`);

  deletePlan(planId);

  // If this was the default plan, clear settings
  const settings = getSettings();
  if (settings?.defaultPlanId === planId) {
    upsertSettings({ defaultPlanId: null });
  }
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  SETTINGS                                                           */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Update planner settings.
 */
export function updatePlannerSettings(data: {
  dailyGoalMinutes?: number;
  preferredStartTime?: string;
  restDays?: DayOfWeekValue[];
  notificationsEnabled?: boolean;
  autoReschedule?: boolean;
  defaultTaskDurationMinutes?: number;
}): StudyPlannerSetting {
  return upsertSettings({
    dailyGoalMinutes: data.dailyGoalMinutes,
    preferredStartTime: data.preferredStartTime,
    restDaysJson: data.restDays,
    notificationsEnabled: data.notificationsEnabled !== undefined
      ? (data.notificationsEnabled ? 1 : 0)
      : undefined,
    autoReschedule: data.autoReschedule !== undefined
      ? (data.autoReschedule ? 1 : 0)
      : undefined,
    defaultTaskDurationMinutes: data.defaultTaskDurationMinutes,
  });
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  TASK CREATION (manual / ad-hoc)                                    */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Create a single task manually on a specific day.
 *
 * Useful for adding custom tasks, extra review sessions, etc.
 */
export function createManualTask(params: {
  planId: string;
  dayId: string;
  taskType: TaskTypeValue;
  title: string;
  description?: string;
  estimatedMinutes?: number;
  priority?: number;
  targetCount?: number;
  links?: TaskLinkBlueprint[];
}): StudyTask {
  const plan = getPlanById(params.planId);
  if (!plan) throw new Error(`Plan ${params.planId} not found.`);

  const day = getDayById(params.dayId);
  if (!day) throw new Error(`Day ${params.dayId} not found.`);

  if (day.planId !== params.planId) {
    throw new Error("Day does not belong to the specified plan.");
  }

  const sortOrder = getNextSortOrder(params.dayId);

  const task = createTask({
    id: generateId("task"),
    planId: params.planId,
    dayId: params.dayId,
    taskType: params.taskType,
    status: "pending",
    title: params.title,
    description: params.description ?? null,
    sortOrder,
    estimatedMinutes: params.estimatedMinutes ?? 30,
    targetCount: params.targetCount ?? null,
    priority: params.priority ?? 0,
  });

  // Create links if provided
  if (params.links && params.links.length > 0) {
    createTaskLinksBatch(
      params.links.map((l, i) => ({
        id: generateId("lnk"),
        taskId: task.id,
        chapterId: l.chapterId ?? null,
        chunkId: l.chunkId ?? null,
        questionId: l.questionId ?? null,
        flashcardId: l.flashcardId ?? null,
        examSessionId: l.examSessionId ?? null,
        sortOrder: i,
        metadataJson: l.metadataJson ?? null,
      })),
    );
  }

  // Log creation event
  createTaskEvent({
    id: generateId("evt"),
    taskId: task.id,
    eventKind: "created",
    payload: { source: "manual", taskType: params.taskType },
    occurredAt: Date.now(),
  });

  recalcDayProgress(params.dayId);
  recalcPlanProgress(params.planId);

  return task;
}

/**
 * Remove a single task.
 */
export function removeTask(taskId: string): void {
  const task = getTaskById(taskId);
  if (!task) throw new Error(`Task ${taskId} not found.`);

  const { dayId, planId } = task;
  deleteTask(taskId);

  recalcDayProgress(dayId);
  recalcPlanProgress(planId);
}

/**
 * Reorder tasks within a day.
 *
 * Accepts a list of task IDs in the desired order.
 */
export function reorderTasks(dayId: string, taskIds: string[]): void {
  for (let i = 0; i < taskIds.length; i++) {
    updateTask(taskIds[i], { sortOrder: i });
  }
  // No aggregate change needed for reordering.
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  INTELLIGENT PLAN GENERATION                                        */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Result of smart plan generation. */
export interface SmartPlanResult extends GeneratePlanResult {
  intelligence: OrchestratorIntelligence;
  remediationTasksCreated: number;
}

/** Result of smart daily plan generation. */
export interface SmartDailyPlanResult extends GenerateDailyPlanResult {
  intelligence: OrchestratorIntelligence;
  remediationTasksCreated: number;
}

/** Result of exam recovery plan creation. */
export interface ExamRecoveryResult {
  recovery: ExamRecoveryPlan;
  plan: StudyPlan;
  daysCreated: number;
  tasksCreated: number;
  linksCreated: number;
}

/**
 * Generate an intelligent weekly plan using the study orchestrator.
 *
 * Same interface as generateWeeklyPlan but enriched with:
 * - FSRS-driven flashcard tasks (actual due cards, not static 50)
 * - Remediation tasks for detected weak topics
 * - Adaptive workload balancing across days
 * - Priority-sorted interleaved task ordering
 */
export function generateSmartWeeklyPlan(
  params: CreatePlanParams,
): SmartPlanResult {
  const settings = getSettings();
  const dailyBudget =
    params.dailyMinutes ?? settings?.defaultTaskDurationMinutes ?? 120;
  const restDays =
    params.restDays ??
    (settings?.restDaysJson as DayOfWeekValue[] | null) ??
    DEFAULT_REST_DAYS;

  const selectedChapters = params.chapterIds
    .map((id) => getChapterById(id))
    .filter((ch): ch is Chapter => ch !== undefined);

  if (selectedChapters.length === 0) {
    throw new Error("No valid chapters selected for plan generation.");
  }

  // ---- Compute intelligence ----
  const intelligence = computeIntelligence(params.chapterIds, dailyBudget);

  // ---- Create plan container ----
  const startDate = params.startDate;
  const endDate =
    params.endDate ??
    computeEndDate(startDate, selectedChapters.length, restDays);

  const currentActive = getActivePlan();
  if (currentActive) {
    updatePlan(currentActive.id, { status: planStatus.paused });
  }

  const plan = createPlan({
    id: generateId("plan"),
    title: params.title,
    description: params.description ?? null,
    status: planStatus.active,
    startDate,
    endDate,
    selectedChapterIdsJson: params.chapterIds,
    goalJson: params.goalJson ?? null,
    repeatPattern: params.repeatPattern ?? null,
  });

  // ---- Generate days ----
  const dayRows = generateDayRows(plan.id, startDate, endDate, restDays);
  createDaysBatch(dayRows);
  const studyDays = dayRows.filter((d) => !d.isRestDay);

  // ---- Generate normal blueprints ----
  const includeTypes = params.includeTaskTypes ?? [
    taskType.chapterRead,
    taskType.chunkReview,
    taskType.questionBlock,
  ];
  // Exclude flashcard_review from normal — FSRS generates those
  const normalTypes = includeTypes.filter(
    (t) => t !== taskType.flashcardReview,
  );
  const normalBlueprints = generateBlueprintsFromChapters(
    selectedChapters,
    normalTypes,
    dailyBudget,
  );

  // ---- Build intelligent flashcard blueprints (FSRS-driven) ----
  const fsrsBlueprints = intelligence.remediationBlueprints.filter(
    (bp) => bp.source.type === "flashcard_due",
  );

  // ---- Build remediation task blueprints ----
  const remediationBlueprints = intelligence.remediationBlueprints.filter(
    (bp) => bp.source.type !== "flashcard_due",
  );

  // ---- Convert remediation to TaskBlueprint format ----
  const allBlueprints = [
    ...normalBlueprints,
    ...remediationToBlueprint(fsrsBlueprints),
    ...remediationToBlueprint(remediationBlueprints),
  ];

  // ---- Interleave for variety ----
  const normalBPs = allBlueprints.filter((bp) => bp.priority === 0);
  const priorityBPs = allBlueprints.filter((bp) => bp.priority > 0);
  const interleaved = interleaveTasks(priorityBPs, normalBPs);

  // ---- Distribute tasks across days ----
  const { tasksCreated, linksCreated } = distributeTasksAcrossDays(
    plan.id,
    studyDays,
    interleaved,
    dailyBudget,
  );

  // ---- Recalculate aggregates ----
  for (const d of dayRows) {
    recalcDayProgress(d.id);
  }
  recalcPlanProgress(plan.id);

  const remediationTasksCreated =
    remediationToBlueprint(intelligence.remediationBlueprints).length;

  return {
    plan: getPlanById(plan.id)!,
    daysCreated: dayRows.length,
    tasksCreated,
    linksCreated,
    intelligence,
    remediationTasksCreated,
  };
}

/**
 * Generate a single smart day plan using orchestrator intelligence.
 *
 * Enriches the day with FSRS flashcard tasks and remediation tasks
 * balanced against the daily budget.
 */
export function generateSmartDailyPlan(
  planId: string,
  date: string,
  chapterIds?: string[],
): SmartDailyPlanResult {
  const plan = getPlanById(planId);
  if (!plan) throw new Error(`Plan ${planId} not found.`);

  const existingDay = getDayByDate(planId, date);
  if (existingDay) {
    const existingTasks = listTasksByDay(existingDay.id);
    if (existingTasks.length > 0) {
      throw new Error(
        `Day ${date} already has ${existingTasks.length} tasks.`,
      );
    }
  }

  const settings = getSettings();
  const dailyBudget = settings?.defaultTaskDurationMinutes ?? 120;
  const restDays =
    (settings?.restDaysJson as DayOfWeekValue[] | null) ?? DEFAULT_REST_DAYS;

  const dayDate = parseDate(date);
  const dow = getDayOfWeek(dayDate);
  const isRest = restDays.includes(dow);

  const day =
    existingDay ??
    createDay({
      id: generateId("day"),
      planId,
      date,
      dayOfWeek: dow,
      isRestDay: isRest ? 1 : 0,
    });

  if (isRest) {
    return {
      day,
      tasksCreated: 0,
      linksCreated: 0,
      intelligence: computeIntelligence([], dailyBudget),
      remediationTasksCreated: 0,
    };
  }

  const chapIds =
    chapterIds ?? (plan.selectedChapterIdsJson as string[] | null) ?? [];
  const chapters = chapIds
    .map((id) => getChapterById(id))
    .filter((ch): ch is Chapter => ch !== undefined);

  if (chapters.length === 0) {
    return {
      day,
      tasksCreated: 0,
      linksCreated: 0,
      intelligence: computeIntelligence([], dailyBudget),
      remediationTasksCreated: 0,
    };
  }

  // ---- Intelligence ----
  const intelligence = computeIntelligence(chapIds, dailyBudget);
  const { budgetAllocation } = intelligence;

  // ---- Normal blueprints (without flashcards) ----
  const normalBlueprints = generateBlueprintsFromChapters(
    chapters,
    [
      taskType.chapterRead,
      taskType.chunkReview,
      taskType.questionBlock,
    ],
    budgetAllocation.normalStudyMinutes,
  );

  // ---- FSRS flashcard blueprints ----
  const fsrsBlueprints = remediationToBlueprint(
    intelligence.remediationBlueprints.filter(
      (bp) => bp.source.type === "flashcard_due",
    ),
  );

  // ---- Remediation blueprints ----
  const remBlueprints = remediationToBlueprint(
    intelligence.remediationBlueprints.filter(
      (bp) => bp.source.type !== "flashcard_due",
    ),
  );

  // ---- Interleave & fit to day ----
  const priorityBPs = [...fsrsBlueprints, ...remBlueprints].filter(
    (bp) => bp.priority > 0,
  );
  const normalBPs = [
    ...normalBlueprints,
    ...fsrsBlueprints.filter((bp) => bp.priority === 0),
    ...remBlueprints.filter((bp) => bp.priority === 0),
  ];
  const interleaved = interleaveTasks(priorityBPs, normalBPs);
  const oneDayBlueprints = fitBlueprintsToDay(interleaved, dailyBudget);

  // ---- Create tasks ----
  let tasksCreated = 0;
  let linksCreated = 0;

  for (let i = 0; i < oneDayBlueprints.length; i++) {
    const bp = oneDayBlueprints[i];
    const { linkCount } = insertTaskFromBlueprint(plan.id, day.id, bp, i);
    tasksCreated++;
    linksCreated += linkCount;
  }

  recalcDayProgress(day.id);
  recalcPlanProgress(planId);

  const remediationTasksCreated = oneDayBlueprints.filter((bp) =>
    bp.description?.includes("جبرانی") ||
    bp.description?.includes("SRS") ||
    bp.description?.includes("مجدد"),
  ).length;

  return {
    day,
    tasksCreated,
    linksCreated,
    intelligence,
    remediationTasksCreated,
  };
}

/**
 * Generate a recovery plan after a completed exam.
 *
 * Creates a dedicated study plan targeting chapters where the user
 * scored below the accuracy threshold.
 */
export function generateExamRecovery(
  examSessionId: string,
  opts?: {
    title?: string;
    startDate?: string;
    dailyMinutes?: number;
    accuracyThreshold?: number;
  },
): ExamRecoveryResult {
  const recovery = generateExamRecoveryPlan(
    examSessionId,
    opts?.accuracyThreshold ?? 70,
  );

  if (recovery.weakChapters.length === 0) {
    throw new Error(
      "No chapters below accuracy threshold — no recovery needed.",
    );
  }

  const settings = getSettings();
  const dailyBudget = opts?.dailyMinutes ?? settings?.defaultTaskDurationMinutes ?? 120;
  const startDate = opts?.startDate ?? toISODate(new Date());
  const restDays =
    (settings?.restDaysJson as DayOfWeekValue[] | null) ?? DEFAULT_REST_DAYS;

  // Estimate days needed
  const totalMinutes = recovery.totalEstimatedMinutes;
  const daysNeeded = Math.max(Math.ceil(totalMinutes / dailyBudget), 2);

  const endDate = computeEndDate(startDate, daysNeeded, restDays);

  // Pause current active plan
  const currentActive = getActivePlan();
  if (currentActive) {
    updatePlan(currentActive.id, { status: planStatus.paused });
  }

  // Create recovery plan
  const chapterIds = recovery.weakChapters.map((wc) => wc.chapterId);
  const plan = createPlan({
    id: generateId("plan"),
    title: opts?.title ?? `جبران آزمون — ${recovery.scorePercent}%`,
    description: `برنامه جبرانی خودکار بعد از آزمون (${recovery.weakChapters.length} فصل ضعیف)`,
    status: planStatus.active,
    startDate,
    endDate,
    selectedChapterIdsJson: chapterIds,
    goalJson: {
      type: "exam_recovery",
      examSessionId,
      weakChapters: recovery.weakChapters.map((wc) => ({
        chapterId: wc.chapterId,
        accuracy: wc.accuracy,
      })),
    },
    repeatPattern: null,
  });

  // Generate days
  const dayRows = generateDayRows(plan.id, startDate, endDate, restDays);
  createDaysBatch(dayRows);
  const studyDays = dayRows.filter((d) => !d.isRestDay);

  // Collect all remediation blueprints
  const allRemediation = recovery.weakChapters.flatMap(
    (wc) => wc.remediationBlueprints,
  );
  const blueprints = remediationToBlueprint(allRemediation);

  // Distribute across days
  const { tasksCreated, linksCreated } = distributeTasksAcrossDays(
    plan.id,
    studyDays,
    blueprints,
    dailyBudget,
  );

  // Recalculate
  for (const d of dayRows) {
    recalcDayProgress(d.id);
  }
  recalcPlanProgress(plan.id);

  return {
    recovery,
    plan: getPlanById(plan.id)!,
    daysCreated: dayRows.length,
    tasksCreated,
    linksCreated,
  };
}

/**
 * Get the current study intelligence snapshot for the active plan.
 *
 * Useful for the dashboard card to display weakness indicators,
 * FSRS workload, and budget allocation without generating a plan.
 */
export function getStudyIntelligence(): OrchestratorIntelligence | null {
  const activePlan = getActivePlan();
  if (!activePlan) return null;

  const chapterIds =
    (activePlan.selectedChapterIdsJson as string[] | null) ?? [];
  const settings = getSettings();
  const dailyBudget = settings?.dailyGoalMinutes ?? 120;

  return computeIntelligence(chapterIds, dailyBudget);
}

/**
 * Get weak topic analysis for the active plan's chapters.
 */
export function getWeakTopicReport(opts?: {
  lookbackDays?: number;
}): WeakTopicAnalysis | null {
  const activePlan = getActivePlan();
  if (!activePlan) return null;

  const chapterIds =
    (activePlan.selectedChapterIdsJson as string[] | null) ?? [];

  return detectWeakTopics({
    chapterIds,
    lookbackDays: opts?.lookbackDays ?? 90,
  });
}

/* ---- Internal: Convert RemediationBlueprint → TaskBlueprint ---- */

function remediationToBlueprint(
  remediations: RemediationBlueprint[],
): TaskBlueprint[] {
  return remediations.map((r) => ({
    taskType: r.taskType as TaskTypeValue,
    title: r.title,
    description: r.description,
    estimatedMinutes: r.estimatedMinutes,
    priority: r.priority,
    targetCount: r.targetCount,
    links: r.links.map((l) => ({
      chapterId: l.chapterId,
      chunkId: l.chunkId,
      questionId: l.questionId,
      flashcardId: l.flashcardId,
      examSessionId: l.examSessionId,
      metadataJson: l.metadataJson,
    })),
  }));
}
