/* ================================================================== */
/*  INTERNAL: Plan Generation Helpers                                  */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Compute a reasonable end date given chapter count and rest days. */
function computeEndDate(
  startDate: string,
  chapterCount: number,
  restDays: DayOfWeekValue[],
): string {
  // Rule of thumb: ~2 study days per chapter
  const studyDaysNeeded = Math.max(chapterCount * 2, 7);
  let added = 0;
  let current = parseDate(startDate);

  while (added < studyDaysNeeded) {
    current = addDays(current, 1);
    const dow = getDayOfWeek(current);
    if (!restDays.includes(dow)) {
      added++;
    }
  }

  return toISODate(current);
}

/** Generate day row insert objects for a date range. */
function generateDayRows(
  planId: string,
  startDate: string,
  endDate: string,
  restDays: DayOfWeekValue[],
): StudyPlanDayInsert[] {
  const rows: StudyPlanDayInsert[] = [];
  let current = parseDate(startDate);
  const end = parseDate(endDate);

  while (current <= end) {
    const iso = toISODate(current);
    const dow = getDayOfWeek(current);
    const isRest = restDays.includes(dow);

    rows.push({
      id: generateId("day"),
      planId,
      date: iso,
      dayOfWeek: dow,
      isRestDay: isRest ? 1 : 0,
    });

    current = addDays(current, 1);
  }

  return rows;
}

/**
 * Generate task blueprints from selected chapters.
 *
 * For each chapter, creates one or more blueprints based on the
 * included task types:
 * - chapter_read: One task per chapter
 * - chunk_review: One task per chunk within the chapter
 * - question_block: One task for the chapter's questions
 * - flashcard_review: One task for the chapter's flashcards
 */
function generateBlueprintsFromChapters(
  selectedChapters: Chapter[],
  includeTypes: TaskTypeValue[],
  _dailyBudget: number,
): TaskBlueprint[] {
  const blueprints: TaskBlueprint[] = [];

  for (const ch of selectedChapters) {
    const chTitle = ch.title;
    const chId = ch.id;

    // Chapter read task
    if (includeTypes.includes(taskType.chapterRead)) {
      blueprints.push({
        taskType: taskType.chapterRead,
        title: `مطالعه فصل: ${chTitle}`,
        description: `مطالعه کامل فصل ${ch.chapterNo}`,
        estimatedMinutes: 45,
        priority: 1,
        links: [{ chapterId: chId }],
      });
    }

    // Chunk review tasks
    if (includeTypes.includes(taskType.chunkReview)) {
      const chunkList = listChunksByChapter(chId);
      for (const chunk of chunkList) {
        blueprints.push({
          taskType: taskType.chunkReview,
          title: `مرور بخش: ${chunk.title ?? `بخش ${chunk.chunkIndex}`}`,
          description: `مرور بخش ${chunk.chunkIndex} از فصل ${ch.chapterNo}`,
          estimatedMinutes: 15,
          priority: 0,
          links: [{ chapterId: chId, chunkId: chunk.id }],
        });
      }
    }

    // Question block
    if (includeTypes.includes(taskType.questionBlock)) {
      blueprints.push({
        taskType: taskType.questionBlock,
        title: `تست فصل: ${chTitle}`,
        description: `پاسخ به سوالات فصل ${ch.chapterNo}`,
        estimatedMinutes: 30,
        priority: 0,
        targetCount: 20,
        links: [{ chapterId: chId }],
      });
    }

    // Flashcard review
    if (includeTypes.includes(taskType.flashcardReview)) {
      blueprints.push({
        taskType: taskType.flashcardReview,
        title: `مرور فلشکارت: ${chTitle}`,
        description: `مرور فلشکارت‌های فصل ${ch.chapterNo}`,
        estimatedMinutes: 20,
        priority: 0,
        targetCount: 50,
        links: [{ chapterId: chId }],
      });
    }
  }

  return blueprints;
}

/**
 * Distribute task blueprints across study days, respecting daily budget.
 *
 * Uses a round-robin approach: fill each day up to the daily budget,
 * then move to the next day.
 */
function distributeTasksAcrossDays(
  planId: string,
  studyDays: StudyPlanDayInsert[],
  blueprints: TaskBlueprint[],
  dailyBudget: number,
): { tasksCreated: number; linksCreated: number } {
  if (studyDays.length === 0 || blueprints.length === 0) {
    return { tasksCreated: 0, linksCreated: 0 };
  }

  let dayIndex = 0;
  let dayMinutes = 0;
  let tasksCreated = 0;
  let linksCreated = 0;
  let sortOrder = 0;

  for (const bp of blueprints) {
    // Advance to next day if current is full
    if (dayMinutes + bp.estimatedMinutes > dailyBudget && dayMinutes > 0) {
      dayIndex++;
      dayMinutes = 0;
      sortOrder = 0;

      // If we've exhausted all days, wrap around
      if (dayIndex >= studyDays.length) {
        dayIndex = 0;
      }
    }

    const day = studyDays[dayIndex];
    const { linkCount } = insertTaskFromBlueprint(planId, day.id, bp, sortOrder);

    tasksCreated++;
    linksCreated += linkCount;
    dayMinutes += bp.estimatedMinutes;
    sortOrder++;
  }

  return { tasksCreated, linksCreated };
}

/** Fit blueprints into a single day's budget (greedy). */
function fitBlueprintsToDay(
  blueprints: TaskBlueprint[],
  dailyBudget: number,
): TaskBlueprint[] {
  const result: TaskBlueprint[] = [];
  let usedMinutes = 0;

  // Prioritize higher priority tasks first
  const sorted = [...blueprints].sort((a, b) => b.priority - a.priority);

  for (const bp of sorted) {
    if (usedMinutes + bp.estimatedMinutes > dailyBudget && result.length > 0) break;
    result.push(bp);
    usedMinutes += bp.estimatedMinutes;
  }

  return result;
}

/** Create a task + links from a blueprint. */
function insertTaskFromBlueprint(
  planId: string,
  dayId: string,
  bp: TaskBlueprint,
  sortOrder: number,
): { task: StudyTask; linkCount: number } {
  const task = createTask({
    id: generateId("task"),
    planId,
    dayId,
    taskType: bp.taskType,
    status: "pending",
    title: bp.title,
    description: bp.description ?? null,
    sortOrder,
    estimatedMinutes: bp.estimatedMinutes,
    targetCount: bp.targetCount ?? null,
    priority: bp.priority,
  });

  let linkCount = 0;
  if (bp.links.length > 0) {
    createTaskLinksBatch(
      bp.links.map((l, i) => ({
        id: generateId("lnk"),
        taskId: task.id,
        chapterId: l.chapterId ?? null,
        chunkId: l.chunkId ?? null,
        questionId: l.questionId ?? null,
        flashcardId: l.flashcardId ?? null,
        examSessionId: l.examSessionId ?? null,
        sortOrder: i,
        metadataJson: l.metadataJson ?? null,
      })),
    );
    linkCount = bp.links.length;
  }

  // Log creation event
  createTaskEvent({
    id: generateId("evt"),
    taskId: task.id,
    eventKind: "created",
    payload: { source: "auto", taskType: bp.taskType },
    occurredAt: Date.now(),
  });

  return { task, linkCount };
}

/** Get the next available sort order for a day. */
function getNextSortOrder(dayId: string): number {
  const tasks = listTasksByDay(dayId);
  if (tasks.length === 0) return 0;
  return Math.max(...tasks.map((t) => t.sortOrder)) + 1;
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\lib\services\planner-recommendation-service.ts
====================================================================================================

/**
 * Planner Recommendation Service — bucketed study recommendations.
 *
 * Reads learning data (FSRS, exams, question attempts) via the study
 * orchestrator and transforms it into categorised recommendation objects
 * the planner UI can display and the user can accept/dismiss.
 *
 * Pure read + compute layer. Accepting a recommendation delegates to the
 * existing planner service to create a real task.
 */

import { db } from "@/db/index";
import { sql } from "drizzle-orm";

import {
  getActivePlan,
  getStudyIntelligence,
  createManualTask,
  generateExamRecovery,
  type TaskLinkBlueprint,
} from "@/lib/services/planner-service";

import {
  getTodayDay,
  createDay,
} from "@/lib/db/queries/planner";

import {
  estimateReviewWorkload,
  getDueCardsByChapter,
  getRetentionStats,
  type ChapterDueSummary,
} from "@/lib/services/fsrs-service";

import {
  listCompletedSessions,
  getExamResultsByChapter,
  type ExamResultsByChapter,
} from "@/lib/db/queries/exams";

import {
  detectWeakTopics,
  generateRemediationBlueprints,
  generateFsrsFlashcardBlueprints,
  type RemediationBlueprint,
  type WeakTopicSignal,
} from "@/lib/services/study-orchestrator-service";

import { getChapterById, type Chapter } from "@/lib/db/queries/chapters";

import type {
  StudyPlan,
  TaskTypeValue,
} from "@/lib/db/queries/planner";

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Recommendation bucket identifiers. */
export type RecommendationBucket =
  | "due_reviews"
  | "flashcard_lapses"
  | "missed_concepts"
  | "weak_areas"
  | "exam_prep"
  | "custom";

/** Action types a user can take on a recommendation. */
export type RecommendationActionType =
  | "add_to_planner"
  | "start_block"
  | "open_notebook"
  | "review_flashcards"
  | "snooze";

/** A user-facing action button on a recommendation card. */
export interface RecommendationAction {
  type: RecommendationActionType;
  /** Persian label for the button. */
  label: string;
  /** Navigation route (for start_block, open_notebook, review_flashcards). */
  href?: string;
  /** Primary action is visually emphasized. */
  primary?: boolean;
}

/** A single recommendation the user can accept or dismiss. */
export interface Recommendation {
  /** Deterministic id (stable across re-fetches for dedup). */
  id: string;
  /** Which bucket this belongs to. */
  bucket: RecommendationBucket;
  /** Persian label for the bucket. */
  bucketLabel: string;
  /** Task type that would be created. */
  taskType: TaskTypeValue;
  /** Display title (Persian). */
  title: string;
  /** Short description (Persian). */
  description: string;
  /** Estimated time in minutes. */
  estimatedMinutes: number;
  /** Priority 0=normal, 1=high, 2=critical. */
  priority: number;
  /** Target item count (questions, cards, etc.). */
  targetCount?: number;
  /** Human-readable reason WHY this is recommended (Persian). */
  reason: string;
  /** Available actions the user can take on this recommendation. */
  actions: RecommendationAction[];
  /** Links to content entities. */
  links: TaskLinkBlueprint[];
  /** Chapter title for display (resolved from first link). */
  chapterTitle?: string;
  /** Source metadata for traceability. */
  source: {
    type: "fsrs_due" | "exam_incorrect" | "exam_omitted" | "weak_topic" | "chronically_wrong" | "exam_recovery" | "flashcard_lapse" | "low_retention";
    examSessionId?: string;
    signalKey?: string;
    weaknessScore?: number;
  };
}

/** Bucketed recommendations returned to the UI. */
export interface RecommendationResult {
  buckets: {
    id: RecommendationBucket;
    label: string;
    description: string;
    recommendations: Recommendation[];
    totalCount: number;
  }[];
  /** Total recommendations across all buckets. */
  totalRecommendations: number;
  /** Active plan that tasks would be added to. */
  activePlan: { id: string; title: string } | null;
  computedAt: number;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Constants                                                          */
/* ================================================================== */

const BUCKET_META: Record<RecommendationBucket, { label: string; description: string }> = {
  due_reviews: {
    label: "مرورهای موعد",
    description: "فلشکارت‌هایی که طبق الگوریتم SRS نیاز به مرور دارند",
  },
  flashcard_lapses: {
    label: "کارت‌های لغزش‌دار",
    description: "فلشکارت‌هایی که بارها اشتباه مرور شده‌اند و نیاز به تقویت دارند",
  },
  missed_concepts: {
    label: "مفاهیم از دست رفته",
    description: "سوالاتی که در آزمون‌های اخیر اشتباه یا بدون پاسخ بودند",
  },
  weak_areas: {
    label: "نقاط ضعف",
    description: "موضوعاتی که عملکرد ضعیفی در آنها داشتید",
  },
  exam_prep: {
    label: "آمادگی آزمون",
    description: "برنامه جبرانی بر اساس نتایج آزمون‌های اخیر",
  },
  custom: {
    label: "تسک‌های سفارشی",
    description: "تسک‌هایی که خودتان اضافه می‌کنید",
  },
};

/** Max recommendations per bucket. */
const MAX_PER_BUCKET = 8;

/** Consider exams from the last N days for recommendations. */
const EXAM_LOOKBACK_DAYS = 30;

/** Chapters below this accuracy in an exam trigger remediation. */
const EXAM_WEAK_THRESHOLD = 70;

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Main: getRecommendations()                                         */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Compute all recommendation buckets for the active plan.
 *
 * Rule-based and fully transparent — no opaque ML.
 */
export function getRecommendations(): RecommendationResult {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  const chapterIds = plan
    ? (plan.selectedChapterIdsJson as string[] | null) ?? []
    : [];

  const recommendations: Recommendation[] = [];

  // 1. Due Reviews (FSRS)
  recommendations.push(...buildDueReviewRecommendations(chapterIds));

  // 2. Flashcard Lapses (frequently failed cards)
  recommendations.push(...buildFlashcardLapseRecommendations(chapterIds));

  // 3. Missed Concepts (recent exam incorrect/omitted)
  recommendations.push(...buildMissedConceptRecommendations(chapterIds));

  // 4. Weak Areas (question attempt analysis + retention data)
  recommendations.push(...buildWeakAreaRecommendations(chapterIds));

  // 5. Exam Prep (recovery plans from recent low-scoring exams)
  const bucketMap = new Map<RecommendationBucket, Recommendation[]>();
  for (const r of recommendations) {
    const list = bucketMap.get(r.bucket) ?? [];
    list.push(r);
    bucketMap.set(r.bucket, list);
  }

  const bucketOrder: RecommendationBucket[] = [
    "due_reviews",
    "flashcard_lapses",
    "missed_concepts",
    "weak_areas",
    "exam_prep",
    "custom",
  ];

  const buckets = bucketOrder.map((id) => {
    const meta = BUCKET_META[id];
    const items = bucketMap.get(id) ?? [];
    return {
      id,
      label: meta.label,
      description: meta.description,
      recommendations: items.slice(0, MAX_PER_BUCKET),
      totalCount: items.length,
    };
  });

  return {
    buckets,
    totalRecommendations: recommendations.length,
    activePlan: plan ? { id: plan.id, title: plan.title } : null,
    computedAt: Date.now(),
  };
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Bucket builders                                                    */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * 1. Due Reviews — FSRS flashcards that are due now.
 *
 * Groups by chapter and creates one recommendation per chapter.
 */
function buildDueReviewRecommendations(
  chapterIds: string[],
): Recommendation[] {
  const results: Recommendation[] = [];

  try {
    const dueSummary = getDueCardsByChapter();
    // Filter to plan chapters if available, otherwise show all
    const relevant =
      chapterIds.length > 0
        ? dueSummary.filter((d) => chapterIds.includes(d.chapterId))
        : dueSummary;

    for (const ch of relevant.sort((a, b) => b.dueCount - a.dueCount)) {
      if (ch.dueCount === 0) continue;
      if (results.length >= MAX_PER_BUCKET) break;

      const chapter = getChapterById(ch.chapterId);
      const chTitle = chapter?.title ?? ch.chapterId;

      results.push({
        id: `rec_due_${ch.chapterId}`,
        bucket: "due_reviews",
        bucketLabel: BUCKET_META.due_reviews.label,
        taskType: "flashcard_review",
        title: `مرور فلشکارت: ${chTitle}`,
        description: `${ch.dueCount} فلشکارت موعد مرور (${ch.overdueCount} عقب‌افتاده، ${ch.newCount} جدید)`,
        estimatedMinutes: ch.estimatedMinutes,
        priority: ch.overdueCount > 0 ? 1 : 0,
        targetCount: ch.dueCount,
        reason: ch.overdueCount > 0
          ? `${ch.overdueCount} کارت عقب‌افتاده — مرور سریع‌تر باعث حفظ بهتر می‌شود`
          : `${ch.dueCount} کارت طبق الگوریتم SRS آماده مرور هستند`,
        links: [{ chapterId: ch.chapterId }],
        chapterTitle: chTitle,
        actions: [
          { type: "review_flashcards", label: "مرور فلشکارت‌ها", href: "/flashcards", primary: true },
          { type: "add_to_planner", label: "اضافه به برنامه" },
        ],
        source: {
          type: "fsrs_due",
        },
      });
    }
  } catch {
    // FSRS data unavailable — skip gracefully
  }

  return results;
}

/**
 * 1b. Flashcard Lapses — chapters with many "Again" (rating=1) events.
 *
 * Queries recent flashcard reviews for lapse events (rating=1).
 * High lapse counts indicate persistent memory failures that need
 * targeted reinforcement beyond normal SRS scheduling.
 */
function buildFlashcardLapseRecommendations(
  chapterIds: string[],
): Recommendation[] {
  const results: Recommendation[] = [];

  try {
    const lookback = Date.now() - 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 30 days

    const rows = db.all<{
      chapter_id: string;
      lapse_count: number;
      card_count: number;
    }>(sql`
      SELECT
        f.chapter_id,
        COUNT(*) AS lapse_count,
        COUNT(DISTINCT fr.flashcard_id) AS card_count
      FROM flashcard_reviews fr
      INNER JOIN flashcards f ON fr.flashcard_id = f.id
      WHERE fr.rating = 1
        AND fr.reviewed_at >= ${lookback}
        AND f.is_suspended = 0
        AND f.is_archived = 0
      GROUP BY f.chapter_id
      HAVING lapse_count >= 3
      ORDER BY lapse_count DESC
    `);

    const relevant =
      chapterIds.length > 0
        ? rows.filter((r) => chapterIds.includes(r.chapter_id))
        : rows;

    for (const row of relevant) {
      if (results.length >= MAX_PER_BUCKET) break;

      const chapter = getChapterById(row.chapter_id);
      const chTitle = chapter?.title ?? row.chapter_id;

      // Enrich with retention data when available
      let retentionNote = "";
      try {
        const stats = getRetentionStats(row.chapter_id);
        if (stats.avgRetention > 0 && stats.avgRetention < 0.7) {
          retentionNote = ` — میانگین یادآوری ${Math.round(stats.avgRetention * 100)}%`;
        }
      } catch {
        // retention stats unavailable
      }

      results.push({
        id: `rec_lapse_${row.chapter_id}`,
        bucket: "flashcard_lapses",
        bucketLabel: BUCKET_META.flashcard_lapses.label,
        taskType: "flashcard_review",
        title: `تقویت حافظه: ${chTitle}`,
        description: `${row.card_count} کارت با ${row.lapse_count} بار لغزش در ۳۰ روز اخیر${retentionNote}`,
        estimatedMinutes: Math.min(row.card_count * 3, 30),
        priority: row.lapse_count >= 10 ? 2 : 1,
        targetCount: row.card_count,
        reason: `${row.lapse_count} بار رتبه «دوباره» در فلشکارت‌های فصل «${chTitle}» — نشانه ضعف در یادآوری این مفاهیم`,
        links: [{ chapterId: row.chapter_id }],
        chapterTitle: chTitle,
        actions: [
          { type: "review_flashcards", label: "مرور فلشکارت‌ها", href: "/flashcards", primary: true },
          { type: "open_notebook", label: "مطالعه دفترچه", href: "/notebooks" },
          { type: "add_to_planner", label: "اضافه به برنامه" },
        ],
        source: {
          type: "flashcard_lapse",
          signalKey: row.chapter_id,
          weaknessScore: Math.min(row.lapse_count * 10, 100),
        },
      });
    }
  } catch {
    // DB unavailable — skip gracefully
  }

  return results;
}

/**
 * 2. Missed Concepts — incorrect/omitted questions from recent exams.
 *
 * Scans completed exams from the last N days, finds chapters with
 * poor results, and generates review + re-attempt recommendations.
 */
function buildMissedConceptRecommendations(
  chapterIds: string[],
): Recommendation[] {
  const results: Recommendation[] = [];

  try {
    const cutoff = Date.now() - EXAM_LOOKBACK_DAYS * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    const recentExams = listCompletedSessions(20).filter(
      (e) => e.completedAt && e.completedAt >= cutoff,
    );

    for (const exam of recentExams) {
      const chapterResults = getExamResultsByChapter(exam.id);

      for (const ch of chapterResults) {
        if (ch.accuracy >= EXAM_WEAK_THRESHOLD) continue;
        if (chapterIds.length > 0 && !chapterIds.includes(ch.chapterId)) continue;
        if (results.length >= MAX_PER_BUCKET) break;

        const examTitle = exam.title ?? "آزمون";

        // Incorrect questions — review task
        if (ch.incorrect > 0) {
          results.push({
            id: `rec_missed_inc_${exam.id}_${ch.chapterId}`,
            bucket: "missed_concepts",
            bucketLabel: BUCKET_META.missed_concepts.label,
            taskType: "question_block",
            title: `مرور سوالات غلط: ${ch.chapterTitle}`,
            description: `${ch.incorrect} سوال اشتباه از ${examTitle} (دقت ${ch.accuracy}%)`,
            estimatedMinutes: Math.min(ch.incorrect * 3, 30),
            priority: ch.accuracy < 50 ? 2 : 1,
            targetCount: ch.incorrect,
            reason: `در آزمون «${examTitle}» ${ch.incorrect} سوال از فصل «${ch.chapterTitle}» اشتباه پاسخ داده شد`,
            links: [
              {
                chapterId: ch.chapterId,
                examSessionId: exam.id,
                metadataJson: {
                  source: "exam_incorrect",
                  accuracy: ch.accuracy,
                  incorrect: ch.incorrect,
                },
              },
            ],
            chapterTitle: ch.chapterTitle,
            actions: [
              { type: "start_block", label: "شروع بلوک سوال", href: "/qbank", primary: true },
              { type: "open_notebook", label: "مطالعه دفترچه", href: "/notebooks" },
              { type: "add_to_planner", label: "اضافه به برنامه" },
            ],
            source: {
              type: "exam_incorrect",
              examSessionId: exam.id,
            },
          });
        }

        // Omitted questions — study first, then attempt
        if (ch.omitted > 0) {
          results.push({
            id: `rec_missed_omit_${exam.id}_${ch.chapterId}`,
            bucket: "missed_concepts",
            bucketLabel: BUCKET_META.missed_concepts.label,
            taskType: "chunk_review",
            title: `مطالعه سوالات بی‌پاسخ: ${ch.chapterTitle}`,
            description: `${ch.omitted} سوال بدون پاسخ از ${examTitle}`,
            estimatedMinutes: Math.min(ch.omitted * 4, 30),
            priority: 1,
            targetCount: ch.omitted,
            reason: `${ch.omitted} سوال از فصل «${ch.chapterTitle}» در آزمون «${examTitle}» بدون پاسخ ماند — احتمالاً نیاز به مطالعه بیشتر دارید`,
            links: [
              {
                chapterId: ch.chapterId,
                examSessionId: exam.id,
                metadataJson: {
                  source: "exam_omitted",
                  omitted: ch.omitted,
                },
              },
            ],
            chapterTitle: ch.chapterTitle,
            actions: [
              { type: "open_notebook", label: "مطالعه دفترچه", href: "/notebooks", primary: true },
              { type: "start_block", label: "شروع بلوک سوال", href: "/qbank" },
              { type: "add_to_planner", label: "اضافه به برنامه" },
            ],
            source: {
              type: "exam_omitted",
              examSessionId: exam.id,
            },
          });
        }
      }
    }
  } catch {
    // Exam data unavailable — skip gracefully
  }

  return results;
}

/**
 * 3. Weak Areas — topics with consistently poor performance.
 *
 * Uses the orchestrator's weak-topic detection which analyses all
 * question attempts and computes composite weakness scores.
 */
function buildWeakAreaRecommendations(
  chapterIds: string[],
): Recommendation[] {
  const results: Recommendation[] = [];

  try {
    const analysis = detectWeakTopics({
      chapterIds: chapterIds.length > 0 ? chapterIds : undefined,
      maxSignals: MAX_PER_BUCKET,
      lookbackDays: 90,
    });

    const blueprints = generateRemediationBlueprints(analysis, {
      maxBlueprints: MAX_PER_BUCKET,
    });

    for (const bp of blueprints) {
      if (results.length >= MAX_PER_BUCKET) break;

      const firstLink = bp.links[0];
      const chapter = firstLink?.chapterId
        ? getChapterById(firstLink.chapterId)
        : undefined;

      const signalKey = bp.source.signalKey ?? "";
      const weaknessScore = (firstLink?.metadataJson as Record<string, unknown>)
        ?.weaknessScore as number | undefined;

      results.push({
        id: `rec_weak_${bp.taskType}_${signalKey}`,
        bucket: "weak_areas",
        bucketLabel: BUCKET_META.weak_areas.label,
        taskType: bp.taskType as TaskTypeValue,
        title: bp.title,
        description: bp.description,
        estimatedMinutes: bp.estimatedMinutes,
        priority: bp.priority,
        targetCount: bp.targetCount,
        reason: weaknessScore != null
          ? `امتیاز ضعف ${weaknessScore} از ۱۰۰ — بر اساس ${analysis.chronicallyWrongQuestionIds.length > 0 ? "اشتباهات مکرر و " : ""}تحلیل عملکرد`
          : `عملکرد ضعیف در حوزه «${signalKey}» شناسایی شد`,
        links: bp.links.map((l) => ({
          chapterId: l.chapterId,
          chunkId: l.chunkId,
          questionId: l.questionId,
          flashcardId: l.flashcardId,
          examSessionId: l.examSessionId,
          metadataJson: l.metadataJson,
        })),
        chapterTitle: chapter?.title,
        actions: [
          { type: "start_block", label: "شروع بلوک سوال", href: "/qbank", primary: true },
          { type: "review_flashcards", label: "مرور فلشکارت‌ها", href: "/flashcards" },
          { type: "add_to_planner", label: "اضافه به برنامه" },
        ],
        source: {
          type: bp.source.type === "chronically_wrong"
            ? "chronically_wrong"
            : "weak_topic",
          signalKey,
          weaknessScore: weaknessScore ?? undefined,
        },
      });
    }
  } catch {
    // Question data unavailable — skip gracefully
  }

  return results;
}

/**
 * 4. Exam Prep — recovery plan from recent low-scoring exams.
 *
 * Finds the most recent completed exam below 70% and generates
 * a comprehensive recovery blueprint.
 */
function buildExamPrepRecommendations(
  chapterIds: string[],
): Recommendation[] {
  const results: Recommendation[] = [];

  try {
    const cutoff = Date.now() - EXAM_LOOKBACK_DAYS * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    const recentExams = listCompletedSessions(10).filter(
      (e) =>
        e.completedAt &&
        e.completedAt >= cutoff &&
        e.scorePercent != null &&
        e.scorePercent < EXAM_WEAK_THRESHOLD,
    );

    for (const exam of recentExams.slice(0, 3)) {
      const chapterResults = getExamResultsByChapter(exam.id);
      const weakChapters = chapterResults
        .filter((ch) => ch.accuracy < EXAM_WEAK_THRESHOLD)
        .sort((a, b) => a.accuracy - b.accuracy);

      if (weakChapters.length === 0) continue;
      if (results.length >= MAX_PER_BUCKET) break;

      const examTitle = exam.title ?? "آزمون";
      const totalIncorrect = weakChapters.reduce(
        (s, ch) => s + ch.incorrect + ch.omitted,
        0,
      );

      // One high-level recovery recommendation per exam
      results.push({
        id: `rec_exam_prep_${exam.id}`,
        bucket: "exam_prep",
        bucketLabel: BUCKET_META.exam_prep.label,
        taskType: "question_block",
        title: `برنامه جبرانی: ${examTitle}`,
        description: `${weakChapters.length} فصل ضعیف — ${totalIncorrect} سوال نیاز به مرور (نمره ${exam.scorePercent}%)`,
        estimatedMinutes: Math.min(totalIncorrect * 3, 60),
        priority: 2,
        targetCount: totalIncorrect,
        reason: `نمره ${exam.scorePercent}% در آزمون «${examTitle}» — ${weakChapters.length} فصل زیر ${EXAM_WEAK_THRESHOLD}% دقت`,
        links: weakChapters.slice(0, 5).map((ch) => ({
          chapterId: ch.chapterId,
          examSessionId: exam.id,
          metadataJson: {
            source: "exam_recovery",
            accuracy: ch.accuracy,
            incorrect: ch.incorrect,
            omitted: ch.omitted,
          },
        })),
        chapterTitle: weakChapters.map((ch) => ch.chapterTitle).join("، "),
        actions: [
          { type: "start_block", label: "شروع بلوک سوال", href: "/qbank", primary: true },
          { type: "add_to_planner", label: "اضافه به برنامه" },
        ],
        source: {
          type: "exam_recovery",
          examSessionId: exam.id,
        },
      });
    }
  } catch {
    // Exam data unavailable — skip gracefully
  }

  return results;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  acceptRecommendation() — Create a planner task from a recommendation */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Accept a recommendation and create a real planner task for today.
 *
 * Delegates to `createManualTask` from the planner service so the
 * task goes through the standard creation pipeline (dueAt, events, etc.).
 */
export function acceptRecommendation(recommendation: Recommendation): {
  taskId: string;
  dayId: string;
} {
  const plan = getActivePlan();
  if (!plan) throw new Error("No active plan — cannot accept recommendation.");

  /* Resolve (or create) today's day inside the plan */
  let day = getTodayDay(plan.id);
  if (!day) {
    const today = new Date();
    const dowNames = [
      "sunday", "monday", "tuesday", "wednesday",
      "thursday", "friday", "saturday",
    ] as const;
    day = createDay({
      id: `day_${Date.now().toString(36)}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`,
      planId: plan.id,
      date: today.toISOString().slice(0, 10),
      dayOfWeek: dowNames[today.getDay()],
    });
  }

  const result = createManualTask({
    planId: plan.id,
    dayId: day.id,
    taskType: recommendation.taskType,
    title: recommendation.title,
    description: recommendation.description,
    estimatedMinutes: recommendation.estimatedMinutes,
    priority: recommendation.priority,
    targetCount: recommendation.targetCount,
    links: recommendation.links,
  });

  return { taskId: result.id, dayId: result.dayId };
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  getRecommendationCount() — Lightweight count for dashboard badge   */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Returns total recommendation count without the full payload.
 * Cheap enough to call from the dashboard summary.
 */
export function getRecommendationCount(): number {
  try {
    const result = getRecommendations();
    return result.totalRecommendations;
  } catch {
    return 0;
  }
}



====================================================================================================
FILE: src\lib\services\study-orchestrator-service.ts
====================================================================================================

/**
 * Study Orchestrator Service — intelligent study engine logic.
 *
 * Analyses question performance, flashcard retention, and exam results
 * to produce smart task blueprints for the planner. Combines:
 *
 * 1. Weak-topic detection (incorrect, repeated-wrong, slow, marked)
 * 2. Remediation task generation (targeted review + re-attempt)
 * 3. Post-exam recovery planning
 * 4. Adaptive workload balancing
 * 5. FSRS-aware flashcard scheduling hints
 *
 * Pure read + compute layer — never writes to the DB directly.
 * The planner service calls this to enrich plan generation.
 */

import { db } from "@/db/index";
import { sql } from "drizzle-orm";

import {
  listDueFlashcards,
  countFlashcards,
  type Flashcard,
} from "@/lib/db/queries/flashcards";

import {
  getExamSessionById,
  getExamResultsByChapter,
  type ExamSession,
  type ExamResultsByChapter,
} from "@/lib/db/queries/exams";

import {
  type Chapter,
} from "@/lib/db/queries/chapters";

import {
  estimateReviewWorkload,
  getDueCardsByChapter,
  type ChapterDueSummary,
  type ReviewWorkload,
} from "@/lib/services/fsrs-service";

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Types                                                              */
/* ================================================================== */

/* ---- Weak-topic detection ---- */

export interface WeakTopicSignal {
  /** Grouping dimension — subject, system, topic, or chapter. */
  dimension: "subject" | "system" | "topic" | "chapter";
  /** The value within that dimension (e.g. "Renal Physiology"). */
  key: string;
  /** Chapter ID if dimension is chapter, or most common chapter in group. */
  chapterId: string | null;
  /** Raw metrics. */
  totalAttempts: number;
  incorrectCount: number;
  omittedCount: number;
  slowCorrectCount: number;
  markedCount: number;
  repeatedWrongCount: number;
  /** Composite weakness score (0–100, higher = weaker). */
  weaknessScore: number;
}

export interface WeakTopicAnalysis {
  /** Top weak signals ordered by weakness score (descending). */
  signals: WeakTopicSignal[];
  /** Questions that were answered incorrectly multiple times. */
  chronicallyWrongQuestionIds: string[];
  /** Questions answered correctly but slowly (>90th pctl time). */
  slowCorrectQuestionIds: string[];
  /** Questions the user marked for later review. */
  markedQuestionIds: string[];
  /** Timestamp of the analysis. */
  analyzedAt: number;
}

/* ---- Remediation ---- */

export interface RemediationBlueprint {
  taskType: "chunk_review" | "question_block" | "flashcard_review";
  title: string;
  description: string;
  estimatedMinutes: number;
  priority: number; // 0=normal, 1=high, 2=critical
  targetCount?: number;
  links: RemediationLink[];
  /** Source signal that triggered this remediation. */
  source: {
    type: "weak_topic" | "exam_recovery" | "chronically_wrong" | "flashcard_due";
    signalKey?: string;
    examSessionId?: string;
  };
}

export interface RemediationLink {
  chapterId?: string;
  chunkId?: string;
  questionId?: string;
  flashcardId?: string;
  examSessionId?: string;
  metadataJson?: Record<string, unknown> | null;
}

/* ---- Exam recovery ---- */

export interface ExamRecoveryPlan {
  examSessionId: string;
  scorePercent: number;
  /** Chapters that scored below threshold. */
  weakChapters: Array<ExamResultsByChapter & { remediationBlueprints: RemediationBlueprint[] }>;
  /** Total remediation blueprints generated. */
  totalBlueprints: number;
  /** Estimated total minutes for recovery. */
  totalEstimatedMinutes: number;
}

/* ---- Adaptive balancing ---- */

export interface DailyBudgetAllocation {
  /** Target budget in minutes for this day. */
  totalMinutes: number;
  /** Minutes for flashcard reviews (FSRS-driven). */
  flashcardMinutes: number;
  /** Minutes for weak-topic remediation. */
  remediationMinutes: number;
  /** Minutes for normal study (chapter read, questions). */
  normalStudyMinutes: number;
  /** Minutes reserved as buffer / catch-up. */
  bufferMinutes: number;
}

/** Full intelligence payload returned to the planner service. */
export interface OrchestratorIntelligence {
  /** Weak topics detected from performance data. */
  weakTopics: WeakTopicAnalysis;
  /** FSRS review workload. */
  reviewWorkload: ReviewWorkload;
  /** Generated remediation blueprints (sorted by priority). */
  remediationBlueprints: RemediationBlueprint[];
  /** Budget allocation for today. */
  budgetAllocation: DailyBudgetAllocation;
  /** Timestamp. */
  computedAt: number;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Constants                                                          */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Weakness score weights. */
const W = {
  INCORRECT: 3,
  OMITTED: 1.5,
  SLOW_CORRECT: 1,
  MARKED: 0.5,
  REPEATED_WRONG: 5,
} as const;

/** Minimum attempts before a topic is considered for weakness. */
const MIN_ATTEMPTS_FOR_SIGNAL = 3;

/** Threshold for "slow correct" — seconds above this are slow. */
const SLOW_THRESHOLD_SECONDS = 120; // will also dynamically compute 90th pctl

/** Default exam recovery threshold (chapters below this % are remediated). */
const EXAM_RECOVERY_ACCURACY_THRESHOLD = 70;

/** Budget allocation ratios. */
const BUDGET = {
  /** Max fraction of daily budget for flashcard reviews. */
  MAX_FLASHCARD_RATIO: 0.35,
  /** Max fraction for remediation. */
  MAX_REMEDIATION_RATIO: 0.30,
  /** Min fraction for normal study. */
  MIN_NORMAL_RATIO: 0.25,
  /** Buffer fraction. */
  BUFFER_RATIO: 0.10,
} as const;

/* ================================================================== */
/*  1. WEAK-TOPIC DETECTION                                            */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Analyze question attempt history to find weak topics.
 *
 * Scans all question_attempts, groups by each taxonomy dimension
 * (subject, system, topic, chapter), and computes composite weakness scores.
 *
 * @param opts.lookbackDays  Only consider attempts from the last N days (default 90)
 * @param opts.maxSignals    Max signals to return per dimension (default 10)
 * @param opts.chapterIds    Restrict to these chapters (optional)
 */
export function detectWeakTopics(opts?: {
  lookbackDays?: number;
  maxSignals?: number;
  chapterIds?: string[];
}): WeakTopicAnalysis {
  const lookbackDays = opts?.lookbackDays ?? 90;
  const maxSignals = opts?.maxSignals ?? 10;
  const cutoff = Date.now() - lookbackDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;

  // ------ Compute dynamic slow threshold (90th percentile) ------
  const slowPctl = db.get<{ pctl: number | null }>(sql`
    SELECT time_spent_seconds AS pctl
    FROM question_attempts
    WHERE outcome = 'correct' AND time_spent_seconds > 0
      AND attempted_at >= ${cutoff}
    ORDER BY time_spent_seconds DESC
    LIMIT 1 OFFSET (
      SELECT CAST(COUNT(*) * 0.1 AS INTEGER)
      FROM question_attempts
      WHERE outcome = 'correct' AND time_spent_seconds > 0
        AND attempted_at >= ${cutoff}
    )
  `);
  const slowThreshold = Math.max(slowPctl?.pctl ?? SLOW_THRESHOLD_SECONDS, 60);

  // ------ Build chapter filter ------
  const chapterFilter =
    opts?.chapterIds && opts.chapterIds.length > 0
      ? sql`AND q.chapter_id IN (${sql.join(
          opts.chapterIds.map((id) => sql`${id}`),
          sql`, `,
        )})`
      : sql``;

  // ------ Per-question aggregation ------
  const perQuestion = db.all<{
    question_id: string;
    chapter_id: string;
    subject: string | null;
    system: string | null;
    topic: string | null;
    total: number;
    incorrect: number;
    omitted: number;
    correct_slow: number;
    marked: number;
  }>(sql`
    SELECT
      qa.question_id,
      q.chapter_id,
      q.subject,
      q.system,
      q.topic,
      COUNT(*) AS total,
      SUM(CASE WHEN qa.outcome = 'incorrect' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS incorrect,
      SUM(CASE WHEN qa.outcome = 'omitted' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS omitted,
      SUM(CASE WHEN qa.outcome = 'correct' AND qa.time_spent_seconds > ${slowThreshold} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS correct_slow,
      SUM(CASE WHEN qa.is_marked = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS marked
    FROM question_attempts qa
    JOIN questions q ON qa.question_id = q.id
    WHERE qa.attempted_at >= ${cutoff}
    ${chapterFilter}
    GROUP BY qa.question_id
  `);

  // ------ Chronically-wrong questions (incorrect ≥ 2 times) ------
  const chronicallyWrongQuestionIds: string[] = [];
  const slowCorrectQuestionIds: string[] = [];
  const markedQuestionIds: string[] = [];

  for (const pq of perQuestion) {
    if (pq.incorrect >= 2) chronicallyWrongQuestionIds.push(pq.question_id);
    if (pq.correct_slow > 0) slowCorrectQuestionIds.push(pq.question_id);
    if (pq.marked > 0) markedQuestionIds.push(pq.question_id);
  }

  // ------ Repeated-wrong: same question wrong in 2+ separate attempts ------
  const repeatedWrongMap = new Map<string, number>();
  for (const pq of perQuestion) {
    if (pq.incorrect >= 2) {
      repeatedWrongMap.set(pq.question_id, pq.incorrect);
    }
  }

  // ------ Aggregate by dimensions ------
  type DimKey = "subject" | "system" | "topic" | "chapter";
  const dimensions: DimKey[] = ["subject", "system", "topic", "chapter"];

  const allSignals: WeakTopicSignal[] = [];

  for (const dim of dimensions) {
    const groupMap = new Map<
      string,
      {
        chapterId: string | null;
        totalAttempts: number;
        incorrectCount: number;
        omittedCount: number;
        slowCorrectCount: number;
        markedCount: number;
        repeatedWrongCount: number;
        chapterVotes: Map<string, number>;
      }
    >();

    for (const pq of perQuestion) {
      const key =
        dim === "chapter"
          ? pq.chapter_id
          : (pq[dim] ?? null);
      if (!key) continue;

      const entry = groupMap.get(key) ?? {
        chapterId: dim === "chapter" ? pq.chapter_id : null,
        totalAttempts: 0,
        incorrectCount: 0,
        omittedCount: 0,
        slowCorrectCount: 0,
        markedCount: 0,
        repeatedWrongCount: 0,
        chapterVotes: new Map<string, number>(),
      };

      entry.totalAttempts += pq.total;
      entry.incorrectCount += pq.incorrect;
      entry.omittedCount += pq.omitted;
      entry.slowCorrectCount += pq.correct_slow;
      entry.markedCount += pq.marked;

      if (repeatedWrongMap.has(pq.question_id)) {
        entry.repeatedWrongCount += repeatedWrongMap.get(pq.question_id)!;
      }

      // Track most common chapter
      const cv = entry.chapterVotes.get(pq.chapter_id) ?? 0;
      entry.chapterVotes.set(pq.chapter_id, cv + pq.total);

      groupMap.set(key, entry);
    }

    for (const [key, data] of groupMap) {
      if (data.totalAttempts < MIN_ATTEMPTS_FOR_SIGNAL) continue;

      // Pick the most common chapter for this group
      let bestChapter = data.chapterId;
      if (!bestChapter && data.chapterVotes.size > 0) {
        let maxVotes = 0;
        for (const [chId, votes] of data.chapterVotes) {
          if (votes > maxVotes) {
            maxVotes = votes;
            bestChapter = chId;
          }
        }
      }

      // Compute composite weakness score (0–100)
      const errorRate = data.incorrectCount / data.totalAttempts;
      const omitRate = data.omittedCount / data.totalAttempts;
      const slowRate = data.slowCorrectCount / data.totalAttempts;
      const markRate = data.markedCount / data.totalAttempts;
      const repeatedRate = data.repeatedWrongCount / data.totalAttempts;

      const rawScore =
        errorRate * W.INCORRECT +
        omitRate * W.OMITTED +
        slowRate * W.SLOW_CORRECT +
        markRate * W.MARKED +
        repeatedRate * W.REPEATED_WRONG;

      // Normalize to 0–100 (max theoretical raw ≈ 11)
      const weaknessScore = Math.min(
        Math.round((rawScore / 11) * 100),
        100,
      );

      if (weaknessScore < 5) continue; // ignore trivially weak

      allSignals.push({
        dimension: dim,
        key,
        chapterId: bestChapter,
        totalAttempts: data.totalAttempts,
        incorrectCount: data.incorrectCount,
        omittedCount: data.omittedCount,
        slowCorrectCount: data.slowCorrectCount,
        markedCount: data.markedCount,
        repeatedWrongCount: data.repeatedWrongCount,
        weaknessScore,
      });
    }
  }

  // Sort by weakness score descending, take top N per dimension
  allSignals.sort((a, b) => b.weaknessScore - a.weaknessScore);

  const signalsByDim = new Map<DimKey, WeakTopicSignal[]>();
  const resultSignals: WeakTopicSignal[] = [];

  for (const sig of allSignals) {
    const dimList = signalsByDim.get(sig.dimension) ?? [];
    if (dimList.length >= maxSignals) continue;
    dimList.push(sig);
    signalsByDim.set(sig.dimension, dimList);
    resultSignals.push(sig);
  }

  return {
    signals: resultSignals,
    chronicallyWrongQuestionIds,
    slowCorrectQuestionIds,
    markedQuestionIds,
    analyzedAt: Date.now(),
  };
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  2. REMEDIATION TASK GENERATION                                     */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Generate remediation blueprints from weak topic signals.
 *
 * For each weak signal, produces targeted tasks:
 * - High weakness (score ≥ 60): chunk_review + question_block + flashcard_review
 * - Medium weakness (score 30–59): question_block + flashcard_review
 * - Low weakness (score < 30): question_block only
 */
export function generateRemediationBlueprints(
  analysis: WeakTopicAnalysis,
  opts?: {
    /** Max blueprints to generate (default 15). */
    maxBlueprints?: number;
    /** Only generate for these dimensions. */
    dimensions?: Array<"subject" | "system" | "topic" | "chapter">;
  },
): RemediationBlueprint[] {
  const maxBlueprints = opts?.maxBlueprints ?? 15;
  const dimensions = opts?.dimensions;
  const blueprints: RemediationBlueprint[] = [];

  // Filter signals
  let signals = analysis.signals;
  if (dimensions) {
    signals = signals.filter((s) => dimensions.includes(s.dimension));
  }

  // Deduplicate: if a chapter appears both as "chapter" and "topic" signal, keep higher
  const seen = new Set<string>();

  for (const sig of signals) {
    if (blueprints.length >= maxBlueprints) break;
    const dedupKey = `${sig.dimension}:${sig.key}`;
    if (seen.has(dedupKey)) continue;
    seen.add(dedupKey);

    const isHigh = sig.weaknessScore >= 60;
    const isMedium = sig.weaknessScore >= 30;
    const priorityLevel = isHigh ? 2 : isMedium ? 1 : 0;
    const label = sig.dimension === "chapter" ? sig.key : `${sig.dimension}: ${sig.key}`;

    // Chunk review (high weakness only)
    if (isHigh && sig.chapterId) {
      blueprints.push({
        taskType: "chunk_review",
        title: `مرور جبرانی: ${label}`,
        description: `مرور محتوای مرتبط با نقطه ضعف شناسایی‌شده (امتیاز ضعف: ${sig.weaknessScore})`,
        estimatedMinutes: 20,
        priority: priorityLevel,
        links: [
          {
            chapterId: sig.chapterId,
            metadataJson: {
              orchestratorSource: "weak_topic",
              dimension: sig.dimension,
              signalKey: sig.key,
              weaknessScore: sig.weaknessScore,
            },
          },
        ],
        source: { type: "weak_topic", signalKey: sig.key },
      });
    }

    // Question block (all levels)
    if (sig.chapterId) {
      const targetCount = isHigh ? 15 : isMedium ? 10 : 5;
      blueprints.push({
        taskType: "question_block",
        title: `تست جبرانی: ${label}`,
        description: `تمرین سوالات مرتبط با نقطه ضعف (${sig.incorrectCount} غلط از ${sig.totalAttempts} تلاش)`,
        estimatedMinutes: isHigh ? 25 : isMedium ? 20 : 15,
        priority: priorityLevel,
        targetCount,
        links: [
          {
            chapterId: sig.chapterId,
            metadataJson: {
              orchestratorSource: "weak_topic",
              dimension: sig.dimension,
              signalKey: sig.key,
              weaknessScore: sig.weaknessScore,
              incorrectQuestionIds: analysis.chronicallyWrongQuestionIds.slice(0, 20),
            },
          },
        ],
        source: { type: "weak_topic", signalKey: sig.key },
      });
    }

    // Flashcard review (medium+ weakness)
    if (isMedium && sig.chapterId) {
      blueprints.push({
        taskType: "flashcard_review",
        title: `فلشکارت جبرانی: ${label}`,
        description: `مرور فلشکارت‌های مرتبط با نقطه ضعف شناسایی‌شده`,
        estimatedMinutes: 15,
        priority: Math.max(priorityLevel - 1, 0),
        targetCount: 20,
        links: [
          {
            chapterId: sig.chapterId,
            metadataJson: {
              orchestratorSource: "weak_topic",
              dimension: sig.dimension,
              signalKey: sig.key,
            },
          },
        ],
        source: { type: "weak_topic", signalKey: sig.key },
      });
    }
  }

  // Add blueprints for chronically wrong questions (if not already captured)
  if (
    analysis.chronicallyWrongQuestionIds.length > 0 &&
    blueprints.length < maxBlueprints
  ) {
    // Look up the chapters of chronically wrong questions
    const wrongChapters = getChaptersForQuestions(
      analysis.chronicallyWrongQuestionIds.slice(0, 50),
    );

    for (const [chapterId, questionIds] of wrongChapters) {
      if (blueprints.length >= maxBlueprints) break;

      blueprints.push({
        taskType: "question_block",
        title: `تست مجدد سوالات اشتباه مکرر`,
        description: `${questionIds.length} سوال که بارها اشتباه پاسخ داده شده`,
        estimatedMinutes: Math.min(questionIds.length * 2, 30),
        priority: 2,
        targetCount: questionIds.length,
        links: questionIds.map((qId) => ({
          chapterId,
          questionId: qId,
          metadataJson: { orchestratorSource: "chronically_wrong" },
        })),
        source: { type: "chronically_wrong" },
      });
    }
  }

  return blueprints.sort((a, b) => b.priority - a.priority);
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  3. POST-EXAM RECOVERY PLANNING                                     */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Analyze a completed exam and generate a targeted recovery plan.
 *
 * @param examSessionId  The completed exam session to analyze.
 * @param accuracyThreshold  Chapters below this % accuracy get remediation (default 70).
 */
export function generateExamRecoveryPlan(
  examSessionId: string,
  accuracyThreshold: number = EXAM_RECOVERY_ACCURACY_THRESHOLD,
): ExamRecoveryPlan {
  const session = getExamSessionById(examSessionId);
  if (!session) throw new Error(`Exam session ${examSessionId} not found.`);
  if (session.status !== "completed") {
    throw new Error(`Exam session ${examSessionId} is not completed (status: ${session.status}).`);
  }

  const chapterResults = getExamResultsByChapter(examSessionId);
  const scorePercent = session.scorePercent ?? 0;

  const weakChapters = chapterResults
    .filter((ch) => ch.accuracy < accuracyThreshold)
    .sort((a, b) => a.accuracy - b.accuracy) // worst first
    .map((ch) => {
      const bps = generateExamChapterRemediation(ch, examSessionId);
      return { ...ch, remediationBlueprints: bps };
    });

  const allBlueprints = weakChapters.flatMap((wc) => wc.remediationBlueprints);
  const totalEstimatedMinutes = allBlueprints.reduce(
    (sum, bp) => sum + bp.estimatedMinutes,
    0,
  );

  return {
    examSessionId,
    scorePercent,
    weakChapters,
    totalBlueprints: allBlueprints.length,
    totalEstimatedMinutes,
  };
}

/** Generate remediation for one weak chapter from an exam. */
function generateExamChapterRemediation(
  ch: ExamResultsByChapter,
  examSessionId: string,
): RemediationBlueprint[] {
  const bps: RemediationBlueprint[] = [];
  const severity = ch.accuracy < 40 ? "critical" : ch.accuracy < 60 ? "high" : "moderate";

  // Priority based on severity
  const priority = severity === "critical" ? 2 : severity === "high" ? 1 : 0;

  // Chunk review for critical/high severity
  if (severity === "critical" || severity === "high") {
    bps.push({
      taskType: "chunk_review",
      title: `مرور فصل ${ch.chapterNo}: ${ch.chapterTitle}`,
      description: `مرور مجدد بعد از آزمون (دقت: ${ch.accuracy}% — ${ch.incorrect} اشتباه، ${ch.omitted} بدون پاسخ)`,
      estimatedMinutes: severity === "critical" ? 30 : 20,
      priority,
      links: [
        {
          chapterId: ch.chapterId,
          examSessionId,
          metadataJson: {
            orchestratorSource: "exam_recovery",
            examSessionId,
            accuracy: ch.accuracy,
            severity,
          },
        },
      ],
      source: { type: "exam_recovery", examSessionId },
    });
  }

  // Get incorrect question IDs from this exam for this chapter
  const incorrectQIds = getIncorrectQuestionIdsFromExam(
    examSessionId,
    ch.chapterId,
  );

  // Question block for incorrect questions
  if (incorrectQIds.length > 0) {
    bps.push({
      taskType: "question_block",
      title: `تست مجدد فصل ${ch.chapterNo}: ${ch.chapterTitle}`,
      description: `پاسخ مجدد به ${incorrectQIds.length} سوال اشتباه از آزمون`,
      estimatedMinutes: Math.min(incorrectQIds.length * 2, 40),
      priority,
      targetCount: incorrectQIds.length,
      links: incorrectQIds.map((qId) => ({
        chapterId: ch.chapterId,
        questionId: qId,
        examSessionId,
        metadataJson: { orchestratorSource: "exam_recovery" },
      })),
      source: { type: "exam_recovery", examSessionId },
    });
  }

  // Flashcard review for the chapter
  const flashcardCount = countFlashcards({ chapterId: ch.chapterId });
  if (flashcardCount > 0) {
    bps.push({
      taskType: "flashcard_review",
      title: `فلشکارت فصل ${ch.chapterNo}: ${ch.chapterTitle}`,
      description: `مرور ${Math.min(flashcardCount, 30)} فلشکارت بعد از آزمون`,
      estimatedMinutes: Math.min(Math.ceil(flashcardCount * 1.5), 30),
      priority: Math.max(priority - 1, 0),
      targetCount: Math.min(flashcardCount, 30),
      links: [
        {
          chapterId: ch.chapterId,
          metadataJson: { orchestratorSource: "exam_recovery", examSessionId },
        },
      ],
      source: { type: "exam_recovery", examSessionId },
    });
  }

  return bps;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  4. ADAPTIVE WORKLOAD BALANCING                                     */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Compute an optimal budget allocation for a study day.
 *
 * Balances three competing demands:
 * 1. FSRS flashcard reviews (time-sensitive, SRS-driven)
 * 2. Weak-topic remediation (performance-driven)
 * 3. Normal forward study (chapter reading, questions)
 *
 * @param dailyBudgetMinutes  Total minutes available for the day
 * @param reviewWorkload      Current FSRS review workload
 * @param remediationMinutes  Total minutes across all remediation blueprints
 */
export function computeBudgetAllocation(
  dailyBudgetMinutes: number,
  reviewWorkload: ReviewWorkload,
  remediationMinutes: number,
): DailyBudgetAllocation {
  const budget = dailyBudgetMinutes;

  // Buffer first (10%)
  const bufferMinutes = Math.round(budget * BUDGET.BUFFER_RATIO);
  const available = budget - bufferMinutes;

  // Flash card demand
  const flashcardDemand = reviewWorkload.estimatedMinutesToday;
  const flashcardCap = Math.round(available * BUDGET.MAX_FLASHCARD_RATIO);
  const flashcardMinutes = Math.min(flashcardDemand, flashcardCap);

  // Remediation demand
  const remediationCap = Math.round(available * BUDGET.MAX_REMEDIATION_RATIO);
  const remediationAlloc = Math.min(remediationMinutes, remediationCap);

  // Normal study gets the rest (at least MIN_NORMAL_RATIO)
  const minNormal = Math.round(available * BUDGET.MIN_NORMAL_RATIO);
  const normalStudyMinutes = Math.max(
    available - flashcardMinutes - remediationAlloc,
    minNormal,
  );

  // Rebalance if over budget
  const total = flashcardMinutes + remediationAlloc + normalStudyMinutes + bufferMinutes;
  if (total > budget) {
    // Shrink buffer and remediation proportionally
    const overage = total - budget;
    const shrinkRemediation = Math.min(
      overage,
      remediationAlloc - Math.round(remediationAlloc * 0.5),
    );
    return {
      totalMinutes: budget,
      flashcardMinutes,
      remediationMinutes: remediationAlloc - shrinkRemediation,
      normalStudyMinutes,
      bufferMinutes: Math.max(
        bufferMinutes - (overage - shrinkRemediation),
        0,
      ),
    };
  }

  return {
    totalMinutes: budget,
    flashcardMinutes,
    remediationMinutes: remediationAlloc,
    normalStudyMinutes,
    bufferMinutes,
  };
}

/**
 * Distribute remediation blueprints across multiple days, respecting daily budget.
 *
 * Returns an array of arrays — one inner array per day.
 */
export function distributeRemediationAcrossDays(
  blueprints: RemediationBlueprint[],
  dailyRemediationBudget: number,
  numDays: number,
): RemediationBlueprint[][] {
  const days: RemediationBlueprint[][] = Array.from(
    { length: numDays },
    () => [],
  );
  const dayMinutes = new Array(numDays).fill(0);

  // Sorted by priority descending
  const sorted = [...blueprints].sort((a, b) => b.priority - a.priority);

  for (const bp of sorted) {
    // Find the day with the least load that can fit this blueprint
    let bestDay = 0;
    let bestLoad = dayMinutes[0];

    for (let i = 1; i < numDays; i++) {
      if (dayMinutes[i] < bestLoad) {
        bestDay = i;
        bestLoad = dayMinutes[i];
      }
    }

    if (bestLoad + bp.estimatedMinutes <= dailyRemediationBudget) {
      days[bestDay].push(bp);
      dayMinutes[bestDay] += bp.estimatedMinutes;
    } else {
      // Try to find any day with space
      let placed = false;
      for (let i = 0; i < numDays; i++) {
        if (dayMinutes[i] + bp.estimatedMinutes <= dailyRemediationBudget) {
          days[i].push(bp);
          dayMinutes[i] += bp.estimatedMinutes;
          placed = true;
          break;
        }
      }
      // If no day fits, place in least-loaded day (overflow)
      if (!placed) {
        days[bestDay].push(bp);
        dayMinutes[bestDay] += bp.estimatedMinutes;
      }
    }
  }

  return days;
}

/**
 * Interleave remediation and normal blueprints for topic variety.
 *
 * Ensures the user doesn't do all remediation first then all normal study.
 * Uses a zipper pattern: R, N, N, R, N, N, R, ...
 */
export function interleaveTasks<T extends { priority: number; estimatedMinutes: number }>(
  remediationTasks: T[],
  normalTasks: T[],
): T[] {
  const result: T[] = [];
  let ri = 0;
  let ni = 0;

  // Put highest priority remediation first
  const sortedRemediation = [...remediationTasks].sort((a, b) => b.priority - a.priority);
  const sortedNormal = [...normalTasks].sort((a, b) => b.priority - a.priority);

  // Pattern: 1 remediation per 2 normal (adjustable)
  while (ri < sortedRemediation.length || ni < sortedNormal.length) {
    if (ri < sortedRemediation.length) {
      result.push(sortedRemediation[ri++]);
    }
    // 2 normal tasks
    for (let k = 0; k < 2 && ni < sortedNormal.length; k++) {
      result.push(sortedNormal[ni++]);
    }
  }

  return result;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  5. FSRS-AWARE FLASHCARD BLUEPRINTS                                 */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Generate flashcard review blueprints based on FSRS due counts per chapter.
 *
 * Replaces the static "50 cards per chapter" blueprint with actual SRS demand.
 */
export function generateFsrsFlashcardBlueprints(
  chapterIds: string[],
  maxMinutes: number,
): RemediationBlueprint[] {
  const dueSummary = getDueCardsByChapter();
  const blueprints: RemediationBlueprint[] = [];
  let usedMinutes = 0;

  // Filter to requested chapters, sort by due count descending
  const relevant = dueSummary
    .filter((d) => chapterIds.includes(d.chapterId))
    .sort((a, b) => b.dueCount - a.dueCount);

  for (const ch of relevant) {
    if (ch.dueCount === 0) continue;
    if (usedMinutes >= maxMinutes) break;

    const minutes = Math.min(ch.estimatedMinutes, maxMinutes - usedMinutes);
    const cardCount = Math.ceil(minutes / 2); // 2 min/card

    blueprints.push({
      taskType: "flashcard_review",
      title: `فلشکارت SRS: ${ch.chapterId}`,
      description: `مرور ${cardCount} فلشکارت موعد (${ch.overdueCount} عقب‌افتاده، ${ch.newCount} جدید)`,
      estimatedMinutes: minutes,
      priority: ch.overdueCount > 0 ? 1 : 0,
      targetCount: cardCount,
      links: [
        {
          chapterId: ch.chapterId,
          metadataJson: {
            orchestratorSource: "flashcard_due",
            dueCount: ch.dueCount,
            overdueCount: ch.overdueCount,
            newCount: ch.newCount,
          },
        },
      ],
      source: { type: "flashcard_due" },
    });

    usedMinutes += minutes;
  }

  return blueprints;
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  6. UNIFIED INTELLIGENCE                                            */
/* ================================================================== */

/**
 * Compute orchestrator intelligence for plan generation.
 *
 * This is the main entry point called by planner-service.
 * Combines weak-topic analysis, FSRS workload, remediation generation,
 * and budget allocation into a single payload.
 *
 * @param chapterIds        Chapters in the current plan
 * @param dailyBudgetMinutes  Daily study budget
 */
export function computeIntelligence(
  chapterIds: string[],
  dailyBudgetMinutes: number,
): OrchestratorIntelligence {
  // 1. Weak-topic detection
  const weakTopics = detectWeakTopics({ chapterIds });

  // 2. FSRS workload
  const reviewWorkload = estimateReviewWorkload();

  // 3. Generate remediation blueprints (from weak topics)
  const topicRemediation = generateRemediationBlueprints(weakTopics, {
    maxBlueprints: 10,
  });

  // 4. Generate FSRS flashcard blueprints
  const fsrsBlueprints = generateFsrsFlashcardBlueprints(
    chapterIds,
    Math.round(dailyBudgetMinutes * BUDGET.MAX_FLASHCARD_RATIO),
  );

  // 5. Merge all remediation
  const allRemediation = [...topicRemediation, ...fsrsBlueprints].sort(
    (a, b) => b.priority - a.priority,
  );

  // 6. Budget allocation
  const totalRemediationMinutes = allRemediation.reduce(
    (sum, bp) => sum + bp.estimatedMinutes,
    0,
  );
  const budgetAllocation = computeBudgetAllocation(
    dailyBudgetMinutes,
    reviewWorkload,
    totalRemediationMinutes,
  );

  return {
    weakTopics,
    reviewWorkload,
    remediationBlueprints: allRemediation,
    budgetAllocation,
    computedAt: Date.now(),
  };
}

/* ================================================================== */
/*  Internal Helpers                                                   */
/* ================================================================== */

/** Look up chapter IDs for a list of question IDs. */
function getChaptersForQuestions(
  questionIds: string[],
): Map<string, string[]> {
  if (questionIds.length === 0) return new Map();

  const batchSize = 500;
  const result = new Map<string, string[]>();

  for (let i = 0; i < questionIds.length; i += batchSize) {
    const batch = questionIds.slice(i, i + batchSize);
    const rows = db.all<{ id: string; chapter_id: string }>(sql`
      SELECT id, chapter_id
      FROM questions
      WHERE id IN (${sql.join(batch.map((qid) => sql`${qid}`), sql`, `)})
    `);

    for (const r of rows) {
      const list = result.get(r.chapter_id) ?? [];
      list.push(r.id);
      result.set(r.chapter_id, list);
    }
  }

  return result;
}

/** Get incorrect question IDs from a specific exam for a specific chapter. */
function getIncorrectQuestionIdsFromExam(
  examSessionId: string,
  chapterId: string,
): string[] {
  const rows = db.all<{ question_id: string }>(sql`
    SELECT esq.question_id
    FROM exam_session_questions esq
    JOIN questions q ON esq.question_id = q.id
    WHERE esq.exam_session_id = ${examSessionId}
      AND q.chapter_id = ${chapterId}
      AND esq.outcome = 'incorrect'
  `);
  return rows.map((r) => r.question_id);
}
